# language_name:        Dakota
# closest ISO 639-3:    dak
# ISO_15924:            Latn
# year_short:           1883
# year_long:            
# vernacular_title:     Dakota Wowapi Wakan
# english_title:        The Holy Bible in the Language of the Dakotas Translated out of the original tongues. By Thomas S. Williamson and Stephen R. Riggs (portions)

# notes:                
01001001	Otokahe ekta Wakantanka maĥpiya kin maka kin ahna kaga .
01001002	Unkan maka kin tanton šni , qa takudan ohnaka šni , qa otpaza ošbe kin akan wanke ca Wakantanka Taniya kin mini kin aman .
01001003	Unkan Wakantanka , Ojanjan kta , eya . Unkan ojanjan .
01001004	Unkan ojanjan wanke cin , he Wakantanka wašte e wanhdake ca , Wakantanka ojanjan kin otpaze cin kici yukinukan ehnaka .
01001005	Qa Wakantanka ojanjan kin , Anpetu eciya , otpaze cin iš , Hanyetu eciya . Unkan oĥtayetu , Qa ohanhanna he anpetu tokaheya kin hee .
01001006	Unkan , Okotonyan wanke kte , mini kin okitahedan , qa mini kin mini kin yukinukan kte , Wakantanka eya .
01001007	Unkan okotonyan kin Wakantanka kage ca , mini okotonyan kuyatanhan kin , qa mini okotonyan akantanhan kin kici yukinukan . Unkan ecetu .
01001008	Unkan okotonyan kin he Wakantanka , Maĥpiya eciya . Unkan oĥtayetu , qa ohanĥanna anpetu icinonpa kin hee
01001009	Unkan , Maĥpiya kin ihukuya mini wanke cin icunonpa kawitaya kte , ca taku puze cin taninyan wanke kte , Wakantanka eya . Unkan ecetu .
01001010	Unkan taku puze cin he Wakantanka , Maka eciye ca , mini kiwitaya kin he , Miniwanca eciya , qa he Wakantanka wašte e wanhdaka .
01001011	Hehan Wakantanka heya , Maka kin wato icaĥye kte , peji kin he su icaĥye kte , waskuyeca can kin he waskuyeca icaĥye kte , waskuyeca mahen su yuke kte , ocaje otoiyohi su kin icaĥye kta , maka akan , Wakantanka eya . Unkan ecetu .
01001012	Unkan maka kin wato aicaga , peji kin ocaje otoiyohi su aicage ca , can kin waskuyeca aicaga otoiyohi mahen su kin yukan ece . Unkan he wašte e Wakantanka wanhdaka .
01001013	Unkan oĥtayetu , qa ohanĥanna he anpetu iciyamni kin hee .
01001014	Unkan Wakantanka heya , Maĥpiya okotonyan kin ekta taku iyoyanpa yuke kte , on anpetu hanyetu kici yukinukanyan un kte ca heon woyaka unpi kte , makoncage , anpetu , omaka , henakiya .
01001015	Qa maĥpiya okotonyan kin ekta hena iyoyanpa un kte , maka kin iyoyam ye kte , eya . Unkan ecetu .
01001016	Wakantanka wiiyoyanpa nom tankinyanyan kaga , tuka uman iyotan tanka kin he anpetu en ounye kte ca unman iyotan tanka kin he anpetu en ounye kte ca uman aoptetu kin he hanyetu en ounye kte ; wicanhpi nakun .
01001017	Hena maĥpiya okotonyan kin ekta Wakantanka ehnaka , maka kin iyojanjan kta e hecon .
01001018	Anpetu hanyetu ko ohinninyan ounye wicakiya , qa ojanjan kin otpaze cin kici yukinukanyan ounye kiya . Unkan he wašte e Wakantanka wanhdaka .
01001019	Unkan oĥtayetu , qa ohanĥanna he anpetu icitopa kin hee .
01001020	Unkan Wakantanka heya , Mini kin taku niyake ota icaĥye kta , qa taku kinyan maka kin iwankam maĥpiya okotonyan kin ohna , okinyanpi kte .
01001021	Hecen Wakantanka hogan tankinyanyan oicaĥye , ca taku niyake , taku mini oicage cin ocaje hiyeye cin owasin , hena mini icaĥkiye ca , taku kinyan hupahu tonyan ocaje otoiyohi . Unkan he Wakantanka wašte e wanhdaka .
01001022	Hena Wakantanka yawašte qa hecen ewicakiya , Icagapi qa ihduotapo , qa miniwanca kin ojudan yakonpo , qa taku kinye cin maka akan ihdoutapi kte .
01001023	Unkan oĥtayetu , qa ohanĥanna he anpetu icizaptan kin hee .
01001024	Hehan Wakantanka heya , Maka kin taku niyake oicage cin iyecen icaĥye kte ; woteca , watutka , wamanica , henakiya ocaje otoiyohi , eya . Unkan ecetu .
01001025	Hecen wamanica ocaje otoiyohi , woteca ocaje otoiyohi , woteca ocaje otoiyohi , qa taku maka asdohan owasin ocaje otoiyohi , henakiya Wakantanka wicakage , ca he wašte e Wakantanka wanhdaka .
01001026	Hehan Wakantanka hecen eya , Unkiye iyeuncecapi qa ouncage unkitawapi kin en wicašta unkagapi kta , qa miniwanca ekta hogan oicage cin wicayuhe kte , maĥpiya ekta taku kinye cin nakun , qa woteca qa maka kin ocowasin , qa watutka taku maka akan sdohan ,
01001027	Wakantanka eyaya iye iyececa wicašta wan kaga , Wakantanka ouncage iyececa kaga ; wica winyan kici wicakaga .
01001028	Qa Wakantanka wicayawašte qa , Icagapi , qa ihduotapo , qa maka kin ojudan iciyapo , qa denakiya wicayuha yaunpi kta , miniwanca ekta hogan oicage , ca maĥpiya ekta taku kinye cin , qa taku niyake maka aškanškan oicage cin owasin , tawa wicaya po ; Wakantan
01001029	Unkan , Ito taku maka akan waicaĥya suton wojupi owasin cicupi , can waskuyeca suton oicage cin owasin , hena nakun ; hena woyute yayapi kta .
01001030	Tuka taku maka akan ni un kin , maĥpiya taku okinye cin , qa taku maka aškanškan kin , taku niya un kin owasin , hena peji wato owasin woyute wicawaqu , Wakantanka eya . Unkan ecetu .
01001031	Unkan Wakantanka taku kage cin owasin wanhdaka ; unkan iyotan wašte . Unkan oĥtayetu qa ohanĥanna he anpetu icišakpe kin hee .
01002001	Hecen maĥpiya kin maka kin iyahna , qa taku ohnaka hiyeye cin owasin tanyan yuštanpi .
01002002	Unkan anpetu icišakowin , Wakantanka toĥtani kage cin owasin ayuštan , qa anpetu icišakowin kin en toĥtani kage ciqon etanhan okihpa
01002003	Qa Wakantanka anpetu icišakowin kin he hdawašte qa hduwakan . Toĥtani Wakantanka kage cin owasin anpetu kin he en ayuštan , qa okiĥpa , heon etanhan .
01002004	Maĥpiya maka ko kagapi kin , Jehowa Wakantanka maka maĥpiya ko kage cin , anpetu kin he en , woicage oyakapi kin dee .
01002005	Can hiyeye cin owasin maka kin en he šni itokam , peji tinta oicage cin owasin uye šni itokam , Jehowa Wakantanka nahaĥin maka kin amagaju ye šni , qa wicašta maka kicanye kte cin wanica .
01002006	Qa maka kin etanhan po wankantkiya u , qa maka itohnake kin , owancaya acuya .
01002007	Hehan Jehowa Wakantanka , maka mdu kin etanhan , wicašta wan kage , ca poge oĥdoka ohna ipoh iyeya hecen wicašta nagi ni kin icaga .
01002008	Unkan Jehowa Wakantanka , Eden heciya wihinanpe cin ekta , wojupi wan kage ca wicašta kin he en ehnaka .
01002009	Qa Jehowa Wakantanka can kin owasin tona owanyag wašte , aicage cin , maka kin etanhan icaĥya , qa wojupi kin cokaya , can wiconi wan kage ca , can wan on taku wašte taku šica ko sdonyapi kin he nakun en icaĥya
01002010	Unkan can wojupi kin hpan ye kta e , watpa wan Eden etanhan uye ca hetanhan ointpa tom icaga .
01002011	Ointpa tokaheya kin Pišon eciyapi ; he ĥawila makoce kin owancaya ohomniya .
01002012	Heciya mazaskazi yuke , ca mazaskazi makoce kin he en iyeyapi kin he wašte . Heciya Bedola , qa iĥe wicašake iyececa .
01002013	Watpa inonpa Giĥon eciyapi ; he Kuš makoce kin ohna iyaya .
01002014	Qa watpa iyamni kin Hedeqel eciyapi ; he Ašur makoce kin wiyohiyanpata kiya kaduza . Qa watpa itopa kin Yuphrate hee .
01002015	Unkan Jehowa Wakantanka Adam icu , qa Eden wojupi kin he kicanye ca awanyake kta e , en ehnaka .
01002016	Qa Jehowa Wakantanka wicašta kin hecen eciya , Can wojupi kin owasin etanhan icakiš iciye šni yate kta .
01002017	Tuka can wan , taku wašte taku šica ko on sdonyapi kin de etanhan yata kte šni ; tohan hetanhan yate cinhan anpetu kin he en nite kta .
01002018	Hehan Jehowa Wakantanka , Wicašta kin de išnana un kin he šica , wanji iye iyececa wecage kta , eya .
01002019	Wanna Jehowa Wakantanka , maka kin etanhan tinta wamanica owasin wicakaga , maĥpiya etkiya taku kinye cin ko owasin , qa Adam en u wicakiya , token caš wicaton kte cin sdonye kta e heon . Unkan token Adam owasin caš wicaton , hecen taku ni un kin otoiyo
01002020	Hecen Adam woteca owasin caš wicakiton , maĥpiya ektakiya taku kinye cin ko owasin , tinta wamanica nakun owasin ; tuka Adam ookiye iye iyececa wanjidan iyeyapi šni .
01002021	Unkan Jehowa Wakantanka woištima tanka wan Adam ahinĥpaye ya , unkan ištima . Unkan Wakantanka cutuhu kin wanji yujon icu , qa conica kin ecen paohduta iyeya .
01002022	Qa Jehowa Wakantanka cutuhu kin , wicašta etanhan icu qon on winyan wan kage , ca wicašta kin en kai .
01002023	Unkan , Mihu kin etanhan de hu ye ca , miceĥpi kin etanhan ceĥpi ya . De wicašta kin etanhan icupi kin , heon de winoĥinca eciyapi kta , Adam eya .
01002024	He etanhan wicašta atkuku hunku kici awicayuštan , qa tawicu kin en ikoyag iciye kta , hecen ceĥpi wanjipidan kta .
01002025	He ehan Adam tawicu kici napin oge iciton šni yakonpi ; tuka ištecapi šni .
01003001	Wanna wamanica hiyeye cin owasin Jehowa Wakantanka wicakage cin , wamduškaška kin hecedan ksapa : qa wamduška kin winyan kin heciya , Can wojupi kin en can otoiyohi etanhan yatapi kte šni awicakehan Wakantanka eya he ?
01003002	Unkan winyan kin wamduška kin heciya , Can wojupi en can waskuyeca aicage cin hena untapi kta ce
01003003	Taku can wajidan wojupi cokaya he cin heceedan , Ihnuhan yatapi qa odutanpi kin , hecanonpi kinhan nitapi kta ce , Wakantanka eya ce .
01003004	Unkan wamduška kin winoĥinca kin hecen eciya , Nitapi kte šni tuka heya ce ;
01003005	Anpetu kin en he yatapi kinhan nišeya išta nimdezapi , qa Taku wakan iyenicecapi , taku wašte taku šica ko sdonyayapi kte cin he Wakantanka sdonya , he etanhan heya ce .
01003006	Unkan can kin waskuyeca woyute wašte , owanyag wašte , qa wicimdeza ksam wicaye kte cin he , winoĥinca wanyake cehan waskuyeca kin icu , qa yute ca hihnaku kin qu , qa iš eya yuta .
01003007	Unkan napin išta mdezapi , qa tancodan yakonpi kin hehan sdonkiciyapi , qa suken can ape heca kagegepi , qa on oge icitonpi .
01003008	Unkan anpetu kin cusni hehan Jehowa Wakantanka ho kin wojupi kin ohna mani kin he naĥonpi , qa Wakantanka itohnake kin etanhan wojupi can kin ehna naicihmanpi
01003009	Hehan Jehowa Wakantanka Adam kipan , qa heciya Tukten yaun he ?
01003010	Unkan , Adam ayupte ca , Niho kin nawaĥon qa kowakipe ca namiciĥbe , tancodan waun kin heon etanhan eya .
01003011	Unkan tancodan yaun , kin tuwe oniciyaka he ? Can wanjidan etanhan yute šni ciši qon , hetanhan yata he ? eya .
01003012	Unkan Adam heya , Winoĥinca mayaqu hee , qa mici un kin , iye can kin etanhan maqu , qa wata ce .
01003013	Unkan Jehowa Wakantanka winoĥinca kin heciya , Tokeca hecanon he ? Unkan , Wamduška kin mahnaye ca wata ce , winoĥinca kin eya
01003014	Unkan Jehowa Wakantanka wamduška kin hecen eciya , Niye decanon , qa heon woteca watutka ko owasin , niš nana niyašicapi . Itpi kin on maka kin asdohan yaun qa tohan yani kin hehanyan maka ece yate kta .
01003015	Qa detanhan niš winoĥinca kin kici toka kiciya yaunpi kta , qa winoĥinca cinhintku kin nicinca kici toka kiciya yaunpi kta . He pa kin nicuwa kta qa niš he siyete kin he yakuwa kta .
01003016	Hehan winoĥinca kin heciya , Iyonicišice ca ihdunišake cin nina mduota kta . Iyokišinya cinca yaton , qa nihihna cantiheyaye ca iye wowidag niye kta
01003017	Unkan wicašta kin heciya , Nitawin kin token eniciye cin anayagoptan , qa can wan etanhan yute šni ciši qon , etanhan yate cin heon niye on etanhan maka kin yašicapi . Taku aicage cin on ĥtayani qa hecen yate kta , tohan yani kin hehanyan .
01003018	Wapepeka toka hu ko icaĥ niciye kta , qa peji maka aicage cin yate kta .
01003019	Niite tenimni kin on aguyapi yahdute kta , maka inicu kte cin hehanyan . Maka kin etanhan inicagapi nakaeš , maka mdu kin henica qa maka kin ekta icicawin yahde kta .
01003020	Hehan Adam iye tawicu kin , Ewe eya caš kiton ; taku ni un kin owasin he ina yanpi kin heon etanhan .
01003021	Unkan Jehowa Wakantanka Adam tawicu kin kici wakihdaka okde wicakicage ca oge wicakicaton
01003022	Qa Jehowa Wakantanka he ya Wicašta kin wanna unkiye wanji he iyeuncecapi , taku wašte taku šica ko sdonya , heon ihnuhan nape yekiye ca wiconi can kin etanhan icu , qa yute ca owihanke wanin ni kte cin .
01003023	Heon Jehowa Wakantanka wicašta kin Eden wojupi kin etanhan iyog iyeya ; maka kin etanhan icage cin he kicanye kta ece .
01003024	Hecen wicašta kin tankan iyeya , qa can wiconi canku kin awanyake kta e , Eden wojupi wiyohiyanpa tanhan Kerubim maza sagye ideya škanškan un ko ewicaĥde .
01004001	Unkan Adam tawicu kin Ewe sdonya , unkan ihdušake ca Qain he ton , qa , Jehowa etanhan wicašte wan mduha ce , eya .
01004002	Qa ake ihdušake ca sunkaku Abel ton . Unkan Abel taĥinca wanuyanpi wihan wicakiya , qa Qain maka kin kicanyan .
01004003	Unkan omaka ihanke kin hehan Qain waskuyeca maka aicage cin hee Jehowa wakiyušna
01004004	Unkan Abel taĥinca wanuyanpi tawa tokaheya tonpi wan , ihdi koya wošna . Unkan Jehowa Abel taku wakiyušna kin ko , akicitonwan .
01004005	Tuka Qain taku wakiyušna ko akicikta šni . Unkan Qain canteptanye ca itohnake tokeca .
01004006	Unkan Jehowa Qain heciya , Tokeca canniniye ca itohnake enicetu šni ?
01004007	Tanyan ecanon kinhan ihaniktapi kte šni he ? Tuka tanyan ecanon šni kinhan woaĥtani tiyopa kin en yanka . Tuka niye qe cantiheniye kta qa niš wowidake yaye kta .
01004008	Unkan Qain sunkaku Abel okiya , qa wojupi ekta napin yakonpi qehan najin hiyaye ca sunkaku Abel kikte .
01004009	Unkan Jehowa Qain heciya , Nisunka Able tukte e he ? Unkan , Sdonwaye šni . Ecin misunka kin he awanhdag waun he eya .
01004010	Unkan token yaĥan he ? Nisunka we kin maka kin etanhan ho umakiya .
01004011	Qa wanna maka kin nisunka we kin ninape etanhan icu kta e i kin hdukawa kin he etanhan niyašicapi ce .
01004012	Detanhan maka kin yakicanyan ešta , taku ota icaĥ niciye kte šni . Maka kin de akan onuniyan qa najica yaun kta ce , eya .
01004013	Unkan Qain Jehowa heciya , Wawaĥtani kin he tanka kin kajujupicašni .
01004014	Anpetu kin dehan maka kin detanhan iyog iyemayaya , qa nitoye kin inaĥbe wakiye kta , maka kin akan onuniyan qa najica waun kta , qa tuwe kašta iyemaye cinhan makte kta .
01004015	Tuka Jehowa heciya , Tuwe Qain kte kinhan , šakowin akihde wošice akipe kta . Qa Jehowa Qain wapetog ton , hecen on tuwe wanyaka ešta ktepi kte šni .
01004016	Unkan Qain Jehowa itoye kin etanhan inapa , Eden wiyohiyanpa tanhan makoce wan , Nod eciyapi kin , he en ounyan .
01004017	Qa Qain tawicu kin sdonya , unkan ihdušake ca Henok ton . Unkan Qain otonwe wan kage ca Henok eya caš kiton , cinhintku caje kin iyecen .
01004018	Unkan Henok cinca wan kicitonpi , Irad hee . Unkan Irad Mecujael cinkšiya . Unkan Mecujael Metušael Lamek cinkšiya .
01004019	Unkan Lamek winoĥinca nom wicayuza Tokaheya kin Ada eciyapi , qa iyokihe Zila eciyapi .
01004020	Unkan Ada Jabel ton he tona wakeya otipi , qa wanuyanpi awanhdakapi kin , hena ateyapi
01004021	Qa sunkaku Jubal eciyapi . Tona candowankiyapi cotanka ko , yahotaninpi kin , hena he ateyapi
01004022	Unkan Zila he Tubal Qain ton . Taku maza zi on kagapi , qa maza sapa on kagapi ko owasin iye onspe qa kaga . Qa Tubal Qain tawinoĥtin Nahama hee .
01004023	Unkan Lamek tawicu Ada Zila kici hewicakiya , Miho kin nahonpo , Lamek tawicu kin mioie kin anagoptanpo . Wicašta wan wakte , on camapapi , qa koška wan on kiunimiciya ce .
01004024	Qain šakowin akihde tokiconpi kinhan , Lamek wikcemna šakowin sanpa šakowin tokiconpi kta ce , eya .
01004025	Unkan ake Adam tawicu kin sdonya ; unkan cinca wan ton , qa , Wakantanka cinca tokeca wan maqu , Abel Qain kta qon hee kiya , eye ca Set eya caš kiton .
01004026	Unkan Set iš eya cinca wan kicitonpi , qa Enoš eya caš kiton . Hehan tokaheya wicašta kin Jehowa caje kin hoyekiyapi
01005001	Adam wicowazi wowapi kin dee Wakantanka Adam kage cehan , taku wakan ouncage iyecen icaĥ kiya .
01005002	Wica winyan ko wicakage ca wicayawašte , qa wicakage cehan Adam eya caš wicaton .
01005003	Unkan Adam waniyetu opawinge sanpa wikcemna yamni ni , qa cinca wan iye ouncage iyecen kicitonpi , qa Set eya caš kiton .
01005004	Qa Set tonpi kin he iyohakam , Adam waniyetu opawinge šahdogan ni , qa cinca wica winyan ko kicitonpi .
01005005	Hecen anpetu owasin Adam ni un kin hena waniyetu opawinge napciwanka sanpa wikcemna yamni , hehan ta .
01005006	Unkan Set waniyetu opawinge sanpa zaptan ni , qa Enoš
01005007	Qa Set Enoš tonpi kin iyohakam waniyetu opawinge šahdogan sanpa šakowin ni , qa cinca wica wiyan ko kicitonpi .
01005008	Hecen anpetu owasin Set ni un kin hena waniyetu opawinge napciwanka sanpa ake nonpa , hehan ta .
01005009	Unkan Enoš waniyetu wikcemna napciwanka ni , qa Qenan kicitonpi .
01005010	Qa Qenan tonpi kin iyohakam Enoš waniyetu opawinge šahdogan sanpa wikcemna sanpa zaptan ni , qa cinca wica winyan ko kicitonpi .
01005011	Hecen anpetu owasin Enoš ni un kin hena waniyetu opawinge napciwanka sanpa zaptan , qa hehan ta .
01005012	Unkan Qenan waniyetu wikcemna šakowin ni , qa Mahalele kicitonpi .
01005013	Qa Qenan Mahalele tonpi kin iyohakam waniyetu opawinge šahdogan sanpa wikcemna topa ni , qa cinca wica winyan ko kicitonpi .
01005014	Hecen anpetu owasin Qenan ni un kin hena waniyetu opawinge napciwanka sanpa wikcemna , hehan ta .
01005015	Unkan Mahalele waniyetu wikcemna šakpe sanpa zaptan ni , qa Jered kicitonpi .
01005016	Qa Mahalele Jered tonpi kin iyohakam waniyetu opawinge šahdogan sanpa wikcemna yamni ni , qa cinca wica winyan ko kicitonpi .
01005017	Hecen anpetu owasin Mahalele ni un kin hena waniyetu opawinge šahdogan sanpa wikcemna napciwanka sanpa zaptan , hehan ta .
01005018	Unkan Jered waniyetu opawinge sanpa wikcemna šakpe sanpa nonpa ni , qa Henok kicitonpi
01005019	Qa Jered Henok tonpi kin iyohakam waniyetu opawinge šahdogan ni , qa cinca wica winyan ko kicitonpi .
01005020	Hecen anpetu owasin Jered ni un kin hena waniyetu opawinge napciwanka sanpa wikcemna šakpe sanpa nonpa , hehan ta .
01005021	Unkan Henok waniyetu wikcemna šakpe sanpa zaptan ni , qa Metušela kicitonpi .
01005022	Qa Henok Metušela tonpi kin iyohakam waniyetu opawinge yamni Wakantanka opeya mani , qa cinca wica winyan ko kicitonpi .
01005023	Hecen Henok anpetu tawa owasin waniyetu opawinge yamni sanpa wikcemna šakpe sanpa zaptan .
01005024	Qa Henok Wakantanka opeya mani , qa en un šni , Wakantanka he ikikcu nakaeš .
01005025	Unkan Metušela waniyetu opawinge sanpa wikcemna šakowin sanpa šahdogan ni , qa Lemek kicitonpi .
01005026	Qa Lamek tonpi kin iyohakam Metušela waniyetu opawinge šakowin sanpa wikcemna šahdogan sanpa nonpa ni , qa cinca wica winyan ko kicitonpi .
01005027	Hecen anpetu owasin Metušela ni un kin hena waniyetu opawinge napciwanka sanpa wikcemna šakpe sanpa napciwanka , hehan ta .
01005028	Unkan Lemek waniyetu opawinge sanpa wikcemna šahdogan sanpa nonpa ni , qa cinca wan kicitonpi .
01005029	Qa , Jehowa maka kin yašice cin he nape on unkicanyanpi qa ĥtaunnipi kin en unkikiyapi kta cin dee ce , eye ca Nowa eya caš kiton .
01005030	Qa Lamek Nowa tonpi kin iyohakam waniyetu opawinge Zaptan sanpa wikcemna šakowin sanpa zaptan ni , qa cinca wica winyan ko kicitonpi .
01005031	Hecen anpetu owasin Lemek ni un kin hena waniyetu opawinge šakowin sanpa wikcemna šakowin sanpa šakowin , hehan ta .
01005032	Unkan Nowa wanna waniyetu opawinge zaptan , hehan šem , ĥam , qa Japet , kicitonpi .
01006001	Hehan wicašta maka akan ota ayapi , qa cunwintkupi kicitonpi .
01006002	Unkan Wakantanka cinkši wicaye cin wicašta cunwintkupi kin hena e wašte wanwicayakapi , qa tona cinpi kin hena etanhan , winoĥinca wicayuzapi .
01006003	Unkan Jehowa heya , Wicašta kin wicaceĥpi kin heca heon waĥtanipi kin en mitaniya he kici owihanke wanin ounye kte šni , tuka anpetu tawa kin hena waniyetu opawinge sanpa wikcemna nonpa kta .
01006004	Unkan anpetu kin hena icunhan , maka kin akan wazise yakonpi , qa Wakantanka cinkši wicaye cin wicašta cunwintkupi kin wicayuzapi , qa cinca kicitonpi kin , hena eepi he iyohakam wicašta wašakapi , wanakaja tanhan wicašta nina caje wicayatapi .
01006005	Unkan wicašta maka akan waĥtanipi kin ota e , Jehowa wanyaka , anpetu osan wicocante oze okaĥ otoiyohi ecedan šica .
01006006	Unkan wicašta maka akan icaĥ wicaye cin heon Jehowa iyopeiciye ca cante iyokišin iciya .
01006007	Qa , Wicašta icaĥ wicawaye cin , maka itohnake kin etanhan wicawakahinte kta ; wicašta , qa woteca , qa watutka , qa taku maĥpiya ektakiya kinyan un kin henakiya icaĥ wicawaye cin heon iyopemiciya ce , Jehowa eya .
01006008	Tuka Jehowa Nowa wanyake ca wacin en yuza .
01006009	Nowa wicoicage oyakapi kin dee . Nowa wicašta oĥan owotanna , qa hecetu wicoicage tawa kin hen , qa Nowa Wakantanka opeya mani .
01006010	Qa Nowa cinca yamni kicitonpi , šem , ĥam , qa Japet .
01006011	Unkan Wakantanka itokam maka kin ĥonwin ce , qa maka owancaya nina waboticapi .
01006012	Unkan Wakantanka maka kin , wanyaka , unkan ĥonwin ; wicaceĥpi owasin maka akan iye tacankupi kin ĥonwin kiyapi ce .
01006013	Unkan Wakantanka Nowa heciya , Taku ceĥpi yukan owasin owihanke kin mitokam u ce ; iyepi kin on maka kin waboticapi on ojudan ; qa maka kin etanhan ihang wicawaye kta .
01006014	Wazi can on wata wan icicaga wo . Mahentu kin oškiškeya yakage kta , qa mahen tanhan akapa tanhan ko canšin apawinta wo .
01006015	Qa hecen yakage kta Wata ohanske cin wicišpa opawinge yamni , ohdakinyan kin wicišpa wikcemna zaptan , qa obusdatu kin wicišpa wikcemna yamni kta .
01006016	Qa wata kin en ojanjan hdepi yakage kta , qa wankantuya wicišpa wanjidan en yahduštan kta . Wata tiyopa kin cuwi kin , ekta yakage kta , owanka tokaheya , inonpa , qa iyamni yakage kta .
01006017	Wanna miye maka akan minitan waye kta , heon taku ceĥpi yuke cin niyake iyeye cin owasin maĥpiya ihukuya , ihang waye kta . Taku maka akan un kin owasin te kta .
01006018	Tuka wicotakuye mitawa kin niye en nici wahdusuta kta , wata kin en oyape kta nicinca om , nitawin , nicinca tawicupi kin , henana om .
01006019	Qa taku niya un kin owasin tuka ceĥpi yukan hiyeye cin ocaje otoiyohi , nom nom mdoka wiye iyahnahna , en owicayahnake kta ; ni wicayaye kta e niye kici wata kin en upi kta .
01006020	Taku kinye cin token ocaje , woteca token ocaje , wamanica maka akan unpi kin token ocaje , owasin ocaje otoiyohi nom nom niyake wicaduhe kta e niye en upi kta .
01006021	Qa niye taku yutapi kin ocaje otoiyohi etanhan icu , qa mnayan wo ; hecen taku yutapi anihduhe , ca woteca kin iš iyacinyan wicayakihduhe kta .
01006022	Unkan Nowa Wakantanka token eciye cin , owasin anagoptan , qa econ .
01007001	Unkan Jehowa Nowa heciya , Niye , tiyohnaka nitawa kin owasin om , wata kin en opa wo ; wicoicage kin de en mitokam owotanna yaun kin wanciyaka ce .
01007002	Woteca wakašotešni ocaje otoiyohi mdoka wiye ahnahna šakowinwin iyacu kta , qa woteca waašapapi kin , hena nom nom mdoka wiye kici iyacu kta .
01007003	Taku maĥpiya ektakiya kinye cin nakun šakowinwin , mdoka wiye ahnahna maka akan aicagapi e niyake wicaduhe kta .
01007004	Ehake anpetu šakowin , hehan maka kin amagaju waye kta , qa taku ni un wakage cin owasin maka kin owancaya etanhan wakahinte kta ce .
01007005	Unkan Nowa , Jehowa token eciye cin owasin ecen econ .
01007006	Nowa tonpi kin ehantanhan waniyetu opawinge šakpe hehan maka kin akan minitan .
01007007	Qa Nowa cinkši wicaye om , qa iye tawicu , cinkši wicaye cin tawicupi ko , hena owasin om minitan mini kin itokapa tanhan wata kin en opa .
01007008	Woteca wakašotešni , qa woteca waašapapi kin , taku kinye cin , taku maka asdohan unpi ko owasin ,
01007009	Nom nom mdoka wiye ahnahna Nowa en hipi , wata kin en ; Wakantanka Nowa econ ši qon he iyecen .
01007010	Unkan anpetu šakowin hehan maka kin akan minitan aya .
01007011	Waniyetu opawinge šakpe hehanyan Nowa ni un kin , wicinonpa , anpetu iake šakowin kin , hehan šbe tanka kin wakoniya hiyeye cin owasin yuomdecapi , qa maĥpiya owanyeye hdepi kin owasin yuzamni ehdepi .
01007012	Qa anpetu wikcemna tom , hanyetu wikcemna tom , hehanyan maka kin ahinheya .
01007013	Anpetu kin he en Nowa , qa šem , qa ĥam , qa Japet , Nowa cinkšiwicaye cin , Nowa tawicu kin nakun , cinca tawicupi yamni om , wata kin en hiyupi ;
01007014	Hena qa wamanica ocaje owasin , woteca ocaje owasin , watutka tona maka asdohan unpi ocaje owasin , taku kinyan ocaje owasin , zitkadan owasin taku šun yukan owasin ,
01007015	Nom nom hipi , Nowa ekta wata kin en , taku ceĥpi yuke cin woniya niyake yuke cin owasin ,
01007016	Hena en hiyupi ; mdoka wiye ahnahna taku ceĥpi yuke cin owasin etanhan upi ; Wakantanka econ qon he iyecetu . Unkan Jehowa tiyopa kin onataka .
01007017	Unkan anpetu wikcemna tom maka kin ahinheye ca , minitan tanka aya ; unkan wata kin okapon maka kin iwankam iyaya .
01007018	Unkan mini kin wašagya aye ca maka kin akan nina ihduota , unkan wata kin mini kin aokapota .
01007019	Unkan mini kin nina hin wašagya , maka kin akan , heon he pajodan owasin , tona maĥpiya ihukuya un kin hena aminitan .
01007020	Wicišpa ake zaptan iwankam mini kin aye , ca paha kin aminitan .
01007021	Unkan taku ceĥpi yuke cin owasin , taku maka akanškan un kin , taku kinyan qa woteca , wamanica , qa watutka tona maka kin akan sdohanpi kin owasin tapi , wicašta iyuĥpa nakun tapi .
01007022	Taku maka puze cin akan ni , taku poge on niya un kin , owasin tapi .
01007023	Unkan taku hiyeye cin maka akan un kin owasin kahintapi , wicašta , woteca , watutka , maĥpiya zitkadan , owasin maka kin etanhan wicakahinta , qa Nowa išnana qa tona wata kin ohna om un kin henana okaptapi .
01007024	Anpetu opawinge sanpa wikcemna zaptan mini kin maka kin akan agya .
01008001	Hehan Wakantanka Nowa kiksuye , ca wamanica woteca ko owasin , iye kici wata ohna yakonpi kin hena ; qa Wakantanka tate wan maka kin akan iyayupte ya , qa mini kin ayuštan .
01008002	Qa miniĥdoka owahinapeye cin onatakapi , maĥpiya owanyeye kin hena koya , qa magaju maĥpiya etanhan kin he ayuštan .
01008003	Unkan mini kin maka kin etanhan kihda , anpetu opawinge sanpa wikcemna zaptan , hehan mini kin oyaĥe aya .
01008004	Wi išakowin , anpetu iake šakowin wi kin en , hehan wata kin Ararat he kin en azi .
01008005	Unkan mini kin iyoopta ye ca oyaĥe aya , wi iwikcemna kin hehanyan ; wi iwikcemna kin anpetu tokaheya kin he an , he paha kin taninyan hiyeya .
01008006	Unkan anpetu wikcemna tom henakeca , hehan Nowa wata kin owanyeye kage ciqon , he yuĥdoka .
01008007	Qa kangi wan tankan iyaye ya , unkan iyaye ca ohnihdeya un , mini kin maka kin etanhan oyaĥe kin hehanyan .
01008008	Mini kin maka itohnake kin etanhan wanna pus aya , wanyake kta e wakiyedan wan nakun tankan iyaye ya .
01008009	Tuka wakiyedan kin tukten sicuha iyahe kte cin iyeye šni , mini kin maka kin owancaya akan un nakaeš ; qa Nowa en wata kin ekta hdi ; unkan nape kin kiyugate ca wata kin en ikikcu .
01008010	Qa ake anpetu šakowin ape , qa hehan ake wakiyedan wan wata kin etanhan iyaye ya .
01008011	Unkan iĥtayetu he ehan wakiyedan kin hdi , qa wihdi can ape wan yapa hdi ; unkan Nowa mini kin maka kin etanhan wanna pus aye cin sdonya .
01008012	Unkan ake anpetu šakowin tokeca ape , qa hehan wakiyedan wan tankan iyaye ya , unkan icimana hdi šni .
01008013	Unkan Nowa tonpi kin ehantanhan waniyetu opawinge šakpe qa itokaheya kin , wi tokaheya , qa anpetu tokaheya , hehan mini kin maka kin akapatanhan puza , unkan Nowa wata kin akaĥpe ciqon yuhdoke ca , maka itohnake kin wanna puza wanyake .
01008014	Wi inonpa kin , anpetu iake šakowin kin , hehan maka kin puza .
01008015	Unkan Wakantanka Nowa okiye ca ,
01008016	Wata kin etanhan ya wo , niye , qa nitawin , qa nicinca , qa nicinca tawicupi kin niye kici ;
01008017	Taku niyake niye kici un kin ko owasin , taku ceĥpi yukan owasin , taku kinyan , woteca , watutka tona maka asdohan unpi kin owasin , tankan awicayaku kte , hecen maka akan cinca kagapi kte ca icagapi , qa ichduotapi kta ce , eciya .
01008018	Unkan Nowa tankan iyaye ca , cinca nakun , tawicu , cinca tawicupi koya .
01008019	Taku niyake owasin , wamanica owasin , qa taku kinyan owasin , taku maka akan sdohan un kin owasin , ocaje otoiyohi wata kin etanhan inanpapi .
01008020	Unkan Nowa wahna wošnapi wan Jehowa kicaga qa , woteca wakašotešni otoiyohi etanhan , qa taku kinyan wakašotešni ocaje otoiyohi etanhan icu , qa wawicayušna , qa huhnah wicaya , wahna wošnapi kin akan .
01008021	Unkan Jehowa waštemna kin omna , qa Jehowa cante kin ekta heya , Wicašta kin heon maka kin ake mdašice kte šni ; ehaeš wicašta kin hokšiyoqopa kin ehantanhan cante oze šica ece , tuka icimana taku niya un kin owasin ihang waye kte šni , hecamon qon iyec
01008022	Tohanyan maka kin wanke cin hehanyan wojupi qa coyapi , qa šni qa didita , qa mdoketu qa waniyetu , qa anpetu qa hanyetu hena ayuštanpi kte šni ce .
01009001	Unkan Wakantanka Nowa , cinca wicaye cin ko , wicayawašte qa , Icagapi qa ihduotapi , qa maka kin owancaya ojudan yapo ;
01009002	Qa taku maka aškanškan taku maĥpiya okinye cin ko owasin , maka watutka owasin , qa mini owanca hogan owasin , ikonipapi qa ikonipapi kta , hena owasin ninape kin en nicupi ce .
01009003	Taku niya , qa škanškan kin owasin woyute nitawapi kta ; peji wato iyecen hena owasin cicupi .
01009004	Tuka we , ceĥpi wiconi kin hee , yatapi kte šni .
01009005	Qa awicakehan we nitawapi kin on yanipi kin awakite kta , wamanica otoiyohi nape kin etanhan awakite kta , wicašta nape kin ko etanhan , otoiyohi hunka wanjiktu nape kin etanhan wicašta wiconi kin he awakite kta .
01009006	Wakantanka iye ouncage iyecen wicašta kin kaga ; heon tuwe wicašta weye cinhan , he wicašta eciyatanhan weyapi kta .
01009007	Qa niyepi icagapi , qa maka kin owancaya ounyanpi , qa he ohna ihduotapo , ewicakiya .
01009008	Qa Wakantanka Nowa , cinca wicaye cin ko , owicakiye ca ;
01009009	Iho miye wicotakuye mitawa ciciyasuta qa nicinca nihektam unpi kte cin om .
01009010	Nakun taku niya un kin , niyepi om unpi kin , taku kinyan , woteca , qa maka wamanica owasin , tona niye om wata kin etanhan inanpapi kin , taku maka akan ni un kin owasin om .
01009011	Niyepi om wicotakuye mitawa wakaga , qa taku ceĥpi yukan owasin minitan mini on icimana awihnuni waye kte šni , qa detanhan maka ihang ye kta on , icimana minitan kte šni , ewicakiya .
01009012	Qa , Wicoicage owasin , hehanyan niyepi en , qa taku ni un kin owasin en , wicotakuye wakage cin wowakta kin dee .
01009013	Mitinazipe kin maĥpiya šoka en ewehnake ca he wicotakuye make kin waqu kin , wowakta kin hee kta .
01009014	Qa tohan maka kin maĥpiya šoka wan ahanzi waye cinhan , maĥpiya šoka kin ekta mitinazipe kin tanin kta .
01009015	Qa wicotakuye mitawa weksuye kta , niyepi om , qa taku ni un kin owasin om , qa taku ceĥpi yuke cin owasin awihnuni kta e , detanhan icimana minitan kte šni .
01009016	Itazipa kin maĥpiya šoke cin en yanke kta , qa wicotakuye Wakantanka kici , qa taku maka akan niya un kin taku ceĥpi yuke cin owasin om , owihanke šniyan un kte cin , he weksuye kta e itazipa kin wanwahdake kta ce , Wakantanka eya :
01009017	Qa , Taku ceĥpi yuke cin maka akan owasin , wicotakuye wicawaqu kin wowakta kin hee kta , Wakantanka Nowa eciya .
01009018	Unkan Nowa cinca wicaye cin , wata qon etanhan inanpapi kin deepi , šem , qa ĥam , qa Japet . Unkan ĥam Kanan atkuku kin hee
01009019	Hena yamni Nowa cinca kin eepi , qa hena etanhan maka kin owancaya enanakiya iyayapi .
01009020	Unkan , Nowa maka kin kicanyan aye ca hastanhanka iyuwi hu hde .
01009021	Qa hetanhan miniša yatke ca witko , qa wakeya ohna tancodan un .
01009022	Unkan ĥam Kanan atkuku kin hee , atkuku tancodan un kin he wanhdake ca cincu nom tankan yakonpi kin , owicakiyaka .
01009023	Unkan šem Japet kici , šina wan icupi , qa napin hiyetepi kin akan ehnakapi , qa iĥeyata manipi , qa ateyapi tancodan un kin akaĥpapi ; itepi kin iĥeyata unpi , hecen ateyapi tancodan un kin wanhdakapi šni .
01009024	Unkan Nowa , Miniša kin etahan kikta , qa cinhintku hakakta kin taku ecakicon qon sdotkiya ;
01009025	Qa heya , Kanan yašicapi kta . Wowidake wowidag yapi kta , cinye wicaye cin he yuhapi kta .
01009026	Jehowa šem taku wakan tawa kin yawaštepi nunwe . Kanan wowidake yuhapi kta .
01009027	Wakantanka Japet yuota kta , qa šem tawakeya kin ohna Japet ounye kta , qa Kanan wowidake yuhapi kta .
01009028	Unkan Nowa , minitan qon iyohakam , waniyetu opawinge yamni sanpa wikcemna zaptan ni .
01009029	Hecen Nowa anpetu tawa owasin , waniyetu opawinge napciwanka sanpa wikcemna zaptan hehan ta .

01010004	Unkan Jawan cinca kin , Eliša , qa Taršiš , Kitim , qa Dodanim .

01010007	Unkan Kuš cinca kin , šeba , qa Cawila , qa Sabta , qa Rahama , qa Sabteca . Unkan Rahama cinca kin šeba , qa Dedan .
01010008	Unkan Kuš Nimrod kicitonpi , he tokaheya maka akan wašaka aya .

01010012	Qa Niniwe Kala kici otahedan Resen otonwe tanka wan hee .

01010014	Qa Partusim , qa Kasluhim , hetanhan Pilištim , qa Kaptorim inanpapi .

01010016	Qa Jebusi kin , qa Amori kin , qa Girgiši kin ,
01010017	Qa ĥiwi kin , qa Hareqi kin , qa Sini kin ,

01010021	Unkan Japet tokapa kin sunkaku šem , he cinca kicitonpi , Heber cinca wicaye cin owasin ateyapi kin hee .

01010024	Unkan Arpakšad šela kicitonpi , qa šela Heber kicitonpi .

01010026	Joktan cinca wicaye cin Almodad , qa šelep , qa ĥatsarmawet , qa Jera ;
01010027	Qa Hadoram , qa Uzal , qa Diqela ;
