01010029	Qa Opir , qa ĥawila , qa Jobal , hena owasin Joktan cinkši wicaya .
01010030	Meša etanhan de cin , Seper ĥe wan wiyohiyanpata wanke cin hehanyan ounyanpi .
01010031	šem cinca wicaye cin hena eepi ; wicowazipi , qa wicoie hduhapi kin iyecen oyatepi kin tamakocepi kin en ounyanpi .
01010032	Nowa cinca wicaye cin wicowazipi kin heepi , oyatepi kin owancaya oyate enanakiya iyayapi minitan qon iyohakam .
01011001	Hehan maka kin owancaya wicaiha wanjidan , qa iapi ko wanjidan .
01011002	Qa wiyohiyanpata ihdaka unpi , qa šinar makoce kin he en , omdaye wan iyeyapi . qa en eyakonpi .
01011003	Qa otoiyohi takodaku hekiciyapi , Ihopo , maka omdoton unkagapi , qa špan unkiyapi kta ce , eyapi . Hecen inyan hee kiya maka omdoton kin he icupi , qa upšija hee kiya bitumen icupi .
01011004	Qa ake hekiciyapi , Ihopo , otonwe wanji unkagapi kte ca nakun conkaške wan , he ointpa kin maĥpiya iyahdeye kta , qa caje unkicagapi kte ; heconkupi šni kinhan , maka kin owancaya omdecaheya unkiyayapi kta .
01011005	Unkan , Jehowa otonwe kin , inatake ko , Adam cinca wicaye cin kagapi kin wanyake kta e kun hiyu .
01011006	Qa , Ehaeš oyate wanjidan , qa owasin iapi wanjidan yuhapi , qa de tokaheya econpi , qa detanhan taku kaga kecinpi owasin takudan teĥike dapi kte šni .
01011007	Iho , kun unyanpi kta ; kinhan iyakitedan iapi nakicihonpi kte šni , Jehowa eya .
01011008	Qa hetanhan Jehowa , maka kin owancaya , yuomden ye wicaya ; unkan otonwe kagapi qon ayuštanpi .
01011009	He etanhan caje kin Babel eciyapi ; heciya Jehowa maka kin owasin iapi kin yuicicaĥi , qa hetanhan maka kin owancaya yuomden enanakiya ye wicaya .
01011010	šem wicowazi wowapi kin dee . šem waniyetu opawinge sanpa nonpa ni , qa hehan Arpakšad kicitonpi , minitan qon iyohakam waniyetu nonpa .
01011011	šem Arpakšad tonpi kin iyohakam , waniyetu opawinge zaptan ni , qa cinca wica winyan ko kicitonpi .
01011012	Unkan Arpakšad waniyetu wikcemna yamni sanpa zaptan ni , qa šela kicitonpi .
01011013	Qa Arpakšad , šela tonpi kin iyohakam , waniyetu opawinge tom sanpa yamni ni , qa cinca wica winyan ko kicitonpi .
01011014	Unkan šela waniyetu wikcemna yamni ni , qa hehan Heber kicitonpi .
01011015	Qa šela Heber tonpi kin iyohakam , waniyetu opawinge tom sanpa yamni ni , qa cinca wica winyan ko kicitonpi .
01011016	Unkan Heber waniyetu wikcemna yamni sanpa topa ni , qa Peleg kicitonpi .
01011017	Qa Peleg tonpi kin iyohakam , Heber waniyetu opawinge tom sanpa wikcemna yamni ni , qa cinca wica winyan ko kicitonpi .
01011018	Unkan Peleg waniyetu wikcemna yamni ni , qa Reyu kicitonpi .
01011019	Qa Peleg , Reyu tonpi kin iyohakam , waniyetu opawinge nonpa sanpa napciwanka ni , qa cinca wica winyan ko kicitonpi .
01011020	Unkan Reyu waniyetu wikcemna yamni sanpa nonpa ni , qa Serug kicitonpi .
01011021	Qa Serug tonpi kin iyohakam , Reyu waniyetu opawinge nonpa sanpa šakowin ni , qa cinca wica winyan ko kicitonpi .
01011022	Unkan Serug waniyetu wikcemna yamni ni , qa Naĥor kicitonpi .
01011023	Qa Naĥor tonpi kin iyohakam , Serug waniyetu opawinge nonpa ni , qa cinca wica winyan ko kicitonpi .
01011024	Unkan Naĥor waniyetu wikcemna nonpa sanpa napciwanka ni , qa Tera kicitonpi .
01011025	Qa Naĥor Tera tonpi kin iyohakam , waniyetu opawinge sanpa wikcemna sanpa napciwanka ni , qa cinca wica winyan ko kicitonpi .
01011026	Unkan Tera waniyetu wikcemna šakowin ni , qa Aberam , qa Naĥor , qa Haran kicitonpi .
01011027	Tera wicowazi wowapi kin dee . Tera iye Aberam , Naĥor , qa Haran kicitonpi . Unkan Haran Lot kicitonpi .
01011028	Unkan Haran , iye atkuku , Tera itokam ta , Ur Kašdim heciya , makoce en tonpi kin he en ta .
01011029	Unkan Aberam , qa Naĥor winoĥinca yuzapi . Aberam tawicu caje kin Sari , qa Naĥor tawicu caje kin Milka eciyapi . Haran he cunwintku iye Milka Iska ko ateyapi .
01011030	Tuka Sari cinca ton šni un , cinca wanica .
01011031	Unkan Tera iye cinhintku Aberam ikikcu , qa takojatpaku , Lot he Haran cinhintku , qa takošku Sari iye cinhintku Aberam tawicu kin hee . Hena om Ur Kašdim etanhan iyaya Kanan makoce kin ekta ye kte , ca Haran ehan hipi qa hen hiyakonpi .
01011032	Qa Tera anpetu tawa kin waniyetu opawinge nonpa sanpa zaptan henakeca , qa Haran hen Tera ta .
01012001	Unkan Jehowa Aberam heciya , Nita makoce kin etanhan ya wo , nitakuye etanhan , qa niyate ti kin etanhan , makoce wan wanyag ciciye kte cin he ekta ya wo .
01012002	Kinhan oyate tanka icaĥ ciye , ca ciyawašte , qa nicaje kin tanka wakage kta ; qa wowašte yaun kta ;
01012003	Qa tona niyawaštepi kin hena wicamdawašte , qa tuwe niyašice cin he mdašice kta , qa niye en wicowazi tona maka akan unpi kin owasin yawaštepi kta ce .
01012004	Unkan Aberam iyaya , Jehowa eciye ciqon he iyecen , qa Lot opa . Aberam wanna waniyetu wikcemna šakowin sanpa zaptan , Haran etanhan iyaye cehan .
01012005	Qa Aberam tawicu Sari ikikcu , qa iye cincu cinhintku Lot nakun , qa taku icihdepi , taku tonpi kin owasin , wicanagi tona Haran en wicatonpi ko , qa unhdaka yapi , Kanan makoce kin ektakiya , qa Kanan makoce kin en hipi .
01012006	Qa Aberam makoce kin ohna ya , šekem ounye cin etu , More utuhu kin en . Unkan hehan Kanani kin makoce kin en unpi .
01012007	Unkan Jehowa Aberam en tanin iciye ca , Wicowazi nitawa kin makoce kin de waqu kta ce , eciya . Unkan Aberam hen wahna wošapi wan , Jehowa tanin iciye cin he kiciga .
01012008	Qa hetanhan unhdaka ya Betel iwiyohiyanpatanhan ĥe wan wanke cin , Betel wiyoĥpeyata , qa Hai wiyohiyanpata otahedan en e wakeya , qa heci wahna wošnapi wan kage ca Jehowa caje kin hoyekiya .
01012009	Qa ake Aberam unhdaka itokaĥ kiya ihdaka ya .
01012010	Unkan makoce kin he en wicaakiĥan , qa Aberam Egupta ekta apamahde ya , hen yanke kta , makoce en un qon nina wicaakiĥan nakaeš .
01012011	Qa Egupta ekta wanna hi kte cehan , tawicu Sari heciya , Winoĥinca owanyag wašte henica sdonwaya ;
01012012	Qa Egupton oyate kin waniyakapi kinhan , De tawicu kin ee ce , eyapi , kta qa miye maktepi kta qa niye niniyanpi kta .
01012013	Ceciya ce , tawinoĥtin ciya keya wo ; hecen tanyan waun kte ca , niye eciyatanhan minagi kin ni kta .
01012014	Qa Aberam Mizarim , Egupta hee , en hi qehan , Egupton oyate kin tawicu kin owanyag wašte ĥinca e wanyakapi .
01012015	Unkan Paro taakicita tancan winoĥinca kin wanyakapi , qa Paro en yatanpi , qa winoĥinca kin Paro ti kin en un kte cin icupi .
01012016	Qa iye kin on Aberam tanyan ecakiconpi ; unkan taĥin wanuyanpi yuha , tatanka nakun , qa šuktanka šonšonna mdoka wiye ko qa ookiye wica winyan ko , qa coma hena owasin .
01012017	Unkan Jehowa Paro oyutan , Sari Aberam tawicu kin on etanhan , Paro tiyohnaka tawa kin koya wowayazan tanka on wicakaštaka .
01012018	Unkan Paro Aberam kico qa heciya , Tokeca hecaminyecon ? He nitawin kin tokeca omayakidake šni he ?
01012019	De mitankši ce , ehe ciqon he tokeca heha he ? Hecen miš mduze kta iwacu tuka . Tuka nitawin wanhdaka wo . Ehdaku qa hunktiya wo .
01012020	Qa Paro wicašta tawa kin hena he iwahokonwicakiya , unkan hde šipi , tawicu taku yuhe cin ko owasin .
01013001	Unkan Aberam Egupta etanhan iyaya , iye tawicu kici , qa taku yuhe cin ko owasin , Lot nakun opa , itokaĥ makoce kin etu .
01013002	Qa Aberam wijica ĥinca , wanuyanpi , mazaska , qa mazaskazi ota yuha .
01013003	Qa itokaĥ makoce kin oti qon ohna ihdaka ku , Betel etu , wakeya iticage ciqon Betel qa Hai otahedan heciya ;
01013004	Tokag ehan wahna wošnapi kage ciqon he ekta , qa hen Aberam Jehowa caje kin hoyekiya .
01013005	Unkan Lot Aberam kici ihdaka un kin he taĥinca , qa tatanka wakeya ko yuha .
01013006	Qa witaya tonwanyanpi kte cin makoce kin iyowinwicakiye šni , ehaeš wanuyanpi ota yuhapi , heon witaya ounyanpi kta okitpanipi .
01013007	Unkan Aberam wanuyanpi wihan wicakiyapi kin qa Lot wanuyanpi wihan wicakiyapi kin akinicapi . Unkan hehan Kanani kin , Perazi kin ko makoce kin en ounyanpi .
01013008	Unkan Aberam Lot heciya , Unhdokinica kte šni , wihan wicakiya mitawa kin , qa wihan wicakiya nitawa kin nakun akinicapi kte šni , hunka wanjin unkiciye cin .
01013009	Makoce ocowasin nitokam wanke šni he ? Ceciciya ce , miye etanhan kinukankiya ya wo . Niš catka tanhan de cinhan miš etapa tanhan , qa niš etapa tanhan kinhan mišcatka tanhan mde kta ce .
01013010	Unkan Lot wankan etonwe , ca Jordan iyomdaye kin ocowasin Zohar itato owancaya mini yukan , ( Sodom Gomora kici Jehowa ihangye cin itokam , ) Jehowa tamaga kin iyecen , qa Egupta makoce kin iyecen .
01013011	Qa Lot Jordan ohna makoce kin owasin kahnige ca , Lot wiyohiyanpata kiya unhdaka ya , hecen otoiyohi hunka wanjitku kin etanhan kinukankiya iyayapi .
01013012	Aberam Kanan makoce kin en ounyan , qa Lot omdaye kin otonwe kin en ounye , ca Sodom en wakeya iticaga .
01013013	Unkan Sodom wicašta kin wicaštapi šni , qa Jehowa en nina waĥtanipisa .
01013014	Unkan Lot Aberam etanhan kinukankiya iyaye cin , he iyohakam Jehowa Aberam heciya , Išta kin yuwankan ikikcu , qa toki yaun kin ihdukšan etonwan wo ; waziyata , qa wiyoĥpeyata
01013015	Makoce kin de wandake cin sitomniyan cicu kte ca , wicowazi nitawa nakun owihankenšni yan .
01013016	Qa wicoicage , nitawa kin maka wiyaka sukaza iyenaka wakage kta . Wicašta wan maka wiyaka sukaza yawa okihi , hecinhan wicoicage nitawa nakun yawapi kta ce .
01013017	Najin qa makoce kin ohanske cin , qa ohdakinyan kin ecen omani wo , he cicu kta ce , eya .
01013018	Unkan Aberam ihdake ca Mamore utuhu kin he ĥebron en wanke cin ekta i , qa en ounye ca hen wahna wošnapi wan Jehowa kicaga .
01014001	Unkan Amrapel šinar en wicašta yatapi ounye cin he ehan , iye qa Ariyok Elasar en wicašta yatapi , qa Tidal Goim en wicašta yatapi ozuye kagapi .
01014002	Bera Sodom en wicašta yatapi , qa Birsa Gomora en wicašta yatapi , qa šinab Adma en wicašta yatapi , qa šemeber Zeboim en wicašta yatapi , qa nakun Bela , Zohar hee , he en wicašta yatapi , hena owasin azuwicayapi .
01014003	Sidim mdaye kin , mini skuya mde kin hee , en hena owasin ecipapi .
01014004	Waniyetu ake nom , hehanyan Kedorlahomer wowidake wicaya , tuka iake yamni kin hehan kipajinpi .
01014005	Unkan waniyetu iake topa , hehan Kedorlahomer qa wicašta yatapi owicape ciqon owasin upi , qa Repaim kin Ašteret Qarnayim en wicakaštaka , qa Zuzim kin ĥam en , qa Emim kin Qiratayim mdaye kin en , hena owasin wicakaštakapi .
01014006	Hori kin nakun , Sehir ĥe tawapi kin en Paran utuhu kin hetu , he ĥopuza kin en un .
01014007	Qa hdicupi , Mišpat wakoniya , Qadeš hee en , qa Ameleqi tamakocepi kin owasin awihnunipi , Amori kin tona Hazazon Tamar en ounyanpi kin nakun .
01014008	Hehan Sodom en wicašta yatapi , qa Gomora en wicašta yatapi , qa Adma en wicašta yatapi , qa Bela Zohar he en wicašta yatapi , qa Zeboim en wicašta yatapi hena owasin zuya iyayapi , qa Sidim mdaye kin en kicizapi .
01014009	Kedorlahomer Elam en wicašta yatapi , qa Tidal Goim en wicašta yatapi , qa Amrapel šinar en wicašta yatapi , qa Ariyok Elasar en wicašta yatapi , wicašta yatapi ece , uman topa uman zaptan ecipapi .
01014010	Unkan Sidim mdaye kin ohna bitumen woha ota , qa Sodom en wicašta yatapi Gomora en wicašta yatapi henios najicapi , qa ohinĥpayapi , qa umanpi kin , tona nipi kin , he onapapi .
01014011	Unkan Sodom Gomora ko woyuha , taku yutapi ko yuhapi qon , owasin icupi qa kihdapi .
01014012	Lot Aberam cincu cinhintku kin Sodom en un kin nakun , taku tawa ko owasin icupi , qa hecen hdapi .
01014013	Unkan wicašta wan okicize etanhan u qa Aberam Heberi kin wokiciyaka , utuhu oju Mamore Amori tawa kin en un ; Mamore Eškol Aner kici hunka wanjin wicaye cin , qa hena yamni Aberam kici dakon kiciyapi .
01014014	Unkan Aberam sunkaku wayaka ahdapi kin he nakihon , hehan wicašta opawinge yamni sanpa wikcemna sanpa šahdogan , iye ti kin en icagapi , qa onspewicakiyapi kin hena awicaye ca wicašta yatapi qon , Dan hehanyan wicakuwa .
01014015	Qa hanyen taokiye kici anawicatan , qa wicakaštake ca owicakuwa , Coba Damaskos icatka tanhan wanke cin hehanyan .
01014016	Qa oyuha qon owasin eyaku ; sunkaku Lot , qa taku tawa ko owasin , winoĥinca oyate ko owasin ahda .
01014017	Qa Kedorlahomer , qa wicašta yatapi owicape ciqon wicakaštakapi kin etanhan hdi kin , hehan Sodom wicašta yatapi kin itkokim ya ; Kaksiza mdaye kin ekta Wicašta yatapi takaksiza kin hee .
01014018	Unkan Melkizedek Salem en wicašta yatapi , Taku wakan otancanke wakiyušnapi kin , he aguyapi miniša ahna Aberam kahi ;
01014019	Qa yawašte , qa heya Wakantanka otancanke maĥpiya maka ko ocowasin tawa kin , he Aberam yawašte nunwe .
01014020	Qa Wakantanka otancanke kin , toka niyanpi kin nape kin en onihnake cin he yawaštepi nunwe , eya . Unkan taku owasin etanhan iwikcemna kin qu .
01014021	Unkan Sodom wicašta yatapi kin Aberam heciya , Oyate kin micu wo , qa woyuha kin he owasin icu , qa yuha un wo .
01014022	Unkan Aberam Sodom wicašta yatapi kin heciya , Jehowa Wakantanka otancanke kin maĥpiya maka ko ocowasin tawa kin , he ekta nape ye wakiya .
01014023	Taku nitawa kin etanhan hahonta wanjidan , hantpa wanjidan ešta iwacu kte šni , qa Aberam wawokihi wakaga ehe kte šni .
01014024	Tuka koška taku yutapi kin hecehnana , qa Aner Eškol qa Mamore wicašta omicipapi kin hena eepi , onšpa tawapi kin ikikcupi nunwe , eya .
01015001	Hena henakeca hehan , owanyake wan en Jehowa oie kin Aberam en hi , qa heciya , Aberam ihnuhan koyakipe cin ; wahacanka nitawa qa taku iyotan tanka yahduhe kte cin he miye ce .
01015002	Unkan Aberam heya , Jehowa Itancan taku mayaqu kta he ? Miš micinca manica qa wati kin taku ohnaka kin Eliezer Damaskon he yuha .
01015003	Qa Aberam heya , Miye cinca mayaqu šni , qa wicašta wan wati kin en tonpi kin he taku mitawa owasin yuhe kta .
01015004	Unkan Jehowa oie kin hoyekiya , De taku nitawa owasin yuhe kte šni ce . Tokešta nitezi kin etanhan inanpe kte cin he taku nitawa kin owasin yuhe kta ce , eya .
01015005	Qa tankan u ši , qa heciya , Maĥpiya ekta etonwe ca wicanhpi kin yawa oyakihi hecinhan hena yawa wo . Qa nicinca kin he iyenakecapi kta ce , eciya .
01015006	Unkan Aberam Jehowa oie kin wicada , qa he woowotanna kiciyawapi .
01015007	Unkan Jehowa heciya , Makoce kin de cicu , qa yahduhe kta e Ur Kašdim etanhan u ciciye cin , Jehowa he miye ce .
01015008	Unkan Jehowa Itancan , tokiya tanhan wahduhe kte cin sdonwakiye kta he ? eya .
01015009	Unkan , Pte wan waniyetu iyamni , qa tatokadan wan waniyetu iyamni , qa tamdoka wan waniyetu iyamni , hena owasin imicu wo , qa wakiyedan wan nakun , tin wakiyedan wan iyahna .
01015010	Unkan hena owasin ikikcu , qa cokaya okiwicakasdece ca wobašpe kin owasin iciyotakons ehnaka , qa zitkadan kin hena bašpe šni .
01015011	Unkan taku kinye cin woteca wicakte qon akan kun upi , unkan Aberam ĥam wicaya .
01015012	Unkan anpetu wi aisinyan iyaye kte cin , hehan woištima tanka wan Aberam ahinĥpaye ca nakun otpaza wohitike ĥinca .
01015013	Unkan Aberam heciya , Wowicake eciyatanhan he sdonya wo , nicinca makoce wan tawapi šni e en waniyetu opawinge tom ounyanpi kte , unkan wowidag wicayapi , qa iyoyag wicayapi kta .
01015014	Unkan oyate wan wicayuhe kte cin he mdaco kta , unkan hehan woyuha ota yuha hinanpapi kta .
01015015	Tuka niye hunkake wicayaye cin ekta tanyan yahde kte ca , pa niska wašte kinahan nihapi kta .
01015016	Qa wicoicage itopa kin , hehan deciya hdipi kta ce . Amori kin woaĥtani kin nahaĥin iyatahdepi šni ce .
01015017	Unkan wi iyaya hehan nina otpaza , qa oceti izita wan , petijanjan ideya wan ko , taku okicasdece ciqon itoopteya iyaya .
01015018	Anpetu kin he en Jehowa wicotakuye wan Aberam kicage ca heya , Makoce kin de Egupta watpa etanhan , watpa tanka Yuphrate eciyapi hehanyan nicinca wicawaqu kta .
01015019	Keni kin , qa Qenizi kin , qa Qadmoni kin ,
01015020	Qa ĥeti kin , qa Perazi kin , qa Repaim kin ,
01015021	Qa Amori kin , qa Kanani kin , qa Girgaši kin , qa Jebusi kin .
01016001	Unkan Aberam tawicu kin Sari cinca kiciton šni , qa Egupton wikoška wan yuha , Hagar eciyapi .
01016002	Qa Sari Aberam heciya , Iho Jehowa miye onamataka ; ceciye , wikoška wan mduhe cin he ekta ya ye ; okini cinca miciton kta , eya . Unkan Aberam Sari oie kin anagoptan .
01016003	Unkan Sari Aberam tawicu kin , he wikoška tawa , Hagar Egupton kin icu , qa Aberam hihnaku kin tawicu kta e qu ; wanna waniyetu wikcemna hehanyan , Aberam Kanan makoce en un qehan hecon .
01016004	Unkan Aberam Hagar en i , unkan ihdušaka wanhdake cehan , yuhe cin he išta kin on ihakta šni .
01016005	Unkan Sari Aberam heciya , šicaya ecamiconpi kin he niye en oiyanihde . Miye wikoška wan mduhe cin he cicu , nimaku kin ekta , unkan ihdušaka wanhdake ca išta kin on ihamakta šni , miye niye kici unkiyotahedan Jehowa yaco kta ce .
01016006	Unkan Aberam Sari heciya , Tokešta wikoška nitawa kin he ninape kin ohna un , token iyonicipi ecen ecakicon wo . Unkan Sari iyoyag ya ; unkan najica iyaya .
01016007	Unkan Jehowa taohnihde wan Hagar tinta kin en iyeya , mini ĥdoka wan ikiyedan , šur canku kin ohna mini ĥdoka he cin hee .
01016008	Qa heya , Sari tawikoška Hagar , tokiya tanhan yau he ? qa toki da he ? Unkan , Sari mayuha itoye kin etanhan nawajica ce , eya .
01016009	Unkan Jehowa taohnihde kin heciya , Niyuhe cin ekta icicawin hde , ca nape kin ihukuya ecihde wo .
01016010	Kinhan nicinca ota wakage kta , qa ota kin heon yawapi kta šni , Jehowa taohnihde kin Hagar eciya .
01016011	Qa , Iho ihdunišake cin cinca wanji yaton kte , ca Išmayel eya caš yakiton kta ; nicakije cin Jehowa nanihon kin heon etanhan .
01016012	Kinhan iš ikce wicašta kin heca kta . Wicašta owasin nape apaha wicayanke kta , qa iš wicašta owasin nape apaha yankapi kte , ca hunka wanjin wicaye cin owasin itokam ounye kte , Jehowa ohnihdeye cin eciya .
01016013	Unkan Wakantanka wanmayake cin he deciya awakita he ? eye ca , Jehowa okiye cin , he Wakantanka wanmayadake cin , eya cašton .
01016014	Heon wakoniya kin he , Tuwe ni qa wanmayake cin tawakoniya eciyapi ; he Qadeš qa Bered otahedan wanka .
01016015	Unkan Hagar Aberam cinca wan kiciton , qa Aberam cinca Hagar ton kin he Išmayel eya caš kiton .
01016016	Aberam wanna waniyetu wikcemna šahdogan sanpa šakpe , Hagar Išmayel Aberam kiciton kin hehan .
01017001	Unkan Aberam wanna waniyetu wikcemna napciwanka sanpa napciwanka , hehan Jehowa Aberam en tanin iciye ca , Taku wakan iyotan wašake cin he miye ; mitokam omani qa iyaonpepica šni un wo .
01017002	Kinhan odakonciciye kta qa , iyakicuya ciyuota kta eciya .
01017003	Unkan Aberam pustag eĥpeiciya ; unkan Wakantanka okiye ca heya ,
01017004	Odakonciciya qa oyate ota ate niyanpi kta ;
01017005	Qa detanhan Aberam eniciyapi kte šni , tuka Abereyam nicaje ee kta ; oyate ota ate niyanpi kte cin cicaga ce .
01017006	Qa nina yuota ciciye ca , oyate cicage kta , niye etanhan wicašta yatapi inanpapi kta .
01017007	Qa miye niye kici wicotakuye cicage kta , qa taku nitawa nihektam u kte cin hena koya , hecen wakage kta , tohanhanyan wiconi kte cin , hehanhanyan hecetu kta , hecen wakan mayada kta , qa nicinca nihektam u kte cin hena owihanke wanin wakan madapi kta .
01017008	Makoce en ihdaka yaun kin , Kanan makoce kin he owasin cicu kta , qa tona enitanhan u kte cin hena , qa owihanke wanin tawayapi kta qa taku wakan mayanpi kta .
01017009	Qa , niye wicotakuye mitawa kin yahduhe kta , niye , nicinca nihektam upi kte cin hena koya , wicoicage tawapi kin en .
01017010	Qa wicotakuye mitawa miye , qa niye kici , qa nicinca nihektam u kte cin hena koya , yahduhapi kte cin he dee ce . Tona wica un kinhan hena bakiĥdayapi kte .
01017011	Ce inkpa ha kin banicihdayapi kta qa odakonciciyapi wowapetokton kin hee kta .
01017012	Wicoicage nitawapi kin tona wica owasin yatipi kin ohna tonpi , qa nicin ca etanhan šni ešta , tuka oyate tokeca cinca , qa mazaska on opetonpi kin owasin , cincatonpi ehantanhan anpetu išahdogan baĥdayapi kta .
01017013	Tuwe yati kin ohna tonpi qa mazaska nitawa on opetonpi kin he baĥdayapi kta , qa odakonciyapi , niceĥpi kin en he wicotakuye owihanke wanice kta .
01017014	Tuwe wica baĥdayapi šni ce inkpa ha kin bakiĥdayapi šni kinhan , wicotakuye mitawa naksa , heon wicašta kin he oyate tawa kin etanhan bašpapi kta , Wakantanka Abereyam eciya .
01017015	Qa detanhan Sari nitawin kin Sari cajedate kte šni , Sara caje kin hee kta ce .
01017016	Qa he mdawašte kte ca , hetanhan cinca wan cicu kte ca , cinca niciton kte cin he nakun mdawašte kte ca , oyate ota nakun wicašta yatapi tanka hetanhan inanpapi kta , Wakantanka Abereyam eciya .
01017017	Unkan Abereyam pustag eĥpeiciye ca iĥa , qa cante kin mahen heya , Wicašta waniyetu opawinge cinca kicitonpi kta he ? qa Sara waniyetu wikcemna napciwanka cinca wan ton kta he ?
01017018	Hehan , Tokin Išmayel nitokam ni un , Abereyam Wakantanka eciya .
01017019	Unkan Wakantanka heya , Han ; awicakehan Sara nitawin cinca wan niciton kta , qa wicotakuye mitawa kin he kici wahdusuta kta ; cinca wicaye kte cin ihektam u kte cin , hena koya wicotakuye owihanke šniyan .
01017020	Išmayel on nakun naciĥon , on mdawašte kta , cinca ota icaĥye wakiye ca iyakicuya yuota wakiye kta , wicašta yatapi ake nom kicitonpi kte ca , oyate tanka icaĥye wakiye kta .
01017021	Tuka Izak kici wicotakuye mitawa kin wahdusuta kta , detanhan omaka wanjica kinhan , makoncage kin de en Sara ton kta .
01017022	Wakantanka ie ca ohinikiye cin , hehan Abereyam itokam wankan ikiyopta .
01017023	Unkan Abereyam cinhintku Išmayel ikikcu , qa nakun tona iye ti kin ohna wicatonpi kin , tona maza ska iye tawa on opewicaton kin hena koya owasin , tona wica iye ti kin ohna yakonpi kin hena , anpetu kin he en ce inkpa ha kin bawicakihdaya , Wakantanka
01017024	Abereyam wanna waniyetu wikcemna napciwanka sanpa napciwanka hehan iye ce inkpa ha kin bakiĥdayapi .
01017025	Qa cinhintku Išmayel waniyetu ake yamni hehan ce inkpa ha kin bakiĥayapi .
01017026	Abereyam cinhintku išmayel kici , anpetu wanjidan en bawicaĥdayapi .
01017027	Qa tiyohnaka wicašta owasin , ti kin ohna wicatonpi , qa oyate tokeca etanhan opewicatonpi kin hena koya , owasin Abereyam kici bawicaĥdayapi .
01018001	Unkan Mamore utuhu kin heciya , Abereyam wakeya tiyopa kin ekta iyotankehan yanke , ca wiyotanhan hehan Jehowa tanin iciya .
01018002	Unkan Abereyam wankan etonwan , qa wicašta yamni itokam najinpi wanwicayake ca , wakeya tiyopa kin etanhan itkowicakipe kta e inyang iyaye ca , maka kin en canpeška makehdeya iajin .
01018003	Qa , Itancan ni išta kin iyokipi ciya hecinhan ceciciya ce , nitaokiye kin etanhan sam iyaye šni wo .
01018004	Mini onge aupi on siha hdujajapi , qa can kin ihukuya ozi iciyapo .
01018005	Kinhan aguyapi onšpa cicaupi kta . Nicantepi kin iwakišakapo , heon nitaokiyepi kin en yahipi , qa hehan idadapi kta ce , eya . Unkan token ehe cin ecen econ wo , eyapi .
01018006	Unkan Abereyam wakeya kin en ohankoya hda , Sara ti kin ekta qa , Aguyapi iyutapi yamni kohanna icu qa pasuta qa aguyapi hmiyanyan kaga wo , eya .
01018007	Hehan Abereyam wanuyanpi ekta inyang ye ca , ptejincadan wan cepa qa wašte ikikcu , qa he koška wan qu ; unkan inaĥniyan pata .
01018008	Unkan pte asanpi qa pte asanpi ihdi , qa ptejincadan pata qon ikikcu , qa wicitokam ehde , qa iye wicikiyedan najin can kin ihukuya . Unkan wotapi .
01018009	Qa Sara nitawin kin toki un he ? eciyapi . Unkan , Wakeya ohna yanka ce eya .
01018010	Unkan , Detanhan omaka akihde kinhan , ake niye en cihi kta qa awektunje kte šni . Hehan nitawin Sara cinca wan ton kta . Unkan Sara wakeya tiyopa kin ohna wicašta kin ihektam yanka tuka he nahon .
01018011	Wanna Abereyam Sara kici wanakaš wotapi , napin kanpi ; winoĥinca ayakonpi kin he , Sara wanna ecece šni un .
01018012	Heon Sara cante mahen iĥa qa , Wamakanka hehan , qa mayuha iš nakun wicaĥinca ešta imduškin kta he ? eya .
01018013	Unkan Jehowa Abereyam heciya , Tokeca e Sara iĥa qa , Awicakehan wamakanka hehan cinca waton kta he ? eya he ?
01018014	Jehowa taku wanji okitpani tukte e he ? Tohantu kte cin ake niye en cihi , qa Sara hokšidan wan ton kta .
01018015	Hehan Sara kokipe ca heon anakiĥbe ca , Iwaha šni ce , eya . Unkan , Hiya iyaha ce , eya .
01018016	Hehan wicašta qon heciya tanhan najinpi , qa Sodom ektakiya etonwanpi ; unkan Abereyam awicaye kta e om iyaya .
01018017	Unkan Jehowa heya , Taku ecamon kte cin he Abereyam anawakiĥbe kta he ?
01018018	Abereyam iš oyate tanka , qa wašaka un kte ca iye eciyatanhan oyate maka ohnaka owasin yawaštepi kta ;
01018019	Qa de sdonwakiye , cinca wicaye cin , tiyohnaka kin iyahna taku owotanna qa ecetu econ wicaši kta , qa Jehowa tacanku kin okicipapi kta , hecen Jehowa Abereyam token wahoye cin owasin kicicaĥi kta .
01018020	Unkan Jehowa heya , Sodom qa Gomora ceyapi kin he tanka , qa waĥtanipi kin teĥika e nawaĥon , heon
01018021	Nakaha kun mde ca ceyapi kin mahiyohi kin ocowasin iyececa econpi kinhan sdonwaye kta , qa ecece šni kinahan sdonwaye kta ce , eya .
01018022	Unkan wicašta qon hetanhan iyayapi , wa Sodom en ipi , qa Abereyam nahaĥin Jehowa itokam yanka .
01018023	Qa Abereyam ikiyadan hinajin qa , Tona oĥan owotanna waĥtanipisa om ihang wicayaye kta he ?
01018024	Okini wicašta owotanna wikcemna zaptan otonwe kin en unpi ešta ihang yaye kta he ? Wicašta owotanna wikcemna zaptan kin hena on , otonwe en unpi kinhan , otonwe kin itonyape kte šni he ?
01018025	Wicašta oĥan owotanna waĥtanipisa om ihang wicayaye kta seca ; tokadan hecanon kte šni . Tona owotanna waĥtanipisa iyecen ecawicakiconpi kin he iyonicipi šni . Maka kin owancaya wayaco un kin he woyaco econ kte šni he ? eya .
01018026	Unkan Jehowa heya , Wicašta owotanna wikcemna zaptan Sodom otonwe en iyewaye cinhan , hena on otonwe kin ocowasin itonwape kta ce .
01018027	Unkan Abereyam ayupte ca , Maka mdu qa cahota hemaca qeyaš mayuhe cin taku ewakiye kta on iapi iwacu .
01018028	Okini wicašta owotanna wikcemna zaptan kin en zaptan ope kte šni seca ; zaptanna kin hena on otonwe kin ocowasin ihang yaye kta he ? eya . Unkan , Ihang waye kte šni , hen wikcemna tom sanpa zaptan iyewaye cinhan , eya .
01018029	Unkan ake ie kta e hda , qa , Okini hen wikcemna tom iyewicayapi kta , eya . Unkan , Wikcemna topapi on ecamon kte šni , eya .
01018030	Unkan , Mayuha ceciciye canniye maye šni wo ; iwae kta ce . Okini wikcemna yamni hen iyeyapi kta seca , eya . Unkan , Wikcemna yamni hen iyewicawaye cinhan ecamon kte šni , eya .
01018031	Unkan , Tokin Mayuhe cin taku ewakiye kta e epen . Okini wikcemna nonpa hen iyeyapi kta seca , eya . Unkan wikcemna nonpa on ihang waye kte šni ce , eya .
01018032	Unkan , Itancan ceciciye canniye maye šni wo ; wancadan iwae kta ce . Okini wikcemna en iyeyapi kta seca , eya . Unkan wikcemna on ihang waye kte šni ce , eya .
01018033	Unkan Jehowa Abereyam okiya ohinikiye cin hehan toki iyaya , qa Abereyam ekta hda .
01019001	Unkan ĥtayetu ehan ohnihde wicaye cin nom Sodom en hipi ; he icunhan Lot Sodom tiyopa kin en iyotankehan yanka , unkan Lot wanwicayke ca itkowicakipe kta najin hiyaya , qa wicitonkam patuš inajin .
01019002	Qa hewicakiya , Itancan ceciciyapi , wati kin en yapo , he wowidake mayaduhapi , heon hanyetu kin de wati kin en yukanpo . Siha kin hdujaja po , qa hanhanna yektapi , qa tokiya dapi hecinhan ekta katinyan yapo , ewicakiya . Unkan , Hiya , ocanku kin de ohna
01019003	Tuka nina cinwicakiya ; unkan aguyapi napohye codan špan ye ca nakun wowicakihan ; unkan yutapi .
01019004	Iwankapi kta itokam , Sodom otonwe wicašta kin owasin tipi kin he aohduteyapi , hokšidan wicaĥinca ko owasin , otonwe ihanke anokatanhan , henana otonwe ohnaka kin owasin kawitaya iheya .
01019005	Qa Lot kipanpi , Wicašta nom hanyetu kin de yati en hipi kin tukte epi he ? Tankan u wicaši wo ; sdonwicunyanpi kte , eyapi .
01019006	Unkan Lot ti kin etanhan inanpe , ca tiyopa kin ecen icu ,
01019007	Qa , Hunka wanjin ciyapi , ceciciyapi ce , ihnuhan hecen šicaya ecanonpi kin .
01019008	Micunkši nonpapi kin nahaĥin wicašta sdonye šni yakonpi , heniyos eicupi , qa token yacinpi ecen wicayakuwapi kta , tuka wicašta kin dena conkaške mitawa ohanzi ihukuya hipi kin heon takudan ecawicakiconpi šni po , ewicakiya .
01019009	Unkan , Tokan hiyaya wo . Wicašta kin de oyate tokeca , tuka den un kta wacin , qa hi qa he unyacopi wacin . Heon ihomeca niye iyotan šicaya unnicuwapi kta , oyate kin eyapi , qa Lot nina paškicapi qa tiyopa kin kaptujapi kta e en yapi .
01019010	Unkan ohnihde unpi kin tiyopa kin yuganpi , qa Lot ti mahen hdicu yapi , qa tiyopa kin onatakapi .
01019011	Unkan oyate kin wicašta cistina wicašta tanka ko , oyate otonwe ohnaka kin owasin , tiyopa kin en hiyeye cin hena išta gonge wicayapi , heon tiyopa kin yutantan akitapi .
01019012	Unkan ohnihde unpi kin Lot heciyapi , Nakun den takuyaya yukan he ? takoš yaye cin nicinkši , nicunkši , qa taku tona otonwe kin ohna duhe cin , de etanhan om tankata inanpa wo .
01019013	Otonwe kin de ihang unyanpi kta , heon unhipi ; oyate kin de owasin woaĥtani hoyapi , qa Jehowa itokam oiyahde iciyapi , heon otonwe kin de owihanke ye unhipi .
01019014	Unkan Lot tankata inanpe , ca wicašta takoš wicaye kte cin , hena hewicakiya , Otonwe kin de etanhan tankata inanpapo ; Jehowa otonwe kin de ihanke ye kta ce . Tuka takoš wicaye kte cin Lot cetunhdapi .
01019015	Anpao hinanpa , unkan ohnihde unpi kin Lot inaĥni yapi , qa , Najin wo ; nitawin ehdaku wo , qa nakun nicunkši nonpa den unpi kin , okini otonwe waĥtani kin en awihnuniniyanpi kta nace .
01019016	Tuka ihduwiyeyapi šni ; unkan ohnihde unpi nape etanhan wicayuzapi , Lot , qa tawicu , qa cunwintku nonpa nape kin wicayuzapi ; Jehowa hena onšiwicakicda , he etanhan otonwe kin tankan ewicayayapi .
01019017	Otonwe tankan awicaipi qa unman heciya , Napa wo , ni iciya wo . Ihnuhan nihektam eyatonwe cin . Omdaye kin ohna tuktedan inajin šni . He kin heciya onapa wo ; hecen yani kta ce .
01019018	Unkan Lot hewicakiya , hiya , Itancan ceciciya ce :
01019019	Wowidake yaya nitokam wopida iyeiciya , qa nitowaonšida kin icantoyahnake cin he miye . Tuka ĥe onawape kte cin owakitpani kta . Okini taku šica hiyohimaye ca mate kta , kowakipa .
01019020	Heon ceciciya , otonwe wan cistina den aškadan he cin , hee iyowahi kta owakihi kta . Ceciciya , heci ye mayan wo ; cistina tuka hecen on minagi kin ni kta .
01019021	Unkan , He wopida kin aciyupte kta ; otonwe cistina kin he ihang waye kte šni .
01019022	Onapa wo ; inaĥni wo . Tohan ehan yai šni hehanyan token waĥan kte šni , eciya He etanhan otonwe kin he Zohar eciyapi .
01019023	Wi toka hinanpa hehan Lot Zohar iyohi .
01019024	Unkan hehan Jehowa magaju ya , Sodom Gomora heniyoza kiya inyan zi peta ko Jehowa maĥpiya eciyatanhan ahinhe wicaya .
01019025	Otonwe kin hena owihanke wicaya , omdaye ko ocowasin , qa tona otonwe kin en ounyanpi , qa makoce kin hen peji koya .
01019026	Tuka Lot tawicu kin hakikta , unkan tancan kin tokeca hinhde ca miniskuya icu .
01019027	He icunhan , hanhanna Abereyam kikta , qa Jehowa okiye ciqon en etkiya ya .
01019028	Qa Sodom , Gomora , makoce ihdukšan koya atonwan ; unkan makoce kin he etanhan šota wan , maza šdoyapi oceti šota iyececa wankantkiya inanpe cin wanyaka .
01019029	Jehowa Omdaye otonwe kin hena , owikanke ye cin he icunhan , Abereyam kiksuye ca otonwe ohna Lot ounye cin ihang wicaye cin hetanhan Lot tankan iyaye ya .
01019030	Unkan Lot Zohar etanhan itawankanhde ye , ca ĥe wan akan cunwintku napin om e ounyan , Zohar he en un kte cin he wikopa heon , qa makoĥdoka wan cunwintku napin om oti .
01019031	Unkan tokapa kin he tankaku kin hecen eciya , Ate unye cin wanna wicaĥinca , qa maka ohnaka wanna wicašta wanica , maka akan econpi qon iyecen , tuwedan unkiye en hi kte šni .
01019032	Iho we , ate miniša yatke unkiye kta , qa kici unwanke kte ; hecen on ate etanhan wicoicage unhdoyapi kta .
01019033	Hanyetu , unkan atkuku miniša yatke kiyapi . Tokapa kin he tokaheya atkuku kici iwanka , tuka atkuku kin cunwintku en hiwanke cin he sdotkiye šni , nakun kikta kin .
01019034	Ihanhanna tokapa kin he tankaku kin heciya , Hinhan ate kici imunka ; ecin ake hanyetu kinhan , miniša yatke unkiye kte ca niš ito kici nunke kte , hecen on ate etanhan wicoicage unhdoyapi kta .
01019035	Unkan ake ihanyetu , unkan atkuku miniša yatke kiyapi ; iš ito hakakta kin atkuku kici iwanka . Iš ake cunwintku en hiwanke cin sdotkiye šni , qa kikta kin nakun .
01019036	Hecen Lot cunwintku napin atkuku etanhan hokšin itpihnakapi .
01019037	Tokapa kin hokšidan wan ton qa Moab eya caš kiton . He Moab oyate ate yapi anpetu kin dehan aiyahdeya .
01019038	Unkan hakakta kin iš eya hokšidan wan ton qa , Benami eya caš kiton . He Amon cinca kin anpe dehan aiyahdeya ate yapi .
01020001	Hehan Abereyam makoce itokaga kin ekta ihdaka ye ca , Qadeš qa šur otahedan iyotanke ca Gerar en ounyan .
01020002	Qa Abereyam tawicu Sara ke ca Mitankši kin dee ce , eya . Unkan Gerar wicašta yatapi Abimelek , he ekta ye wicaši qa Sara icu .
01020003	Unkan hanyen , Wakantanka Abimelek ekta hi , qa wowihanmde wan en heciya , Iho nite , winoĥinca iyacu kin he wicašta wan tawicu kin heca nakaeš .
01020004	Tuka Abimelek nahaĥin Sara ikiyedan wanke šni , qa heya ; Itancan oyate owotanna wan he nakun te wicayaye kta he ?
01020005	Mitankši kin dee , emakiye šni he ? qa winyan kin iš Timdo waya ce , emakiye šni he ? Micante kin ecedan qa minape iyecetu kin on hecamon .
01020006	Unkan Wakantanka wowihanmde kin en heciya , Miš nakun nicante ecedan kin en hecanon kin sdonwaya qa , heon ecihdaku , miye en wayaĥtani kte šni , qa dutan kte cin iyowin ciciye šni .
01020007	Qa wanna , iho , wicašta qon tawicu kin kicu wo , iš wicašta wokcan kin heca , kinhan niye on cekiye kta , hecen yani kta ; tuka ake yecu šni kinahan nite kte ca nakun taku nitawa kin owasin , he sdonya wo .
01020008	Unkan Abimelek hanhanna hin kikta , qa ookiye wicayuhe cin owasin wicakico , qa hena owasin owicakiyaka : Unkan wicašta kin nina kokipapi .
01020009	Unkan Abimelek Abereyam kico qa , Tokeca e hecaunyeconpi ? Qa niye en wawaĥtani kin tukte e on woaĥtani tanka wan miye qa oyate mitawa ko iyahde unyayapi ? Woecon wan econpi kta iyecece šni tuka hecamiyecon , eciya .
01020010	Qa , Taku wandaka on hecen ecanon he ? Abimelek Abereyam , eciya .
01020011	Unkan Abereyam heya , Tuwedan deciya Wakantanka ohoda šni qa mitawin on maktepi kta kepce cin heon hecamon ;
01020012	Qa awicakehan tankši waya ce . Ate waye cunwintku kin hee , tuka ina tawa šni , qa mitawin ee kta mduza .
01020013	Qa Wakantanka ate ti kin etanhan ihdaka ye maye cehan winyan qon hewakiya ; Taku wašta ionšimayada kte cin dee ce . Makoce owasin tokiya kašta en unki kinhan , Timdo emakiya wo , epe ciqon , eya .
01020014	Hehan Abimelek taĥin wanuyanpi ikikcu , qa tatanka qa hokšidan wicinyanna ko iwicakikcu qa Abereyam qu ; tawicu Sara nakun kicu .
01020015	Qa Abimelek heya , Mitamakoce nitokam wanka ce ; tukten niišta iyonicipi kinhan hen iyotanka wo .
01020016	Qa Sara heciya , Iho nitimdo mazaska kektopawinge waqu ; iho he niišta akaĥpe kte cin ee , tona nici unpi kin owasin en , qa tokan nakun owasin en ; hecen Sara iyopeyapi .
01020017	Hehan Abereyam Wakantanka icekiya ; unkan Wakantanka Abimelek asni yan , tawicu kici qa wikoška yuhe cin owasin . Unkan cinca tonpi .
01020018	Jehowa , Sara Abereyam tawicu kin on etanhan , Abimelek tiyohnaka tawa owasin tamnipi kin suksuta onawicataka tuka qon .
01021001	Unkan Jehowa heye ciqon , he iyecen Sara ekta hi , qa Jehowa , eciye ciqon , he iyecen ecakicon .
01021002	Unkan Sara ihdušake ca Abereyam okanta cinca wan kiciton ; Wakantanka eye ciqon iyehantu qehan .
01021003	Unkan Abereyam cinhintku kicitonpi , Sara ton kin he , Izak eya caš kiton .
01021004	Qa Abereyam Izak bakiĥdaya anpetu išahdogan tonpi kin ehantanhan , Wakantanka econ ši qon iyecen .
01021005	Abereyam wanna waniyetu opawinge , hehan cinhintku Izak kicitonpi .
01021006	Unkan Sara heya , Wakantanka iĥa mayan , qa tona naĥonpi kin imiciyuškinpi kta .
01021007	Qa Sara hokšiyoqopa azin kiye kte cin , tuwe Abereyam eciye kta he ? wicaĥinca tuka cinca weciton kin , eya .
01021008	Unkan hokšidan kin tanka aye ca azin ayaštan kiyapi . Unkan Izak azin ayaštan kiyapi anpetu kin he en , Abereyam wohe ca wicota wicakico .
01021009	Unkan Hagar Egupton kin cinhintku Abereyam kiciton kin he , wowiĥaĥa kin he Sara wanyake ca ;
01021010	Wikoška kin de cinhintku kin iyahna tankan ye wicaya ye . Wikoška kin de cinhintku kin , micinkši Izak kici woyuha tawaye kte šni , eya .
01021011	Unkan oie kin he , Abereyam išta kin en teĥike ĥinca , cinhintku kin heon etanhan .
01021012	Unkan Wakantanka Abereyam heciya , Wikoška duhe cin , qa hokšidan kin on etanhan , niišta kin en teĥike šni nunwe . Taku Sara eniciye cin owasin ecen ho kin anagoptan wo . Izak he en wicoicage nitawa kin caje yatapi kta .
01021013	Wikoška cinhintku kin nicinkši kin hee , heon he nakun oyate wan icaĥ wakiye kta ce .
01021014	Unkan Abereyam hanhanna hin kikta , qa aguyapi mini apaĥta wan ahna icu , qa Hagar qu , taĥpa kin akan ehnaka , hokšidan nakun qa toki ye ši . Unkan iyaye ca Beršeba tinta kin onuni .
01021015	Unkan mini apaĥta kin etanhan mini wanna yahepapi , qa hokšidan kin canhaka wan ihukuya eĥpekiya ;
01021016	Qa iyaye ca iyotakons iyotanka kitana tehan , wanhinkpe kihiyeyapi hehanyan : Hokšidan te kte cin wanwahdake kte šni ce , eya ; heon aisinyan iyotanke ca hoyeye ca ceya .
01021017	Unkan Wakantanka hokšidan ho kin nahon , qa Wakantanka taohnihde maĥpiya eciyatanhan Hagar kipan , Hagar taku yaka he ? Wakantanka he oyanke kin etanhan hokšidan ho kin nahon . Kokipe šni wo .
01021018	Najin qa hokšidan kin ikikcu qa , nape kin on hduha wo . Iye oyate tanka wan icaĥ wakiye kta ce , eya .
01021019	Qa Wakantanka winyan išta kin yuĥdoka , unkan miniĥdoka wan wanyake ca ekta i , qa mini apaĥta kin iyatahde ye ca hokšidan kin yatke kiya .
01021020	Unkan Wakantanka hokšidan kin kici un ; hecen tanka icage ca tinta kin en ounye ca itazipa on waoka .
01021021	Qa Paran tinta kin en ounye ca hunku kin Egupta makoce kin etanhan , tawicu kte cin kiciyuza .
01021022	Unkan hehan Abimelek qa taakicita tancan Pikol henioza Abereyam heciyapi ; Taku ecanon kin owasin en Wakantanka oniciya .
01021023	Iho hecen eya wo , Wakantanka namaĥon cihnaye kte šni , nicinkši nitakoja ko wicawahnaye kte šni , taku wašte ecamiyecon kin iyecen ecacicon kta , makoce en ounwaye cin nakun .
01021024	Unkan , Miš ecen eya wakonze kta ce , Abereyam eya .
01021025	Hehan miniĥdoka wan Abimelek taokiye kin kipi qon , he Abereyam cajeyate ca he on Abereyam Abimelek iyopeya .
01021026	Unkan , Tuwe hecon kin sdonwaye šni , qa ni nakun omayakidake šni , nakun miš he nawaĥon šni , nakaha heceyedan , eya .
01021027	Unkan Abereyam taĥinca wanuyanpi pte wanuyanpi ko ikikcu , qa hena Abimelek qu ; unkan napin odakota wan kicicagapi .
01021028	Hehan Abereyam taĥinca cinca wiyedan šakowin akipam ewicaĥde .
01021029	Unkan Abimelek Abereyam heciya , Taĥinca wiyedan šakowin kinukan ewicayahde kin he taku he .
01021030	Unkan Miniĥdoka kin de miš waqe cin he yuotaninpi kte cin , heon taĥinca wiyedan šakowin kin hena minape kin etanhan iyacu kta , eya .
01021031	Unkan heon etanhan makoce kin he Beršeba eciyapi , napin heciya Wakantanka namaĥon eya , ekiciyapi .
01021032	Unkan Beršeba hen odakota wan kicicagapi ; hehan Abimelek najin taakicita tancan nakun qa Pilištim tamakocepi kin ekta hdapi .
01021033	Unkan Abereyam Beršeba heciya taškoju wan oju , qa hen Jehowa Taku wakan owihanke wanica hoyekiya .
01021034	Qa Abereyam Pilištim tamakocepi kin en anpetu ota ounyan .
01022001	Unkan hena owasin iyohakam , Wakantanka Abereyam iyutan ye ca heciya , Abereyam , eya houkiya . Unkan , Iho miye ce , eya .
01022002	Unkan , Nicinkši heceyedan wašte yakidake cin Izak he icu , qa Moriya makoce kin ekta ye ca heciya ĥe wan ociciyake kte cin he akan petan wahdušna wo , eya .
01022003	Unkan Abereyam hanhanna hin kikta , qa šuktanka šonšonna aqin kiton , qa koška nom iwicakikcu cinhintku Izak nakun , can on wošna kte cin he kakse ca , najin qa hena om , makoce tukte en Wakantanka cajeyate ciqon heciya iyaya .
01022004	Anpetu iyamni Abereyam wankan etonwe ca , tukten ke cin he tehan tanhan wanyaka .
01022005	Qa Abereyam koška wicayuhe cin hewicakiya , Den iyotankapo šuktanka šonšonna iyahna , qa miš hokšidan kici kan unkipi hinhan canpeška makehdeya unkanpi , qa den dukanpi kin en unhdipi kta .
01022006	Qa Abereyam can on wašna kte cin icu , qa cinhintku Izak akan ehnake ca peta isan ko nape kin en icu , qa sakim iyayapi .
01022007	Unkan Izak atkuku Abereyam kici okiye ca , Ate , eya . Unkan Micinkši nawaĥon ce , eya . Unkan , Iho peta can ko yukan , tuka woteca kin wošnapi on tukte e he ? eya .
01022008	Unkan , Micinkši Wakantanka taĥin wanuyanpi wakiyušnapi on okide kta , eya . Hecen sakim yapi .
01022009	Qa wanna tukten Wakantanka ye ši qon hen hiyohipi , qa hen Abereyam wahna wošnapi wan kage ca , cinhintku Izak iyakaške ca wahna wošnapi kin akan ekihnaka , can kin iwankam .
01022010	Qa cinhintku te kiye kta e nape kiyugate ca isan kin ikikcu .
01022011	Hehan maĥpiya kin eciya tanhan Jehowa ohnihde ye cin kipan , Abereyam , Abereyam , eya . Unkan Nawaĥon ce , eya .
01022012	Unkan , Hokšidan kin ekta ninape kin ye kiye šni , qa takudan ecakicon šni wo . Wanna niye Wakantanka ikoyape cin sdonwaya ce ; nicinkši heceyedan , tuka mayaqu kta wicayada he etanhan , eya .
01022013	Hehan Abereyam wankan etonwe ca , inyun iĥeyata tamdoka wan oteĥi ohna he kin on ikoyag najin , he wanyake ca , Abereyam ekta i , qa tamdoka kin icu , qa cinhintku kin hee kiya hee petan wošna .
01022014	Qa Abereyam makoce kin he , Jehowa wiwanhdake kta , eya caš ton ; heon Jehowa he tawa kin akan tanin iciye kta ce , nahaĥin eyapi .
01022015	Unkan maĥpiya kin eciya tanhan Jehowa ohnihde ye cin inonpa akihde Abereyam kipan ;
01022016	Miye kaeš caje mihdate Jehowa eya ; Taku ecanon kin de nicinca wanjidan tuka itonyakipe šni ;
01022017	Heon wowašte on ciyawašte kta , nicinca iyakicuya yuota wakiye kta . Maĥpiya wicanhpi iyena , qa miniwanca kahda wiyaka sukaza iyeye cin iyena , taku nitawa iyacin kte ca , nicinca toka wicayapi kin otonwe tawapi kin yuhapi kta .
01022018	Qa mioie kin anayagoptan kin heon nicinca kin on maka kin oyate owasin wicayawaštepi kta ce , eya .
01022019	Unkan Abereyam koška wicayuhe cin ekta hda ; unkan najinpi qa yuwitaya Beršeba ekta hdapi ; qa Abereyam Beršeba en ounyan .
01022020	Hena owasin iyohakam Abereyam hecen eya okiyakapi ; Milka he nakun nicinye Naĥor he cinca kiciton .
01022021	Uz tokapa kin hee , qa sunkaku Buz , qa Qemuel Aram he atkuku ;
01022022	Qa Kesed , qa ĥazo , qa Pildaš , qa Idlap , qa Betuel .
01022023	Unkan Betuel he Rebeka kicitonpi . Hena šahdogan kin Milka he Naĥor Abereyam cincu kin kiciton .
01022024	Unkan tawicu tokeca kin , Ruma eciyapi he Teba , qa Gaham , qa Taĥos , qa Mahaka hena wicaton .
01023001	Unkan Sara waniyetu opawinge sanpa wikcemna nonpa sanpa šakowin henakeca , waniyetu kin hena Sara ni .
01023002	Hehan Sara ta , Arba otonwe kin heciya , ĥebron Kanan makoce kin etu hee . Unkan Abereyam Sara on iyokišice ca akiceye kta e en hi .
01023003	Hehan Abereyam tawicu te cin itokapa tanhan najin qa , ĥet cinca wicaye cin owicakiya .
01023004	Qa , Miš wicašta ihdaka waun qa aškatudan nicipi wahimdotanka , wicašta hnakapi mduhe kta e niyepi om maqupo ; kinhan makite cin mitokapa tanhan wehnake kta ce , eya .
01023005	Unkan ĥet cinca wicaye cin ayuptapi , qa Abereyam heciyapi ;
01023006	Itancan anaungoptanpo : Wicašta yatapi wakan unkiyepi cokaya henica . Wicašta hnakapi unhapi kin tukten iyonicipi kin nicite cin en kihnaka wo . Unkiš wanjidan kašta wicašta hnakapi unhapi kin hen nicite cin yehnake kta e teĥinda kte šni .
01023007	Unkan Abereyam najin qa ĥet cinca wicaye cin oyate makoce yuhapi kin wicitokam apatuja .
01023008	Qa owicakiye ca , Makita mitokapa tanhan wehnake kte cin he iyonicipipi hecinhan anamagoptanpi , qa Epron Zohar he cinhintku cin makiyapo .
01023009	Kinhan Makpela imnija oĥdoka yuhe cin , tamaga ihanke en un kin , mazaska iyenakeca kin heon maqu kte cinhan , niyepi cokaya wicašta hnakapi wan mduhe kta ce , ewicakiya .
01023010	Unkan Epron ĥet cinca wicaye wicehna ounyan ; qa Epron ĥeti kin Abereyam ayupta ; ĥet cinca wicaye cin , otonwe tiyopa ohna upi kin hena owasin naĥonpi ;
01023011	Hiya , Itancan namaĥon wo . Maga kin cicu ; imnija oĥdoka en un kin he nakun cicu . Mitaoyate cinca wicaye cin wanmayakapi he cicu . Nicite cin kihnaka wo , eya .
01023012	Unkan Abereyam oyate makoce tawapi kin wicitokam patuja .
01023013	Qa ia , Iho amayadupte cinahan , namaĥon wo . Maga kin on mazaska cicu kta . Icu wo ; kinhan makite cin wehnake kta , Epron eciya , oyate makoce yuhapi kin hena naĥonpi .
01023014	Unkan Epron Abereyam ayupte ca heciya ;
01023015	Itancan namaĥon wo . Maga kin mazaska opawinge topa iyehantu ce ; tuka unkiyotahedan he taku ? Nicite cin ekihnaka wo .
01023016	Unkan Epron ie cin he Abereyam anagoptan , qa mazaska opawinge tom wopeton icupi kin heca Abereyam aspe ye ton qa qu , he Epron ĥet cinca wicaye cin naĥonpi cajeyate ciqon hee .
01023017	Unkan Epron tamaga Makpela en wanka , Mamore iyotakons he qu ; maga kin imnija oĥdoka he en wanke cin he nakun , qa can tona he en han qa tona ihdukšan he cin he nakun owasin ;
01023018	Abereyam tawa kte cin , ĥet cinca wicaye cin tona otonwe tiyopa kin ohna yapi kin he wanyakapi .
01023019	Hehan Abereyam tawicu Sara ekihnaka ; Makpela maga imnija oĥdoka kin he en , Mamore ikiyedan , ĥebron Kanan makoce kin etu hee .
01023020	Unkan maga imnija oĥdoka iyahna , Abereyam wicašta hnakapi on yuhe kte cin , ĥet cinca wicaye cin qupi .
01024001	Unkan Abereyam wanna wicaĥinca omaka ota ; unkan Jehowa taku owasin en Abereyam yawašte .
01024002	Unkan Abereyam he taokiye tiyohnaka tawa tokapa kin , taku yuhe cin owasin awanyag un kin heciya ; Ninape kin miceca ihukuya ekihnaka wo ;
01024003	Kinhan , Jehowa Taku wakan maĥpiya maka ko yuhe cin namaĥon , eye ciciye kta , Kanani oyate om manke cin cunwintkupi kin etanhan micinkši on winoĥinca iyacu kte šni .
01024004	Tuka mitamakoce qa mitakuye kin hena ekta de kte ca , hetanhan micinkši Izak on winoĥinca iyacu kta , kehe kta ce , eya .
01024005	Unkan , taokiye kin heya , Okini winoĥinca kin makoce kin de ekta omape kta tawatenye kte šni ; hecinhan makoce etanhan yau qon , nicinkši ake ekta ye wakiye kta he ?
01024006	Unkan , Ihnuhan micinkši icicawin heciya ye yakiye cin .
01024007	Taku Wakan maĥpiya yuhe cin , ate ti kin etanhan qa makoce wan en matonpi kin etanhan , imacu qa omakiye ca , Makoce kin de nicinca waqu kta ce , eya konza , he taohnihde kin nitokam ye ši kta , kinhan micinkši kin on heciya tanhan winoĥinca wan iyacu kta
01024008	Winoĥinca kin onipe kta tawatenye šni , hecinhan iyakonze kin de on iyaonpepicašni yaun kta , tuka micinkši heciya ye yaye kte šni ce .
01024009	Unkan taokiye qon nape kin iye yuhe cin Abereyam ceca kin ihukuya ekihnake ca ecen eya konza .
01024010	Qa ookiye kin , iye yuhe cin camo tawa kin etanhan , camo wikcemna , qa iye yuhe cin taku wašte tawa kin owasin etanhan icu , qa hena yuha iyaye ca Naĥor otonwe kin ekta i , Aram watpa otahedan etu .
01024011	Qa otonwe kin itankan miniĥdoka ikiyedan , camo kin canpeška makehdeya inajin wicakiya , ĥtayetu mini huwe ipi eca iyehantu .
01024012	Qa heya , Jehowa Abereyam mayuhe cin Wakan nida ceciciya , nakaha tanyan ihuni makiye ca Abereyam mayuhe cin he wowašte ecakincon ye .
01024013	Miniĥdoka kin ekta nawajin ; qa otonwe kin wicašta cunwintkupi kin mini huwe upi kta .
01024014	Qa wikoška wan tuwe kašta hewakiye kta ; Wakiškotpa nitawa kin au wo , mini mdatke kta ce ; unkan , Yatkan ye qa camo nitawa kin nakun yatke wicawakiye kta , eye cinhan , tokin nitaokiye Izak yuhen yakahnige cin hee , kinhan mayuhe cin wowaonšida ecayecon
01024015	Unkan iš ia nahaĥin ayaštan šni ehan , Rebeka u , Abereyam cincu Naĥor tawicu Milka he cinhintku Betuel he cunwintku kin hee , wakiškotpa hiyeta onpe ca u .
01024016	Wikoška owanyag wašte ĥinca , hokšiwina , qa wicašta tohini sdonye šni , miniĥdoka kin ekta kun ye ca wakiškotpa kin ojudan icu qa wankan hiyu .
01024017	Unkan ookiye qon itkokim inyang ye ca , Wakiškotpa duhe cin etanhan mini onge yatke makiya wo , eya .
01024018	Unkan , Itancan yatkan ye , eye ca wakiškotpa kin nape kin on kun akihde , qa yatke kiya .
01024019	Unkan ayaštan hehan , Camo nitawa kin nakun hena on mini awau kta , yatkan ayaštanpi kin hehanyan , eya .
01024020	Qa inaĥni qa wakiškotpa tanka kin okaštan , qa inyanka miniĥdoka kin ekta mini huwe ya heon , qa camo kin owasin mini wicakahi .
01024021	Unkan wicašta kin yušinyaye ca taku eye šni , canku ohna u kin he Jehowa ohinniyan tanyan ikiyuštan kta hecinhan he sdonye kta .
01024022	Unkan camo kin mini yatkan ayaštanpi , hehan wicašta qon mazaskazi maza oin tanka , mazaska hanke iyecen tke , he icu qa nakun maza huhu nom mazaska wikcemna iyecetu , hena owasin wikoška nape kin en ye kiya ;
01024023	Qa , Tuwe hunkake yaya he ? Omakiyaka wo , niyate ti kin ohna unkiwankapi kta okan he ? eya .
01024024	Unkan , Milka cinhintku Betuel Naĥor kiciton kin he cunwintku kin miye ce , eya .
01024025	Qa , Peji puze ca taku yutapi ko ota , qa nakun wankapi kta okan ce , eciya .
01024026	Unkan wicašta qon pamahdedan yanke ca Jehowa cekiye ca ,
01024027	Jehowa Abereyam mayuhe cin taku wakan da kin he yawaštepi nunwe . Towicake towaonšida ko mayuhe cin ektakiya ayuštan šni , tuka mayuha sunkaku ti kin canku kin ohna Jehowa amau ce , eya .
01024028	Unkan wikoška kin dus hde ca iye hunku ti kin en hena owasin oyaka .
01024029	Rebeka timdoku wan yukan , Laban eciyapi , qa Laban iš dus iyaya wicašta qon ekta miniĥdoka kin en .
01024030	Laban oin tanka , qa maza huhu tankšitku nape kin akan wanyake ca Rebeka tankšitku oie ye cin , Wicašta kin hecen emakiya eye cin he nahon qa , hehan wicašta qon miniĥdoka kin ekta , camo kin icaĥda najin kin en hi .
01024031	Qa heya , Jehowa he niyawašte kin u wo . Tokeca tankan nayajin he ? Miš tipi kin wanna wiyeya wakaga , camo yukanpi kte cin nakun .
01024032	Unkan wicašta qon tipi kin ekta hi ; unkan camo kin kiyuške ca peji puza taku yutapi ko camo kin qu , qa mini on siha hdujaja kta wicašta om hi kin nakun hdujajapi kta e au .
01024033	Qa woyute nakun qu . Unkan , Taku on wahi kin owahdake šni kinhan onšpadan wate kte šni ce , eya . Unkan , Ia wo eya .
01024034	Unkan , Abereyam tahokšidan wan he miye :
01024035	Qa Jehowa he mayuhe cin nina yawašte , qa taĥin wanuyanpi qu , qa pte , qa mazaska , qa mazaskazi , qa wicašta winyan ko wowindag wicaye cin , qa camo , qa šuktanka šonšonna , hecen wicašta okinihan .
01024036	Qa mayuhe cin tawicu kin Sara cinca wanton , mayuhawanna wicaĥinca hehan he kiciton , unkan taku yuhe cin owasin kicu .
01024037	Qa Kanani makoce tawapi kin en manke cin he cunwintkupi kin etanhan micinkši on winoĥinca duze kte šni :
01024038	Tuka hunkake wicawaye cin tipi kin ekta de kte ca , takuwicawaye cin etanhan micinkši on winoĥinca wan duze kta ce , mayuhe cin eya konza , keye maši .
01024039	Unkan , Okini winoĥinca kin mici u kte šni , mayuhe cin ewakiya .
01024040	Unkan , Taku wakan wada Jehowa itokam mawani kin , he taohnihde wan nici ye ši kte ca , mitakuye qa ate ti kin etanhan , winoĥinca wan micinkši on duze kta e , canku yaye cin tanyan ihuni niciye kta ce .
01024041	Tuka taku eya konze ciciye cin nihiyahde kte šni , takuwicawaye cin ekta de cinhan , qa nicupi šni kinhan , hehan taku eya konze ciciye cin iyahde niciye kte šni , emakiya .
01024042	Unkan nakaha miniĥdoka kin ekta wahi qa hepa , Jehowa Abereyam mayuhe cin he wakan nida , canku ohna wau kin tanyan ihuni mayakiya hecinhan ;
01024043	Iho miš miniĥdoka kin icaĥda nawajin qa wikoška wan mini huwe hiyu qa , Wakiškotpa duhe cin etanhan mini onge yatke makiya ye , ewakiye kta .
01024044	Unkan , Yatkan ye , qa nakun camo nitawa kin mini wicawakahi kta ce , emakiye cinhan , winoĥinca wan mayuhe cin cinhintku yuze kta e Jehowa kahnige cin hee kte .
01024045	Miš cante mahen ia nahaĥin mdaštan šni , unkan inyun Rebeka hinanpe ca miniĥdoka kin ekta kun i qa mini icu ; unkan , Tokin yatke mayakiyen , ewakiya .
01024046	Unkan tawakiškotpa kin inaĥniyan kun ahi qa , Yatkan ye , qa camo nitawa kin nakun woyatke wicawaqu kta ce , eya ; unkan mdatke ca camo kin nakun yatkanpi .
01024047	Unkan imonge ca , Tuwe cunwintku niyan he ? ewakiya . Unkan Betuel cunwintku he miye , Naĥor cinhintku Milka kiciton kin hee . Hehan oin tanka ite kin akan ewahnaka , maza huhu nakun nape kin akan .
01024048	Qa pamahdedan manke ca Jehowa cewakiya , Jehowa Abereyam mayuhe cin taku wakan da kin he mayuhe cin cinhintku kin on , mayuhe cin sunkaku cunwintku iwacu kta e canku wicaka ohna amau kin he mdatan .
01024049	Qa niyepi wanna wowaonšida wowicake ko mayuhe cin ecayeconpi kte cinhan omakiyakapo , qa ecayeconpi kte šni kinhan omakiyakapo : etapa tanhan mduhomni kta qa iš catka tanhan , eya .
01024050	Unkan Laban Betuel ko ayuptapi qa Taku kin de Jehowa etanhan u qa taku šica qa iš taku wašte unkeniciyapi kta unkokitpanipi ce , eyapi .
01024051	Iho Rebeka nitokam un ; icu qa hda wo . He niyuhe cin cinhintku kin yuze kta , Jehowa oie ye cin iyececa .
01024052	Unkan Abereyam taokiye kin iapi hena nahon qehan , Jehowa ohoda kta e makata patuš iyaya .
01024053	Hehan ookiye qon mazaska oin qa mazaskazi oin ikikcu , wokoyake nakun , qa hena Rebeka qu , timdoku hunku ko taku teĥika wacaqu .
01024054	Hehan wotapi qa wayatkanpi , iye wicašta opapi kin hena koya . Wankapi qa hanhanna kiktapi qa . Mayuhe cin ekta hdicu mayan wo , eya .
01024055	Unkan timdoku hunku ko , Wikoška unkicipi yanke kte , wikcemna can hehanyan , hehan ye kta ce , eyapi .
01024056	Unkan , Jehowa iš canku mitawa kin tanyan ihuni mayan heon mayutehanpi šni po . Mayuhe cin ekta kihde mayanpo , ewicakiya .
01024057	Unkan , Wikoška kin unkicopi qa , iye i kin etanhan unkiwangapi kta ce , eyapi .
01024058	Qa Rebeka kipanpi , qa , Wicašta kin de kici de kta he ? eciyapi . Unkan , Mde kta ce , eya .
01024059	Unkan Rebeka tawinoĥtinpi kin ye yapi , qa azinkiye ciqon , qa Abereyam taokiye , qa wicašta tawa nakun .
01024060	Qa Rebeka yawaštepi qa , Unkitawinoĥtinpi kin he niye , kektopawinge oyawa tanka icaga wo , qa cinca wicayaye kte cin toka wicayapi otonwe kin yuhapi kte , eciyapi .
01024061	Hehan Rebeka najin , wikoška yuhe cin nakun , qa camo akan iyotankapi , qa wicašta qon kici iyayapi . Hecen ookiye qon Rebeka icu qa kihda .
01024062	Wanna Izak miniĥdoka , Tuwe ni un kin wanmayaka tawa kin hetanhan u , qa makoce puze cin en iyotanka .
01024063	Qa ĥtayetu ca Izak cekiye kta e manin ya , hehan wankan etonwe ca camo upi kin wanwicayaka .
01024064	Rebeka nakun wankan etonwe ca Izak wanyake ca camo kin etanhan ipsica .
01024065	Qa ookiye kin heciya , Wicašta wan itkounkipapi ĥewoskan omani kin he tuwe ? Unkan , Mayuhe cin hee , ookiye kin eya . Unkan ite akaĥpe wan icu qa aihdaĥpa .
01024066	Unkan ookiye kin , taku token econ kin owasin Izak okiyaka .
01024067	Hehan Izak iye hunku Sara tawakeya kin mahen Rebeka tin ye ši , qa yuze ca tawicu kin wašte kidaka . Hecen Izak iye hunku Sara te cin iyohakam iwacintonhnag yapi .
01025001	Hehan ake Abereyam winoĥinca wan yuza , Qetura eciyapi .
01025002	Unkan cinca kiciton kin dena eepi , Zimran , qa Jokšan , qa Medan , qa Midian , qa Išbak , qa šuha .
01025003	Unkan Jokšan iš šeba qa Dedan kicitonpi . Unkan Dedan iš Ašurim , qa Letušim , qa Lumim cinkši wicaya .
01025004	Unkan Midian cinca wicaye cin , Epa , qa Heper , qa Hanok , qa Abida , qa Eldaha . Hena owasin Qetura cinkši wicaya .
01025005	Unkan Abereyam taku yuhe cin iyuĥpa Izak qu .
01025006	Tuka winoĥinca uman cinca Abereyam kicitonpi kin hena Abereyam taku wicaqu , qa nahaĥin iye ni un kin wiyohinyanpata makoce kin ekta ye wicaši , cinhintku Izak etanhan .
01025007	Abereyam anpetu tawa kin waniyetu ni un kin dena ee , waniyetu opawinge sanpa wikcemna šakowin sanpa zaptan , hehanyan ni .
01025008	Hehan Abereyam niya šni ta iyaya , pa ska wašte , qa wicaĥinca imna ; hehan taoyate kin ekta okipa yapi .
01025009	Qa cinca wicaye cin Izak Išmayel kici kihnakapi ; Makpela imnija oĥdoka kin en Mamore itokam , Zohar ĥeti he cinhintku Epron tamaga qon en .
01025010	Maga wan Abereyam ĥet cinca wicaye cin opewicakicaton , he en Abereyam hnakapi , tawicu Sara kici .
01025011	Unkan Wakantanka , Abereyam te cin iyohakam , cinhintku kin Izak yawašte , qa Izak tuwe ni un qa wanmayake cin miniĥdoka tawa kin ekta ounyan .
01025012	Hagar Egupton kin Sara tawikoška kin he Abereyam cinca wan kiciton , Abereyam cinhintku Išmayel wicoicage tawa kin dee .
01025013	Išmayel cinca wicaye cin cajepi kin deepi , wicowazipi qa cajepi kin iyececa . Išmayel cinca tokapa kin he Nebayot , hehan Qedar , qa Adbel , qa Mibšam ;
01025014	Qa Mišma , qa Duma , qa Masa ;
01025015	Hada , qa Teman , Jetur , Napiš qa Qedma .
01025016	Hena Išmayel cinkši wicaya ; toki tipi qa tonwanyanpi kin ecen eciyapi , wicaštayatapi ihdawapi ake nom , taoyatepi kin om .
01025017	Išmayel ni un kin waniyetu kin dena ee , waniyetu opawinge sanpa wikcemna yamni sanpa šakowin , henakeca ; hehan niya šni ta iyaye ca taoyate kin ekta okipa yapi .
01025018	Hunka wanjin wicaye cin owasin wicehna ta . Hawila etanhan šur itokam un kin ektakiya de cin qa hetanhan Ašur etu makoce kin he en ounyanpi .
01025019	Unkan Izak Abereyam cinhintku wicoicage tawa kin dee , Abereyam he Izak kicitonpi .
01025020	Unkan Izak wanna waniyetu wikcemna topa , hehan Rebeka yuza , he Betuel Arami kin he cunwintku , Aram Mdaye kin etanhan , Laban Arami kin tawinoĥtin kin hee tawicu kta e yuza .
01025021	Qa Izak tawicu kin cinca ton šni kin heon , Jehowa anakicigoptan , hecen Rebeka Izak tawicu kin ihdušaka .
01025022	Unkan hokšiyoqopa Rebeka mahen akinicapi ; unkan , De taku hwo hecetu kta hecinhan token on hemaca he ? eye ca Jehowa iwange kta e ekta i .
01025023	Unkan , Nitamni kin mahen oyate nonpa , qa nitezi kin etanhan oyate nonpa inanpapi kta , qa oyate wan wašaka keš oyate uman sanpa wašake kta , qa hakakta kin he tokapa kin wowidake yuhe kta ce , Jehowa eciya .
01025024	Unkan anpetu cinca ton kte cin wanna henakeca , qa inyun tamni kin mahen cekpa yukan .
01025025	Unkan tokapa kin hiyu owancaya gi , pte ha šina iyecen ; unkan Esa eya caštonpi .
01025026	Hehan sunkaku kin hiyu , qa nape kin Esa siyete kin yus un ; heon Jakob eya caš kiton Hena tonpi kin ehan , Izak waniyetu wikcemna šakpe .
01025027	Unkan hokšipidan tanka icagapi , qa Esa wotihni wayupika , wicašta ĥewoskan un kin heca , tuka Jakob wicašta waĥbadan wakeya oti .
01025028	Unkan Izak Esa wašta kidaka , taku o kin yuta heon . Tuka Rebeka Jakob wašte kidaka .
01025029	Unkan Jakob wahanpi ohe cin icunhan Esa tinta kin etanhan u qa watuka un ;
01025030	Qa , Akiĥan mate kta heon wahanpi ša kin de onge maqu wo , mdatke kta ce , Esa Jakob eciya . Heon Edom eya caje yatapi .
01025031	Unkan , Watonikapa kin he nakaha maqu wo , Jakob eya .
01025032	Unkan Esa , Wanna mate kta qa watomakapa kin de taku okihi kta he ? eya .
01025033	Unkan Jakob , Nakaha Wakantanka icajeyan emakiye wo , eya . Unkan Wakantanka icajeyan eciya . Hecen Esa watokapa tawa kin he Jakob qu .
01025034	Unkan Jakob omnica hanpi aguyapi kici Esa qu , unkan yute ca yatkan qa najin , qa toki iyaya . Hecen Esa watokapa kin ihakta šni .
01026001	Unkan makoce kin he en wicaakiĥan tokeca wan , Abereyam anpetu tawa icunhan wicaakiĥan tokaheya qon he iyohakam . Unkan Izak Pilištim tawicašta yatapi Abimelek eciyapi ekta i , Gerar etu .
01026002	Unkan Jehowa iye en tanin iciye ca heciya , Egupta ekta de kte šni ce , makoce wan ociciyake kte cin hen yanka wo .
01026003	Makoce kin de en ounyan wo , kinhan nici waun qa ciyawašte , qa makoce kin dena owasin cicu kta , nicinca ko wokonze Abereyam niyate konza ewakiye cin he wahdusuta ;
01026004	Qa nicinca yuota wakiye kta maĥpiya wicanhpi sukaza iyenaka , qa makoce kin dena owasin nicinca wicawaqu kta , qa oyate maka kin ohnaka owasin nicinca kin on yawaštepi kta .
01026005	Nakaeš Abereyam miho kin anamagoptan qa mitawoahope , mitawokonze , mioie , qa mitoope kin hena yuhe cin heon etanhan .
01026006	Unkan Izak Gerar en ounyan .
01026007	Unkan wicašta heciya tipi kin tawicu kin on iwangapi ; unkan , Mitankši kin dee ce eya . Rebeka owanyag wašte , qa iye on okini wicašta deciya yakonpi kin maktepi kta ecin heon , Mitawin dee eye kte cin itonpa .
01026008	Unkan wanna anpetu ota hen yanke cehan , Pilištim wicašta yatapi Abimelek ojanjan hdepi wan etanhan eyokasin qa Izak tawicu Rebeka kici škata e wanwicayaka .
01026009	Hehan Abimelek Izak kico qa , Awicakehan nitawin hee . Tokeca , Mitawinoĥtin dee ehe ciqon he ? eya . Unkan okini iye on mate kta epce cin heon hepa ce , Izak eya .
01026010	Unkan , De taku ecaunyeconpi he ? Wanna ecadan oyate etanhan wicašta wan nitawin kici iwanke kta unkanš , taku šica iyahde unyayapi kta tuka ce , Abimelek eya .
01026011	Qa Abimelek oyate tawa owasin iwakta wicaya , Tuwe wicašta kin de yutan , qa iš tawicu yutan kinhan te kta ce , eya .
01026012	Unkan , Izak makoce kin he en woju , qa omaka kin he en opawinge akihde kamna . Hecen Jehowa Izak yawašte .
01026013	Unkan wicašta kin tanka qa ohinniyan tanka aya , wijica ĥinca .
01026014	Qa ocihde , taĥinca , qa pte wanuyanpi , qa ookiye ota yuha ; heon Pilištim icekinpi .
01026015	Unkan miniĥdoka , tona atkuku taokiye qapi qon atkuku Abereyam ni qehan , hena owasin Pilištim aohduteyapi , maka okatapi .
01026016	Unkan Abimelek Izak heciya , Unkiyepi etanhan toki iyaya wo , waunšakapi keš niš sam iyeya wanišaka ce .
01026017	Unkan Izak hetanhan iyaye ca Gerar kaksiza kin he en eti , qa hen iyotanka .
01026018	Qa miniĥdoka atkuku Abereyam ni kin icunhan qapi qon , qa Abereyam te cin iyohakam Pilištim kin hena aohduteyapi kin , hena ake Izak qe ca Abereyam caš ton qon hena iyecen Izak caje yata .
01026019	Qa Izak hokšidan wicayuhe cin kaksiza ohna qapi qa , en minicaduza miniĥdoka wan iyeyapi .
01026020	Hehan Gerar wanuyanpi wihan wicakiyapi tawa kin , Izak wanuyanpi wihan wicakiyapi tawa kin om akinicapi qa , Mini kin he unkitawapi ce , eyapi ; heon miniĥdoka kin he Esek Izak caš ton , heciya kiyušepi kin heon .
01026021	Unkan ake miniĥdoka tokeca wan qapi ; unkan he on nakun akinicapi , heon he Sitna cašton .
01026022	Qa hetanhan ihdaka ye ca miniĥdoka tokeca wan qapi , qa he on akinicapi šni . Unkan he Rehobot eya caš kiton ; Wanna Jehowa tankaya unkiyukanpi kaga makoce kin en , heon unkicagapi kta ce , eya .
01026023	Unkan hetanhan itawankanhde ye ca Beršeba ekta i .
01026024	Unkan hanyetu kin he en Jehowa tanin iciye ca heciya , Niyate Abereyam taku wakanda kin he miye ce . Wikopešni un wo ; niyate Abereyam mitaokiye kin heon nici waun , qa ciya cašte , qa nicinca yuota wakiye kta ce .
01026025	Unkan kakiya wahna wošnapi wan kaga ca Jehowa caje kin hoye kiye ca , kakiya wakeya oti , qa kan Izak taokiye kin miniĥdoka wan qapi .
01026026	Hehan Abimelek Gerar etanhan Izak en hi ; iye takodaku Ahuzat , Pikol taakicita tancan koya .
01026027	Unkan šice mayadakapi qa niyepi kin etanhan toki iyaye mayašipi , qa tokeca en mayahipi he ? Izak ewicakiya .
01026028	Unkan , Unkanitonwanpi qa Jehowa nici un kin he wanunyakapi qa , Iho wokonze yuke kte , unkiyotahedan qa odakonkiciyapi unnicagapi kta ce , unkeyapi .
01026029	Hecen unkiš unniyutanpi šni , qa taku wašte ecedan ecaunniconpi , qa wounkiyapi iyaye unnišipi kin he iyecen , niš dehan Jehowa niyawašte , taku šica ecaunyeconpi kte šni , eyapi .
01026030	Unkan wowicakihe ca wotapi qa wayatkanpi .
01026031	Qa ihanhanna kiktapi qa konza ekiciyapi , napin hunka wanjitku kici heconpi qa , Izak kihde wicaši . Unkan wookiye iyayapi .
01026032	Anpetu kin he en Izak taokiye kin en hipi , qa miniĥdoka qapi kin he okiyakapi qa , Mini iyohi unyanpi ce , eyapi .
01026033	Unkan , Konzapi eya caš kiton . Heon anpetu kin de hehanyan otonwe kin heciya un kin Beršeba eciyapi .
01026034	Unkan Esa wanna waniyetu wikcemna topa , hehan Beri ĥeti kin he cunwintku Judit , qa Elon ĥeti he cunwinktu Basmat , henios wicayuza . Hena napin on , Izak Rebeka ko cante šicapi .
