01027001	Unkan Izak wanna wicaĥinca išta kin mdeze šni , hecen wawanyake šni ; hehan Izak cinhintku tokapa kin Esa kipan qa , Micinkši , eya . Unkan , Iho miye ce , eya .
01027002	Unkan , Wanna wicamaĥinca , qa tohan mate kte cin sdonwakiye šni .
01027003	Ceciya ce , nakaha wipe ikikcu wo , wanju itazipa ko ikikcu , qa ĥewoskan ye ca tado imakihni wo .
01027004	Qa mate kte cin itokam , minagi kin niyawašte kta e , tado skumna taku wašte wadaka heca micage , ca makau wo . Wate kta ce , eya .
01027005	Unkan Rebeka Izak cinhintku Esa okiye cin he nahon . Unkan Esa atkuku kin on wotihni kta e ĥewoskan iyaya .
01027006	Hehan Rebeka cinhintku Jakob heciya Iho niyate Esa nicinye okiya nawaĥon ;
01027007	Qa , Tado makau qa taku skumna wašte micaga wo ; wate kta qa mate šni kin itokam Jehowa itokam ciyawašte kta ce , eciya .
01027008	Heon micinkši token econ ciši miho kin anamakigoptan ye .
01027009	Ecadan wanuyanpi ekta ye ca tatokadan cinca nom wašte imakicu ye , kinhan tado skumna wecage kta , niyate wašte daka iyececa .
01027010	Unkan niyate te cin itokam niyawašte kta e en ayai kta ; unkan yute kta ce .
01027011	Unkan , Jakob hunku kin Rebeka heciya ; Ecah micinye Esa wicašta hin šma heca , qa miš wicašta šdušduta hemaca .
01027012	Okini ate mayutan kte cinhan wicaĥnayesa wan iyececa iyemaye kta , hecinhan mayašicapi kin he iyahde ciciye kta , mayawaštepi kin hee kte šni ce .
01027013	Unkan , Micinkši niyašicapi kin he miye en amaupi nunwe . Tokešta miho kin anamakigoptan , qa imakicu ye , hunku kin eciya .
01027014	Unkan ekta ye ca ikikcu qa hunku kin au ; unkan hunku kin tado skumna atkuku wašte dake cin iyecen kaga .
01027015	Hehan Rebeka šina wašte wan , cinhintku tokapa Esa he tawa ti kin ohna yuhe cin he icu , qa cinhintku hakakta Jakob in kiya .
01027016	Qa tatokadan cincadan ha kin he Jakob nape kin , qa tahu šdušduta kin akan ehnaka .
01027017	Qa tado skumna kage ciqon aguyapi koya cinhintku Jakob nape kin en qu .
01027018	Unkan atkuku kin en au qa , Ate , eya . Unkan , Iho micinkši ni tuwe he ? eya .
01027019	Unkan Jakob atkuku kin heciya , Esa nicinkši tokapa kin he miye ce . Token emayakiye cin ecen ecamon ce . Ceciciya najin qa iyotanka wo ; qa ninagi kin mayawašte kta e tado awahi kin yuta wo , eya .
01027020	Unkan , Micinkši token inaĥniyan iyeyaya he ? Izak cinhintku kin eciya . Unkan Jehowa wakanyada kin he itkomakim u kiya heon etanhan , eya .
01027021	Unkan , Micinkši mikiyedan u wo , ciyutan kta ce , Esa micinkši kin de niye qa iš dee šni uman tukte sdonwaye kta , Izak Jakob eciya .
01027022	Hehan Jakob atkuku Izak ikiyedan hinajin , unkan yutan qehan , Ho kin Jakob ho kin hee , tuka nape kin Esa nape kin eepi , eya .
01027023	Nape kin hin šma cincu Esa nape kin iyececapi ; heon etanhan iyekiye šni , qa Jakob yawašte .
01027024	Esa micinkši kin de niye he ? eya iwanga . Unkan , Han he miye ce , eya .
01027025	Unkan , Mikiyedan u wo . Minagi kin niyawašte kta e , taku micinkši o kin wate kta ce , eya . Unkan ikiyedan hinajin , unkan wota , miniša nakun en au ; unkan yatkan .
01027026	Hehan atkuku Izak , Iho micinkši mikiyedan u qa i imaputaka wo , eciya .
01027027	Unkan en ye ca i iputaka , unkan wokoyake omna kin he omna , qa yawašte omna kin he iyececa .
01027028	Qa Wakantanka maĥpiya cu kin nicu kte ca nakun maka kin wasna qa aguyapi qa miniša ko ota .
01027029	Oyate wowindag wicayaye kta nitokam wicašta yatapi makata eĥpeiciyapi kta . Nihunka wanji yuha un wo , qa nihun cinca wicaye cin nitokam patujapi kta , tuwe niyawašte kin yawaštepi kta ce , eya .
01027030	Wanna Izak Jakob yawašte hdaštan , unkan Jakob atkuku Izak itoye kin etanhan kitana aisinyan iyaya , hehan cincu Esa wotihni kin etanhan hdi .
01027031	Qa iš nakun tado skumna kage ca atkuku kin en ahi , qa atkuku kin heciya , Ate najin qa nicinkši taku o kin etanhan yuta wo ; ninagi kin mayawašte kte cin heon etanhan .
01027032	Unkan atkuku Izak , Ni tuwe he ? eciya . Unkan , Nicinkši tokapa Esa he miye ce , eya .
01027033	Unkan Izak woyušinyaye tanka ĥinca on nina yušinyaya ; Token tuwe tado ihni qa makahi , unkan owasin etanhan wata , yahi šni ehan , qa mdawašte qa nakun iye yawaštepi kta ce , eya .
01027034	Esa atkuku oie kin nahon hehan nina ceye ca šicaĥowaye ca , Ate miš nakun mayawašte ye , atkuku kin eciya .
01027035	Unkan , Nisunka hi qa wohnaye kin eciya tanhan niyawaštepi kin icu , eya .
01027036	Unkan , Jakob eciyapi caje kin iyecetu šni he ? Wanna nonpa yušna mayan ; watomakapa kin he tokaheya kin qa nakaha mayawaštepi kin icu ; eyeca ; Woyawašte wan miyecipatan šni he , eya .
01027037	Unkan Izak ayupte ca , Ecah ohiniciye kte he wakage , ca hunka wanjin wicaye cin owasin wicayuhe kta waqu , aguyapi miniša ko yuhe kta waqu , qa dehan micinkši taku ecacicon kta he ? Esa eciya .
01027038	Unkan , Ate woyawašte kin wanjidan duha he ? Miš nakun mayawašte wo , ate , Esa atkuku kin eciye ca , Esa panyanhan ceya .
01027039	Unkan atkuku Izak ayupte ca , Maka wasna kin ohna ounyaye kte ca maĥpiya cu kin aniu kte ;
01027040	Qa nitacanhpi kin on yani kte ca nisunka wowidag niye kta ; tuka tohan wašaka inicage cinhan iye tawanapin nitahu kin etanhan dukse kta ce , eciya .
01027041	Unkan Esa Jakob šice kidaka , woyawašte kin on atkuku kin yawašte kin heon etanhan , qa Esa cane kin mahen heya ; Ate aceyapi kte cin anpetu kin hena wanna ikiyedan qa , hehan misunka Jakob wakte kta ce .
01027042	Unkan Rebeka he cinhintku tokapa token ie cin he okiyakapi , unkan ekta ye ši qa cinhintku hakakta Jakob kico qa , Iho nicinye Esa niye tokicon qa nikte kta e oiciya ce .
01027043	Iho micinkši miho kin anamakigoptan ye . Najin qa timdo Laban en Haran ektakiya najica ya ye .
01027044	Qa timdo kici nanke kta anpetu tonana ; nicinye canniye niye cin ayuštan kin hehanyan .
01027045	Nicinye wocanniye aniyuštan qa , taku ecayecon akiktonje cin hehantu , kinhan hetanhan icicu kta e wahociye kta ce . Ehaeš token on etanhan anpetu wanjidan en niye napin makitaninpi kte šni he ? eciya .
01027046	Unkan Rebeka Izak heciya , Wani kin he wanna owihanketa , ĥet cunwintku wicaye cin on etanhan , Jakob winoĥinca wan dena iyececa , ĥet cunwintku kin etanhan , yuze cinhan token on wani kta he , eya .
01028001	Hehan Izak Jakob kipan , qa yawašte qa wahokonkiye ca , Kanan cunwinkupi kin etanhan winoĥinca duze kte šni .
01028002	Najin Aram Mdaye kin ekta ya wo , nihun atkuku Betuel ti kin ekta , qa hetanhan timdoku Laban cunwintku kin etanhan winoĥinca wan yuza wo .
01028003	Qa Taku wakan iyotan wašake cin niyawašte , qa iyakicuya yuota niciye kta , qa oyate ota yaun kta .
01028004	Qa Abereyam yawaštepi kin nicu , makoce wan en ounyaye cin Wakantanka Abereyam qu qon he nicinca om yahduhe kta , eciya .
01028005	Hecen Izak Jakob ye ši ; unkan iyaya Aram Mdaye kin ekta , Betuel cinhintku Laban Arami kin en , Jakob Esa kici hunkupi kin Rebeka timdoku kin hee .
01028006	Unkan Izak Jakob yawašte , qa Aram Mdaye kin ekta ye ši kin , heciya tanhan winoĥinca wan yuze kta , qa yawašte qehan , Kanan cunwintkupi kin etanhan winoĥinca duze kte šni ce , eciye cin he Esa wanyaka .
01028007	Unkan Jakob atkuku hunku kici anawicagoptan , qa Aram Mdaye kin ektakiya ya .
01028008	Unkan Kanan cunwintkupi kin iye atkuku Izak išta kin en šicapi e Esa wanyake cehan ;
01028009	Esa Išmayel ekta i , qa Abereyam cinhintku Išmayel cunwintku Mahalat , Nebayot tawinoĥtin kin he yuza , tawicu nonpa tuka he nakun yuza .
01028010	Unkan Jakob Beršeba etanhan iyaya Haran ektakiya .
01028011	Qa toki i kin hen iwanka , wi wanna iyaya nakaeš , qa inyan hen yanke cin etanhan icu , qa ipahin ekihnake ca heciya ištima .
01028012	Qa wihanmde ca inyun taku iyadipi wan makata han , qa pa kin maĥpiya kin ekta iyohiya ; unkan Wakantanka ohnihde wicaye cin adipi qa kun hiyupi .
01028013	Qa inyun Jehowa iwankam najin , qa , Niyate Abereyam taku wakan da qa Izak taku wakan da kin Jehowa he miye ce . Makoce akan nunke cin he cicu kta nicinca koya .
01028014	Qa nicinca maka watušekšeca sukaza kin iyenakapi kta , eniciciya idade kta wiyoĥpeyata , qa wiyohiyanpata , qa waziyata , qa itokaga , qa niye nicinca koya en wicowazi tona maka akan unpi kin owasin yawaštepi kta .
01028015	Iho miš nici waun , qa toki da ešta awanciyake kta , qa makoce kin de ekta acihdi kta , eĥpeciye kte šni , tohan taku ociciyaka wahduštan šni kin hehanyan eya .
01028016	Unkan Jakob wihanmde cin etanhan kikta qa , Awicakehan Jehowa den yanka , tuka miš sdonwaye šni , eya .
01028017	Hecen kokipe ca , Oyanke kin de itonpapi kta tuka ce , Wakantanka ti kin qa maĥpiya tiyopa kin dee šni he ? eya .
01028018	Qa hanhanna hehan Jakob najin qa inyan wan ipahin ehnake ciqon he icu , qa wokiksuye kte cin ehde , qa he pa kin akan wihdi akaštan .
01028019	Qa oyanke kin he Betel , ( Taku Wakan ti kin ) eya cašton , tuka tokag ehan otonwe kin he Luz eciyapi .
01028020	Unkan Jakob wokonze wan iciconze ca heya , Wakantanka mici un kinhan , qa canku kin de ohna mde cin he ohna awanmayake cinhan , qa aguyapi wate kta maqu qa wokoyake komayake kta nakun ;
01028021	Qa ate ti kin ekta tanyan wahdi hecinhan Jehowa eceedan wakanwada kta ce .
01028022	Qa inyan wokiksuye ewehde kin de Wakantanka tipi tawa kta ce , qa taku mayaqu kte cin owasin etanhan , iwikcemna kin cicu kta ce .
01029001	Hehan Jakob Wiyohiyanpata cinca tamakocepi kin ektakiya siha on mani iyaya .
01029002	Qa etonwe ca inyun tinta ohna miniĥdoka wan , qa taĥin wanuyanpi optaye yamni heciya miniĥdoka kin icaĥda wankapi , miniĥdoka kin he etanhan optaye kin mini wicaqupi ece . Unkan miniĥdoka i kin akan inyan tanka wan yanka .
01029003	Unkan hen optaye kin owasin mniciyapi eca , miniĥdoka i kin akan tanhan inyan kin yuptanyanpi qa ; taĥinca kin mini wicaqupi ca inyan kin hen yanke kte cin miniĥdoka i kin akan ehnakapi .
01029004	Unkan , Hunka wanjin ciyapi tokiya tanhan yaunpi he ? Jakob ewicakiya . Unkan , Haran unketanhanpi ce , eyapi .
01029005	Unkan , Laban Naĥor cinhintku sdonyayapi he ? ewicakiya . Unkan , Han he sdonunyanpi ce , eyapi .
01029006	Unkan , Zaniyan un he ? ewicakiya . Unkan , Zaniyan un , nakun wanyaka wo ; cunwintku Raĥel taĥin wanuyanpi kin om hiyu ce , eyapi .
01029007	Unkan , Anpetu nahaĥin tanka ihan . Wanuyanpi mniciyapi kte cin nahaĥin iyehantu šni . Taĥinca mini wicaqupi qa wihan wicakiyapo , eya .
01029008	Unkan , Unkokitpanipi ce ; optaye kin owasin mniciyapi kin , hehan inyan kin miniĥdoka i kin etanhan yuptanyanpi kinhan , hehan taĥinca kin mini wicunqupi kta ce , eyapi .
01029009	Om wohdaka icunhan , Raĥel atkuku taĥinca tawa om hi ; wihan wicakiya nakaeš .
01029010	Hecetu unkan Jakob , iye hunku kin he timdoku Laban cunwintku Raĥel he wanyake ca , hunku timdoku kin Laban taĥinca tawa nakun , qa Jakob ikiyedan i qa , inyan qon miniĥdoka i kin akan tanhan yuptanye ca , hunku kin he timdoku Laban taĥinca tawa mini wi
01029011	Qa Jakob Raĥel i iputake ca ho taninyan ceya .
01029012	Qa Jakob Raĥel heciya , Niyate sunkaku kin hemaca , Rebeka cinhintku kin he miye ce . Unkan inyan hde ca atkuku okiyaka .
01029013	Unkan Laban he tawinoĥtin cinhintku kin Jakob taku ohdake cin Nahon qehan , itkokim inyang ye ca , poskin yuze ca , i iputake ca ti kin timahen u ši . Unkan Jakob Laban hena taku kin owasin okiyaka .
01029014	Unkan , Mihu , qa miceĥpi kin he niye ce , Laban Jakob eciya . Unkan anpetu tona wi wanjidan en un kin kici yank .
01029015	Unkan Laban Jakob heciya , Hunka wanjin ciye cin on ituya wowidag ciye kta he ? Taku iyuwin yacin kin he omakiyaka wo , eya .
01029016	Wanna Laban cunwintku nonpa , tokapa kin Leha eciyapi , qa hakakta kin Raĥel eciyapi .
01029017	Qa Leha išta kin wankadan ; tuka Raĥel okaĥ wašte owanyag wašte ĥinca .
01029018	Unkan Jakob Raĥel wašte dake ca , Raĥel nicunkši hakakta kin he on waniyetu šakowin wowidag mayaye kta , eya .
01029019	Unkan he cicu hinhan wašte kta ; wicašta tokeca waqu kinhan wašte kte šni . Mici ti wo , Laban eya .
01029020	Unkan Jakob Raĥel on waniyetu šakowin okiya ; tuka he wašte dake cin on išta kin en anpetu tonana yawa .
01029021	Hehan , Mitawin maqu wo , kici imunke kta , anpetu kin wanna henakeca ce , Jakob Laban eciya .
01029022	Unkan Laban otonwe kin wicašta owasin mnawicaye ca wowicakihan .
01029023	Qa otpaza hehan cunwintku Leha he icu , qa Jakob en au . Unkan kici wanka .
01029024	Unkan Laban wikoška wan yuhe cin Zilpa , he icu qa cunwintku Leha wikoška yuhe kta e qu .
01029025	Ihanhanna inyun Leha hee , qa Jakob Laban heciya , Raĥel on ociciye šni he ? Tokeca mayahnayan he ?
01029026	Unkan , Hakakta kin tokaheya qupi , qa hehan tokapa kin deciya hecen econpi šni ;
01029027	Anpetu šakowin kin de ihuniyan wo ; kinhan he nakun cicu kta , tokata waniyetu šakowin tokeca omayakiye kta cin heon etanhan , Laban eya .
01029028	Unkan Jakob ecen econ , qa šakowin kin he ihuniyan . Unkan Laban cunwintku Raĥel he tawicu kta e qu .
01029029	Qa wikoška wan yuhe cin Bilha , he Laban cunwintku Raĥel wikoška yuhe kta e qu .
01029030	Unkan Jakob Raĥel kici wanke ca , nakun Raĥel wašte dake ca ake waniyetu šakowin uman Laban cajeyate ciqon he yuštan .
01029031	Unkan Leha šice dakapi kin he Jehowa wanyake ca , Leha tamni kin yuĥdoka , tuka Raĥel cinca ton šni .
01029032	Unkan Leha Ihdušake ca , cinca ton , qa Ruben eya caš kiton ; Makiyušepi kin Jehowa wanyake , unkan dehan mihihna wašte madake kta ce , eya .
01029033	Qa ake ihdušake ca cinca ton , qa , šice madapike cin he Jehowa naĥon , qa cinca kin de nakun maqu , eye ca , šimeyon eya caš kiton .
01029034	Qa ake ihdušake ca cinca ton qa , Wanna detanhan mihihna tinsa mahduze kta : Wanna cinca yamni weciton , eye , ca Lewi eya caš kiton .
01029035	Unkan ake ihdušake ca cinca ton qa , Dehan Jehowa mdatan kta ce , eye caš kiton . Hehan cinca ton kin ayuštan .
01030001	Unkan Raĥel Jakob cinca kiciton šni e wanhdake ca , Raĥel he cunku inakiwizi qa Jakob heciya , Cinca maqu ye , Hecanon šni kinhan mate kta ce .
01030002	Unkan Jakob canniye ye ca , Raĥel heciya , Miye Wakanmatanka kecanni he ? Iye taku tamni ton kin onanitaka ce .
01030003	Unkan , Iho wikoška mduhe cin Bilha he ekta ya ye ; unkan mišiyoto kin akan cinca ton kinhan , iye etanhan cinca waton kta ce ;
01030004	Eye ca wikoška yuhe cin Bilha he tawicu kta e qu . Unkan Jakob he en i .
01030005	Unkan Bilha ihdušake ca Jakob cinca kiciton .
01030006	Unkan Wakantanka mayaco qa , nakun houwaye cin namaĥon , qa cinca wan maqu , Raĥel eye ca , Dan eya caš ton .
01030007	Unkan ake Raĥel tawikoška Bilha ihdušake ca cinca icinonpa Jakob kiciton .
01030008	Unkan Wakantanka omakiye ca micun kici ĥtawani , qa ohiwaya ce , Raĥel eye ca Neptali eya caš ton .
01030009	Unkan Leha cinca sanpa ton šni e wanhdake cehan wikoška yuhe cin Zilpa icu , qa Jakob tawicu kta e qu .
01030010	Unkan Leha wikoška yuhe cin Zilpa , he Jakob cinca kiciton .
01030011	Unkan , Wicota kta , Leha eye ca , Gad eya caš ton .
01030012	Unkan Leha wikoška yuhe cin Zilpa Jakob cinca icinonpa kiciton .
01030013	Unkan , Wopida mayanpi , cunwintku unpi kin mayawaštepi kta ce , Leha eye ca Ašer eya caš ton .
01030014	Unkan aguyapi baksapi kin icunhan Ruben magata iyaye ca , dudaim iyeye ca hena hunku kin ekta kai . Unkan Raĥel Leha heciya ; Nicinkši dudaim au kin etanhan maqu ye .
01030015	Unkan , Mihihna yaki kin he taku cistina naceca , micinkši dudaim tawa kin , he nakun iyacu kta he ? eciya . Unkan , Nicinkši dudaim tawa kin he on hanyetu kin de nici iwanke kta ce , eya .
01030016	Unkan ĥtayetu hehan , Jakob maga tanhan hdi ; unkan Leha itkokim inanpe ca , Miyahna yau kta , micinkši dudaim tawa kin hena on opeciton ce , eya . Unkan hanyetu kin he kici wanka .
01030017	Unkan Wakantanka Leha anagoptan : unkan ihdušake ca cinca izaptan Jakob kiciton .
01030018	Qa , Wikokša mduhe cin he mihihna waqu kin heon , Wakantanka iyunwin maqu , Leha eye ca , Isakar eya caš kiton .
01030019	Unkan ake Leha ihduške ca cinca išakpe Jakob kiciton .
01030020	Qa , Nakaha Wakantanka taku wašte itumakiĥan , nihihna cinca šakpe weciton , heon detanhan mici ti kta ce , eye ca , Zebulon eya caš kiton .
01030021	Qa he iyohakam cinca winyan ton qa , Dina eya caš kiton .
01030022	Unkan Wakantanka Raĥel kiksuye ca Wakantanka anakicigoptan , qa tamni kin yuĥdoka .
01030023	Unkan ihdušake ca cinca wan ton qa , Taku iyamaonpapi qon Wakantanka wanna emicihdaku ;
01030024	Qa Wakantanka cinca tokeca wan nakun maqu kta , eye ca , Josep eya caš kiton .
01030025	Unkan Raĥel Josep ton kin hehan , Jakob Laban heciya , Wanna hde mayan wo . Mitamakoce qa toki manke kte cin ekta wahde kta .
01030026	Mitawin micinca ko maqu wo , wahde kta ce ; hena on taken ĥtawani , qa wowindag mayaye cin niš sdonyaya ce .
01030027	Unkan , Tokin niišta kin en iyocicipin , niye on etanhan Jehowa mayawašte wahdukcan .
01030028	Taku on omayakiye kta atayedan omakiyaka wo ; hecece cinhan cicu kta ce , Laban eciya .
01030029	Unkan , Niš token ociciye ca , nitawanuyanpi kin token mici unpi qon sdonyaya .
01030030	Wahi kin itokam taku cistina duhe ciqon , qa wanna ota aye ca , misiha kin eciya tanhan Jehowa niyawašte . Unkan wanna tohan wati ohnaka kin on taku micicage kta he ? eya .
01030031	Unkan , Taku cicu kta he ? eya . Unkan Jakob heciya , Takudan mayaqu kte šni , tuka taku kin de ecanon kinhan ake taĥinca nitawa kin awanwicamdake kta .
01030032	Nakaha wanuyanpi owasin ehna mawani kta , qa tona hdehdega qa hdehdeze cin iyog iyewicawaye kta , taĥinca wanuyanpi kin tona gigi kin owasin , qa tatokadan tona hdehdege ca hdehdeze cin heniyos akipam ewicawahde kta ; qa tokata taĥin wanuyanpi ehna ton
01030033	Unkan tokata mioĥan owotanna mihduotanin kta ; taku mitawa nitokam u kinhan , tatokadan tona hdedegapi šni , qa hdehdezapi šni , qa taĥin wanuyanpi ehna tona gigi šni kin hena owasin mawanon kehe kta .
01030034	Unkan , Tokin token ehe cin hecetun , Laban eya .
01030035	Qa anpetu kin he en tatokadan mdoka tona hdehdeza hdehdega ko , qa tatokadan wiye tona hdehdege ca hdeškaška kin owasin , tona akan hin san kin hena koya owasin , akipam ewicahdaku , taĥin wanuyanpi ehna tona gigi kin nakun owasin , qa hena cinkši wica
01030036	Qa anpetu yamni imani , iye Jakob kici ihehanyan kaga . Unkan Laban woteca optaye ihe cin hena Jakob wiĥan wicakiya .
01030037	Qa Jakob can sakadan icu , waga teca qa can su , qa uma hena owasin etanhan icu , qa ha kin pago hdeza , ska tanin kta e hecen hdehdeza kaga .
01030038	Qa watpadan tukten wanuyanpi mini yatkanpi kin hena ohna , can sakadan pago qon ehde , wanuyanpi itokapa tanhan , unkan wanuyanpi yatke upi en kiyuĥapi ece .
01030039	Hecen can sakadan qon ekta wanuyanpi kin kiyuĥapi , qa wanuyanpi hdehdeza hdehdega hdeškaška ko wicatonpi .
01030040	Unkan Jakob tacincadan yukinukan ewicahnake ca wanuyanpi itepi kin taku hdeza ektakiya ewicahde , Laban wanuyanpi gigi kin owasin , qa wanuyanpi tawa kin yukinukan ewicahde , Laban tawanuyanpi kin kici ewicahde šni .
01030041	Qa tohan wanuyanpi wašakapi kiyuĥapi eca , Jakob can sakadan qon watpadan ohna wanuyanpi išta kin wicitokam ehde ; can sakadan kin ekta kiyuĥapi kta e hecon .
01030042	Tuka wanuyanpi wankapidan eca , ehde šni , hecen tona wankapi kin hena Laban tawa , qa tona wašakapi kin hena Jakob tawa .
01030043	Hecen wicašta kin tanka ĥinca icage ca wanuyanpi ota ton , qa nakun winyan taokiye qa hokšidan , qa camo , qa šuktanka šonšonna .
01031001	Hehan , Taku ate unyanpi tawa qon he owasin Jakob icu , qa taku ate yuhe ciqon etanhan , woyuha tanka kin de owasin icicaga , Laban cinkši wicaye cin eyapi kin Jakob naĥon .
01031002	Qa Laban ite kin he nakun Jakob wanyaka , qa iye ektakiya wanna tokeca .
01031003	Nakun , Niyate makoce tawapi kin ekta , qa takuwicayaye cin ekta hda wo , kinhan nici waun kta ce , Jehowa Jakob eciya .
01031004	Heon Jakob tuwe ekta ye ši qa , tawicu napin Raĥel Leba kici , tinta kin heciya , tawanuyanpi kin ekta wicakico .
01031005	Qa , Niyatepi kin wanna tokeca amatonwe cin wanmdaka , tuka ate taku wakan da kin mici un .
01031006	Qa token owakihi ohinniyan niyatepi kin owakiya sdonyayapi ;
01031007	Tuka niyatepi kin mahnaye ca , wikcemna akihde taku maqu kte cin yutokeca , tuka kiunni maye kte cin Wakantanka iyowinye šni .
01031008	Kaken , Hdehdegapi kin hena iyunwin duhe kta ce , eye cehan , waunyanpi kin owasin hdehdegapi kin heca ece wicatonpi ; qa , Hdehdezapi kin hena iyunwin nitawa kta eye cehan , hehan wanuyanpi owasin hdehdezapi heca ece wicatonpi ece .
01031009	Hecen Wakantanka niyatepi tawanuyanpi kin ki ece , qa he maqu .
01031010	Wanuyanpi kin kiyuĥapi eca wiwahanmde ca , ewatonwe ca , inyun tamdoka hdehdeza hdehdega hdeškaška hecapi ko , wanuyanpi akan adipi e išta on wanmdaka .
01031011	Nakaun wiwahanmde ca , Wakantanka taohnihde ye cin hemakiya ; Jakob . Unkan , Iho miye ce , epa .
01031012	Unkan , Išta yuwankan ikikcu qa , tamdoka wanuyanpi adipi kin awicatonwan wo ; hdehdeza hdehdega hdeškaška hecapi ; token Laban ecanicon kin he owasin wanmdaka ce .
01031013	Taku wakan Betel en tanin iciye cin he miye , hen wokiksuye sdayaye ca , hen taku konza emayakiya . Wanna najin , qa makoce kin de etanhan , iyaye ca taku wicayaye cin ekta hda wo , eya .
01031014	Unkan Raĥel Leha ko ayuptapi ; ate ti kin ohna taku unhapi kte ca taku unkitawapi kte cin yukan he ?
01031015	Oyate tokeca unhdawapi šni he ? Wiyopeunyanpi , qa nakun mazaska unkitawapi kin owasin yusota .
01031016	Heon woyuha ate unyanpi kin etanhan Wakantanka ki kin he iyuĥpa unkiye unkitawapi , qa unkicincapi tawapi ce . Iho wanna token Wakantanka econ niši kin owasin ecen econ ye , eyapi .
01031017	Unkan Jakob najin , qa cinca tawicu ko owasin camo akan ewicahnaka ,
01031018	Qa atkuku Izak en Kanan makoce kin ekta kihde kta e tawanuyanpi kin owasin awicaya , woyuha icicage cin , qa taku tonpi kiton kin , taku Aram Mdaye kin en ihdamna kin owasin .
01031019	Wanna , Laban taĥinca kin hdušda iyaye cehan , Raĥel he atkuku terapim tawa kin manon .
01031020	Unkan Jakob Laban Arami kin cante kin manon najica iyaya , okiyake šni nakaeš .
01031021	Hecen najica , taku tawa kin owasin hduha najin , qa watpa kin iyuwege ca , Gilead ĥe kin ektakiya etonwan .
01031022	Unkan anpetu iyamni kin hehan , Jakob wanna najica Laban okiyakapi .
01031023	Unkan hunka wanjin wicaye cin wicakico , hena om okide ye ca , šakowin can icimanipi hehan , Gilead ĥe kin en kihdegapi .
01031024	Unkan , Wakantanka hanyen Laban Arami kin en hi qa , wihanmde cin en heciya , Ihnuhan taku wašte taku šica uman tukte kašta eyakiye cin , eya .
01031025	Unkan Laban Jakob kihdege cehan , Jakob ĥe kin en wakeya oti , qa Laban hunka wanjin wicaye cin om Gilead ĥe kin hiyahanpi .
01031026	Qa Laban Jakob heciya , Taku tokanon micante kin mayahnaye ca , micunkši canĥpi on wayaka iyecen awicayahda .
01031027	He tokeca e hecanon he ? Anamayakiĥbe ca , manicinon , omayakidake šni . Omayakidaka unkanš wiyuškinyan iyaye ciye ca , cicidowan , qa cancega candowankiyapi ko ciciyahoton kta tuka hecanon .
01031028	Micinca wica winyan ko i iwicawaputake kte , iyowin mayakiye šni . Wanna witkoya hecanon .
01031029	Dehan taku šica ecacicon kta nape wamašaka , tuka niyate taku wakan da kin hinhan hemakiya ; Ihnuhan Jakob taku wašte taku šica unman tukte kašta eyakiye cin , eya .
01031030	Wanna niyate ti kin ekta yahde kte ĥinca , tuka tokeca Taku wakan mitawa kin mayanon he ? eya .
01031031	Unkan Jakob waayupte ca , Kowakipe cin heon , qa okini nicunkši kin hena mayaki kta naceca ce epe cin heon hecamon ;
01031032	Taku wakan nitawa kin tuwe kici iyeyakiye cinhan , he ni kte šni . Hunka wanji unye cin wicitokam , taku nitawa mici un kin , tukte e he , iyukcan qa ikikcu wo . Raĥel hena manon tuka Jakob he sdonye šni , qa heciya .
01031033	Hehan Laban Jakob tawakeya kin en ti mahen i , Leha tawakeya kin nakun , qa wikoška nonpa tawakeyapi kin ; tuka iyekiye šni ; hehan Laban Leha tawakeya kin etanhan hdinanpe ca , Raĥel tawakeyapi kin ; tuka iyekiye šni ; hehan Laban Leha tawakeya kin etanh
01031034	Tuka Raĥel terapim kin icu , qa camo aqinpi kin en ehnake ciqon , qa akan iyotanka . Unkan Laban wakeya kin owancaya yutan qa iyekiye šni .
01031035	Unkan atkuku kin heciya , Itancan nitokam nawajin owakitpani , hececa šta canniye maye šni ye . Winoĥinca ayakonpi kin hemaceca ce . Unkan nina akita tuka terapim kin iyekiye šni .
01031036	Unkan Jakob canniye ca , Laban kige , Taku šica ecamon qa wawaĥtani kin tukte e he , on hecen mayakuwa ?
01031037	Mitawaĥpaya kin owasin mayakidutan , wakšica yati kin etanhan wanji iyeyaye cin tukte e he ? takuwicunye cin wicitokam ehnaka wo ; hecece cinhan uman tukte unkitawa kta yukcanpi nunwe .
01031038	Waniyetu wikcemna nonpa kin dena nici waun , tuka tawiyedan nitawa kin kpapi šni , qa , nitawanuyanpi tamdoka kin hena wate šni .
01031039	Taku yaĥdecapi kin niye en cicai šni , he miye piya wakaga ce . Hanyen manonpi kin , qa anposkan manonpi kin he koya , minape kin etanhan mayakida .
01031040	Kaken waun , anposkan ipuza mata , qa hanyen osni ; woištima miišta kin amayuštan .
01031041	Miye waniyeta wikcemna nonpa kin yati kin en wowidag mayeye ; waniyetu ake topa nicunkši nonpa on , qa waniyetu šakpe nitawanuyanpi kin on , ociciye ca , taku mayaqu kte cin wikcemna akihde mayadutokan .
01031042	Ate taku wakan da kin , Abereyam taku wakan da kin qa Izak Tokokipe kin , mici un kin ; hecetu šni unkanš wanna cokadan kihde mayaši kta tuka ; mawaĥbadan kin qa minape ĥtanipi kin he Wakantanka wanyake ca , hinhan iyopeniyan ce , Jakob Laban eciya .
01031043	Unkan Laban Waayupte ca , Jakob heciya , Cinca winyan kin dena micunkši eepi , qa hokšidan kin dena micinca eepi , qa wanuyanpi kin dena wanuyanpi mitawa eepi , qa taku niye wanyahdake cin he iyuĥpa mitawa ce . Tuka de micunkši qa iš cinca wicatonpi kin
01031044	Tokin wanna wicoun unkicagen , miye qa niye , hecen waayatanin unkiyotahedan yuke kta .
01031045	Unkan Jakob inyan wan icu , qa wokiksuye e pasdata :
01031046	Qa , Inyan icupo , Jakob hunka wanjin wicaye cin ewicakiya . Unkan inyan icupi , qa paha wan kagapi qa , hen paha kin akan wotapi .
01031047	Unkan paha kin he , Igar sahaduta Laban eya cašton ; tuka Jakob he Galed eya cašton .
01031048	Unkan Laban heya , Anpe dehan paha kin de unkiyotahedan waayatanin kta ; Galed Waayatanin paha kin he ka , paha kin he eciyapi .
01031049	Qa , Micunkši wicayakiduše , qa winoĥinca tokeca duze cinhan , wicašta tuwe he atonwe kta unkici un šni , unkiyotahedan Wakantanka he waayatanin kta .
01031050	Tohan kinukankiya unkiyaye cinhan Jehowa unyacopi kta , Laban eye ca , Wayaco caš ton .
01031051	Qa , Wanyaka wo , paha kin de , wokiksuye unkiyotahedan ewehde kin de ;
01031052	Paha kin waayatanin , wokiksuye kin de waayatanin , taku šica on paha kin de kapeya imdamde ca niye en cii kte šni , qa niš kapeya yahihdu qa hiyohi mayaye kte šni .
01031053	Abereyam taku wakan da kin , Naĥor taku wakan da kin , hunkake wicayapi taku wakan dapi kin unyacopi kta , Laban Jakob eciya . Unkan Jakob iye atkuku Izak Tokokipe kin cajeyan konza .
01031054	Hehan Jakob ĥe kin akan wošnapi wan wakiyušna , qa aguyapi yutapi kta e hunka wanjin wicaye cin wicakico . Unkan aguyapi yutapi qa ĥe kin en wankapi .
01031055	Unkan ihanĥanna Laban kikta qa iye cinca wica winyan ko i iwicaputake ca , wicayawašte qa , hehan Laban tohe kin ekta kihda .
01032001	Unkan Jakob tacanku kin ohna iyaye ca , Wakantanka ohnihde wicaye cin iktokim hipi .
01032002	Unkan Jakob wanwicayake cehan , Wakantanka wicobe tawa kin dee ce , eye ca oyanke kin he Maĥanaim caš ton .
01032003	Hehan Jakob Edom wojupi kin Sehir makoce kin etu , cincu Esa ti kin ekta , ohnihde wicaye cin ye wicaši .
01032004	Qa wahokonwicakiye ca , Itancan mitawa Esa hecen eyakiyapi kta ce , eya ; Laban kici wati qon dehantu .
01032005	Qa pte , qa šuktanka šonšonna , qa taĥinca , qa hokšidan wikoška ko , ota wicamduha , qa onšimayada kda e itancan ociciyag ye wicawaši , nitaokiye Jakob eya .
01032006	Unkan Jakob ohnihde wicaye cin hdipi qa , Nicinye Esa ekta unkipi unkan iš nitkokim u qa , wicašta opawinge tom opapi ce , eyapi .
01032007	Hehan Jakob nina kokipe ca , oyate kici un kin nonpakiya ewicakihde , taĥinca , pte , camo , ko owasin ošpaye nonpa wicakaga .
01032008	Qa Esa ošpaye wanji en hi qa hena wicakte kinhan , ošpaye uman okapte cin inašdoke kta ce , eya .
01032009	Hehan Jakob heya , Abereyam ate waye wakan nida , qa ate Izak wakan nida Jehowa niye , Nitamakoce , qa takuwicayaye cin ekta hda wo , kinhan taku wašte ecacicon kta ce , emayakiye ciqon ;
01032010	Miye nitowaonšida qa iewicayake cin owasin nitaokiye ecayecon kin aopten waun ; sagye kin heceyedan hduha Jordan watpa kin de imduwege ca , wanna ošpaye nonpa imacaga .
01032011	Wanna cinye nape kin etanhan emahdaku wo ; Esa nape kin etanhan ; hi kinhan cinca hunkupi kin kici mikte kta kowakipa ce .
01032012	Niye , Ohinniyan taku wašte ecacicon kte ca , wiyaka mini wanca kahda sukaza utkana on yawapica šni , iyenaka nicinca wakage kta ehe ciqon , eya .
01032013	Unkan hanyetu kin he hen wanka , qa taku cincu Esa qu kte cin ikikcu , taku nape en hiyu ;
01032014	Takokadan wiye opawinge nonpa , qa mdoka wikcemna nonpa , taĥin wanuyanpi wiye opawinge nom mdoka wikcemna nonpa ahna ;
01032015	Camo azinkiyapi wikcemna yamni cincapidan om , pte wikcemna tom , qa tatanka wikcemna , šuktanka šonšonna wiye wikcemna nonpa cincadan wikcemna ahna .
01032016	Qa ookiye wicayuhe cin woteca otoiyohi kinnukan yuhe wicaši , qa , Optaye otoiyohi yukinukan awicahiyayapo , ewicakiya .
01032017	Qa tokaheya kin wahokonwicakiya , Tohan cinye itkonicipapi kinhan , qa , Tuwe tawa niyan he ? qa toki da qa taku nitokam un kin he tuwe tawa he ? eya iniwange cinhan :
01032018	Hehan , Nitaokiye Jakob dena tawa , tuka itancan mitawa Esa qu kta ; unkan iš nakun unkihektam u ce , ehapi kta ce , ewicakiya .
01032019	Unkan inonpa , qa iyamni , qa nakun owasin tona optaye ihakam yapi kin , Esa iyeyayapi kinhan oie kin hena iyecen eyakiyapi kta ce :
01032020	Nakun , Nitaokiye Jakob unkihektam u ce , ehapi kta ce , ewicakiya . Taku waqu kin mitokapa tanhan ye cin , hecen ite kin iyokipi waye kta , qa hehan ite kin iyowinmakiye kta ce , eya .
01032021	Unkan taku qu kin , he tokata iyokipta ; tuka iš hanyetu kin he taobe kin om wanka .
01032022	Qa hanyetu kin he en , najin qa tawicu nonpa kin iwicacu qa cinca wicaye cin ake wanji , qa Jabok oiyuwege kin en iyuwega .
01032023	Qa iwicakikcu , qa watpa kin iyuweĥ wicaye ca , taku tawa kin owasin iyuweĥ wicakiya .
01032024	Qa Jakob išnana hekta yanka , unkan wicašta wan anpao kin hehanyan kici kiihdušpa .
01032025	Qa wicašta kin tokadan ohiye šni e wanhdake cehan , cecunte okihe kin en yuza ; unkan kici kiihdušpapi kin icunhan , Jakob cecuntoštan kin papšon iyaye .
01032026	Unkan , Amayuštan wo ; wanna anpao hinanpa ce , eya . Unkan , Mayadawašte šni kinhan , aciyuštan kte šni ce , eya .
01032027	Qa , Token eniciyapi he ? eya . Unkan Jakob emakiyapi ce , eya .
01032028	Unkan , Nicaje Jakob eniciyapi kte šni . Detanhan Israel eniciyapi kta , Wakantanka wicašta ko , kici kinihdušpe ca niye ohiyaya ce , eciya .
01032029	Unkan , Tokin nicaje kin omayakidaken , Jakob eya iwanga . Unkan , Token on etanhan micaje kin inonga he ? eye ca hen yawašte .
01032030	Unkan , oyanke kin he , Ite wakan , Jakob eya caš ton . Taku Wakan ite icitkokim wanmdaka ešta minagi kin zaniyan un ce , eya .
01032031	Unkan Ite wakan iyokipte cehan , anpetu wi hinanpa , qa Jakob ceca kin on hušte .
01032032	Heon etanhan Israel cinca wicaye cin anpetu kin dehan ceca škotpa kin akan kan kiksuye šni qon he yutapi šni ; Jakob ceca škotpa kin akan kan kiksuye šni kin he oyutan kin heon etanhan .
01033001	Unkan Jakob wankan etonwe ca inyun , Esa u . wicašta opawinge tom kici wanwicayake ca , hokšiyoqopa kin akipam ewicakihde , Leha kici , qa Raĥel kici , qa wikoška nonpapi kin om .
01033002	Qa wikoška kin cinca wicayapi kin om tokaheya ye wicaši , qa hena ihektapa tanhan Leha cinca wicaye cin om , qa hena ihektapa tanhan Raĥel Josep kici .
01033003	Qa iye owasin wicitokam ye ca , cincu ikiyedan u kin icunhan šakowin akihde patuja .
01033004	Unkan , Esa itkokim inyanke ca , nape kin yuze ca tahu kin akan eĥpeiciye ca i iputaka , qa napin ceyapi .
01033005	Hehan Esa wankan etonwe ca , tawicu cinca wicaye cin ko wanwicayake ca , Dena token takuyaya he ? eya . Unkan , Wakantanka towaonšida kin on nitaokiye cinca qu kin dena eepi ce , eya .
01033006	Hehan wikoška kin cinca wicayapi kin om ikiyadan hipi , qa patujapi .
01033007	Hehan Leha cinca wicaye cin om ikiyadan hi qa patujapi ; qa ehake Josep Raĥel kici ikiyadan hipi , qa patujapi .
01033008	Unkan , Optaye kin dena owasin itkowicawakipe cin , token yaka he ? eya . Unkan , Mayuhe cin išta kin iyokipi ciye kta e heon .
01033009	Unkan , Misunka taku ota wahduha ce . Taku nitawa kin hduha un wo , Esa eya .
01033010	Unkan , Hiya niišta kin iyokipi ciye cinhan , minape kin etanhan taku waqu kin iyacu kta , nitohnake Wakantanka itohnake iyecen wanciyake ca iyocicipi kin heon etanhan .
01033011	Tokin taku ciyawašte kin en aniupi kin he iyacun . Wakantaka onšimada ece , qa taku owasin mduha , Jakob kitanyan eya ; unkan icu .
01033012	Qa heya , Ihdaka unye ca miye tokaheya mde kta ce .
01033013	Unkan , Hokšiyoqopa wankapidan e mayuhe cin sdonye ca , nakun taĥinca pte ko ihdušaka micicapi qa , anpetu wanjidan keš awicapapi kinhan , wanuyanpi owasin tapi kta .
01033014	Tokin itancan nitaokiye itokam yahden , qa miš wanuyanpi mitokam token manipi , qa hokšiyoqoqa kin token manipi kin , ecen iwahnanna mde kta , mayuhe cin ekta Sehir en wai kin hehanyan .
01033015	Unkan , Iho oyate mici unpi kin etanhan wanjikši nici eĥpewicawaye kta ce , Esa eya . Unkan tokeca e , mayuhe cin ešta kin iyocicipi hecinhan , eya .
01033016	Unkan anpetu kin he en , Esa tacanku kin ohna Sehir ektakiya kihda .
01033017	Tuka Jakob Sukot ekta unhdaka i qa , hen tipi icicage ca , taku tawa kin nakun ohanzi hdepi wicakicaga ; heon otonwe kin he Sukot eya cajeyatapi .
01033018	Qa Jakob Aram Mdaye kin etanhan u qehan , šekem otonwe tawa kin Kanan makoce kin etu zaniyan hi , qa otonwe kin itokam ticaga .
01033019	Qa makoce onšpa , tukten wakeya iticage cin , šekem atkuku ĥamor cinca wicaye cin napepi kin etanhan opewicakicaton , mazaska opawinge nom wicaqu .
01033020	Unkan hen wahna wošnapi wan kage ca , El Israel ta Wakantanka kin eya cašton .
01034001	Hehan Dina Leha he cunwintku Jakob kiciton kin , he makoce wicinyanpidan wanwicayake kta e toki iyaya .
01034002	Unkan wicašta yatapi ihdawa ĥamor ĥiwi kin he cinhintku šekem , he , wanyake ca icu qa kici wanka , hecen wieyaku .
01034003	Qa šekem nagi kin Dina Jakob cunwintku kin en nina iyaskape ca wikoška kin wašte dake ca , wikoška cantohnag ye cin ecen okiya .
01034004	Qa , Wicinyanna kin de miciyuza wo , šekem iye atkuku ĥamor eciya .
01034005	Unkan cunwintku yuašapapi kin he Jakob nakiĥon , tuka cinkši wicaye cin tinta ekta wanuyanpi om yakonpi , qa hdipi kin hehanyan Jakob inina yanka .
01034006	Unkan ĥamor šekem atkuku kin Jakob kici okiye kta e en i .
01034007	Unkan Jakob cinkšiwicaye cin tinta kin etanhan hdipi , qa he naĥonpi , qa iyokišicapi ; nina canniye yapi , Jakob cunwintku kin kici iwankapi : hecen econpi kte šni tuka , Israel witkoya ecakiconpi heon etanhan .
01034008	Unkan ĥamor hewicakiya , Micinkši šekem nagi kin nicunkšipi kin iyaskapa ; he tawicu kta e qupo .
01034009	Kinhan takuunkiciyapi kta ; nicunkšipi kin hena unqupo , qa niš cunkši wicunyanpi kin wicayuzapo .
01034010	Qa unkiyepi om dukanpi kta , makoce kin nitokam un kta ce , en unpo qa makoce kin en wopetonpi qa he yuhapo .
01034011	Qa šekem wikoška atkuku timdo wicaye cin ko hewicakiya ; Cantemakiyapo , kinhan token emayakiyapi kin ecen cicupi kta .
01034012	Wikoška kin mitawin un kta e mayaqupi kinhan , woĥpayapi iyakicuya tanka mayakidapi , taku qupi tanka ešta ; token emayakiyapi kin ecen cicupi kta .
01034013	Unkan Jakob cinkši wicaye cin tawinoĥtinpi kin Dina yušapapi qon kiksuyapi , qa heon šekem he atkuku ĥamor kici hnayeya awicayuptapi .
01034014	Qa , Taku hececa econpi unkokitpanipi . Wicašta wan ha iyotan kin baĥdayapi šni kin heca tankši unyanpi kin unqupi kinhan , he wišten unkiciyapi kta naceca .
01034015	Decehnana on unkaniyuptapi kta ; unkiš baunkiĥdayapi kin , niš nakun tona wica owasin henicecapi kinhan ;
01034016	Hehan cunkši wicunyanpi kin unnicupi kta , qa nicunkšipi kin wicunyuzapi kta , qa nicipi oununyanpi qa oyate unwanjipidan kta .
01034017	Tuka taku de en anaunyagoptanpi šni kinhan , baniciĥdayapi šni kinhan , cunkši unyanpi kin he unkikikcupi , qa toki unkiyayapi kta ce , ewicakiyapi .
01034018	Unkan , ĥamor šekem ĥamor cinhintku kici wicoie kin he wašte dakapi .
01034019	Qa koška kin Jakob cunwintku kin cantiheya , heon taku eyapi kin kohanna econ . Iye atkuku ti kin ohna yakonpi kin hena owasin iyakapeya kinihanpi .
01034020	Hehan ĥamor iye cinhintku šekem kici otonwe tawapi kin ekta kipi , qa otonwe tawapi kin ekta kipi , qa otonwe tawapi kin wicašta om wohdakapi , qa heyapi ,
01034021	Wicašta kin dena unkiyepi om wokiyapi , heon makoce kin en ounyanpi qa , hen iciyopeyapi kte . Ito makoce kin wicitokam tankaya un kinhan , cunwintkupi kin wicunyuzapi kta , qa cunkši wicunyanpi kin wicunqupi kta .
01034022	Tuka decehnana on wicašta kin wicadapi kta ; wiciye bakiĥdayapi kin he iyecen unkiye tona wica owasin baunkiĥdayapi kinhan ; unkiye om ounyanpi , qa oyate unwanjipidan kta .
01034023	Decehnana en anawicungoptanpi kinhan , unkiyepi om ounyanpi kta ; kinhan tawanuyanpi , qa taku yuhapi kin owasin , taku tonpi koya unkitawapi kte šni he ? eyapi .
01034024	Unkan wicašta tona otonwe tiyopa kin omanipi kin hena owasin , ĥamor iye cinhintku šekem kici anawicagoptanpi , qa bakiciĥdayapi , tona wica otonwe tiyopa kin omanipi kin owasin .
01034025	Unkan anpetu iciyamni kin yazanpi kin icunhan Jakob cinhintku kin nonpa , šimeyon Lewi kici Dina timdo wicaya , tacanĥpipi kin ikikcupi , qa kokipešniyan otonwe kin tatpe ipi , qa tona wica owasin wicaktepi .
01034026	ĥamor iye cinhintku šekem ko canĥpi hi kin on wicaktepi , qa Dina šekem ti kin etanhan ehdakupi qa hdohdapi .
01034027	Hehan Jakob cinkši wicaye cin wicakaĥugapi kin en ipi , qa , otonwe wan tankšitkupi kin yušapapi qon he ocowasin wicakipi ;
01034028	Taĥinca , qa tatanka , qa šuktanka šonšonna , taku otonwe kin ohna un , taku magata un kin ko owasin icupi .
01034029	Taku yuhapi qon owasin tašiceca tawicupi ahna nakun wayaka icupi , qa taku tipi kin ohna iyeyapi kin owasin icupi .
01034030	Hehan Jakob šimeyon Lewi kici hewicakiya , Iyoyag mayayapi , šicamna mayakagapi makoce wojutipi kin wicitokam , Kanani , qa Perazi kin , qa miye matonana hecen tamatpe mniciyapi , qa maktepi kta , hecen miš wati ohnaka ko owasin awimahnuni kta .

01035002	Unkan Jakob tiyoknaka tawa , qa tona kici unpi kin owasin hewicakiya ; Taku wakan tokeca duhapi kin , hena owasin yutokan iyewicayapo ; piiciyapi qa wokoyake teca ihduzapo ;
01035003	Qa najinpo , Betel ekta itawankanhde unyanpi kte ce . Heciya wahna wošnapi wan wakage kta , anpetu wan iyomakišice cehan , Taku wakan namaĥon , qa canku ohna imdamde cin mici ye cin , he wecage kta ce , eya .
01035004	Unkan Taku wakan tokeca yuhapi kin hena owasin Jakob qupi , oinpidan noge oinpi kin hena koya . Unkan hena owasin naĥma , šekem ekta utuhu wan he cin , he ihukuya .
01035005	Hehan ihdaka iyayapi , qa Jehowa otonwe ihdukšan unpi kin yušinye wicaya ; hecen Jakob cinkši wicaye cin wicakuwapi šni .
01035006	Unkan Jakob , iye oyate opeya un kin koya owasin , otonwe wan Luz eciyapi , Betel hee , Kanan makoce kin en , he ekta ipi .
01035007	Qa hen wahna wošnapi wan kage ca , oyanke kin he El Betel eya caš ton , cincu etanhan najica iyaye cehan , heciya iye en Wakantanka ihdutanin kin , heon etanhan .
01035008	Hehan Debora Rebeka azin kiye ciqon ta , unkan Betel hukun utuhu he cin , he ihukuya hnakapi , qa he , Utuhu oceyapi , eciyapi .
01035009	Wanna Jakob Aram Mdaye kin etanhan hiyu , hehan ake iye en Wakantanka tanin iciye ca yawašte .
01035010	Qa , Tokata Jakob nicaje qon eniciyapi kte šni , detanhan Israel eya cajeniyatapi kta , Wakantanka eciye ca , hecen Israel caš ton .
01035011	Qa , El Iyotan wašaka he miye ; ihduota qa cinca ota yuha wo ; oyate qa , oyate obe ota niye etanhan unpi kta , qa wicašta yatapi ninite kin etanhan inanpapi kta .
01035012	Qa makoce wan Abereyam Izak kici wicawaqu qon , he niye cicu kte ca nicinca nihektam unpi kte cin , makoce kin he wicawaqu kta ce , Wakantanka eciya .
01035013	Qa oyanke kin en , Wakantanka okiye ciqon hetanhan wankantkiya ikiyopta .

01035015	Qa oyanke kin en , Wakantanka okiye ciqon , he Jakob Betel eya caš ton .

01035017	Wanna kitan ecinyan cinca ton , hehan , Ihnuhan koyakipe cin , cinca kin de wica e nakun duhe kta ce , cincatonkiyesa eciya .
01035018	Unkan wanna te kta , nagi kin iyaya icunhan , Benoni eya caš kiton ; tuka atkuku kin Benjamin eciya .

01036003	Qa Išmayel cunwintku Basmat , Nebayot tankšitku he nakun yuza .

01036007	Taku yuhapi kin he odota , heon witaya iyotankapi kin okitpanipi , wanuyanpi ota yuhapi kin heon , makoce kin en ounyanpi kte cin iyowinwicakiye šni .

01036011	Unkan Elipaz cinkši wicaye cin dena eepi ; Teman , Omar , Zepo , Gatam , qa Kenaz .

01036013	Unkan Ruhel cinkši wicaye cin dena eepi ; Naĥat , qa Zera , qa šama , qa Miza . Esa tawicu Basmat cinkši wicaye cin hena eepi .

01037003	Unkan Israel , cinkši wicaye cin owasin sam iyeya , Josep wašte kidaka wanna wicaĥinca ehan kicitonpi kin heon etanhan , qa onĥdoĥda hanska wan Josep kicaga .

01037008	Unkan cinye wicaye cin heciyapi , Ehanqon tawaunyayapi kta he ? qa iš wowidake unyaduhapi kta he ? Qa iyakapeya šice kidakapi , wihanmde ciqon oie ko heon .

01037010	He atkuku cincu ko owicakiyaka ; unkan atkuku he iyopekiye ca , Wowihanmde wan iyahanmde cin de taku how ? Miye qa nihun nicinye ko owasin nitokam makipusdiya eĥpeunkiciyapi kta he ? eciya .

01037014	Unkan , Iho ekta de ca nicinye wanuyanpi ko zaniyan yakonpi hecinhan wanhdake ca , hoši makahdi wo , eciya . Unkan ĥebron kaksiza kin etanhan iyaye ca šekem ekta i .
01037015	Qa tinta onuni ; unkan wicašta wan wanyake ca , Den taku ayakita he ? eya iwanga .
01037016	Unkan , Cinye wicawaye cin awicawakita ce . Ceciye tukten wiĥan wicakiyapi kin omakiyaka wo , eya .
01037017	Unkan wicašta qon , Wanna detanhan iyayapi ; Dotan ekta unyanpi kta ce , eyapi nawaĥon ce , eya . Unkan Josep cinye wicaye cin wicihakam ye ca Dotan en iyewicaya .
01037018	Unkan tehantanhan wanyakapi qa wicikiyedan u šni kin itokam , naĥmana te yapi kta awacinpi .
01037019	Qa otoiyohi hunka wanjitku kin hekiciyapi , Wanyakapo ; wihanmdesa kin de wanna u .
01037020	Ihopo dehan unktepi , qa makoĥdoka wan ohna eĥpeunyanpi kte ca , Wamanica ocin šica wan he temya ce , unkeyapi kinhan , wihanmde ciqon toketu kte cin wanunyakapi kta ce , ekiciyapi .
01037021	Ruben he naĥon qa , napepi kin etanhan ehdaku kta e , Unktepi kte šni , eya .
01037022	Napepi kin etanhan ehdaku kte ca , atkuku kin en akiyahde kta e Ruben hewicakiya ; Weyapi šnipo . Woĥa ĥewoskantuya wanke cin de ohna iyeyapo , tuka ninapepi on apapi šnipo .
01037023	Unkan kaketu , Josep iye cincu najinpi kin en hi qehan , taonĥdoĥda yušdokapi , onĥdoĥda hanska un kin hee ;
01037024	Qa Josep icupi , qa woĥa wan en iyoĥpeyapi , tuka woĥa kin takudan ohnaka šni , mini wanica .
01037025	Qa aguyapi yutapi kta e iyotankapi , qa pa yuwankan ikikcupi qa , Išmayeli optaye wan Gileyad eciyatanhan u kin wanwicayakapi , camo yuhapi kin taku waštemna canšin pejihuta koya qinpi , Egupta ekta kun yapi kta .
01037026	Unkan Juda hunka wanjin wicaye cin hewicakiya , De sunka unyanpi unktepi kinhan , we kin naunĥmanpi ešta taku unkihdamnapi kta he ?
01037027	Ihopo , Išmayeli kin dena en wiyopeunyanpi kte . De sunka unyanpi qa kici ceĥpi unwanjipidan kin heon , nape on unkatapi kte šni , eya . Unkan hunka wanjin wicaye cin anakigoptanpi .
01037028	Hehan wicašta wopeton hecapi Midiani en hiyayapi . Unkan Josep yuzapi , qa woĥa qon etanhan yuwankan ehdakupi , qa mazaska wikcemna nonpa on Josep wiyopeyapi . Unkan Išmayeli kin Josep opetonpi , qa Egupta ekta ayapi .
01037029	Unkan Ruben woĥa qon ekta hi , unkan Josep en un šni , heon tawokoyake hdupota ,
01037030	Qa hunka wanjitku kin en wicahdi qa , Hokšidan kin tanin šni ce , miš toki imdamde kta how , ewicakiya .
01037031	Unkan Josep taonĥdoĥda qon icupi qa tatokadan mdoka wan ktepi , qa we kin on oputkanpi .
01037032	Hehan tuwe onĥdoĥda hanske cin ahde šipi qa ateyapi kin kahipi qa heciyapi ; De iyeunyanpi ce . Ito de nicinkši onĥdoĥda tawa qa iš tawa šni uman tukte hecetu hecinhan iyukcan wo .
01037033	Unkan iyekiye ca , Micinkši taonĥdoĥda qon dee . Wamanica šica wan he temya . Ehanqon Josep wanna yapotapi ce , eya .
01037034	Unkan Jakob tawokoyake hdupote ca , wašihda qa anpetu ota cinhintku kin akiceya .
01037035	Unkan cinca wicaye cin owasin wica winyan ko magagaye wacinpi , tuka iš magaga yapi cin šni , qa , Iyomakišica ecen micinkši en Hades ekta mde kta ce , eye ca cinhintku kin akiceya .
01037036	Unkan Midiani kin Egupta en Josep wiyopeyapi ; unkan Potipar Paro taakicita tancan opeton .
01038001	Hena owasin hecetu , unkan Juda hunka wanjin wicaye cin etanhan apamahde ye ca , Adulami wicašta wan ĥira eciyapi ekta i ;
01038002	Qa hen Juda Kanani wicašta wan šuha eciyapi , he cunwintku wanyake ca yuze ca en i .
01038003	Unkan ihdušake ca cinca wan ton ; unkan Er eya caš kiton .
01038004	Unkan ake ihdušake ca , cinca wan ton qa , Onan eya caš kiton .
01038005	Qa ake cinca wan ton qa , šela eya caš kiton . He ton kin ehan Kezib en un .
01038006	Unkan Juda eye cinhintku tokapa kin Er , winoĥinca wan , Tamar eciyapi yus kiya .
01038007	Unkan Er Juda cinhintku tokapa kin he šica e Jehowa wanyake ca , Jehowa he te ya .
01038008	Hehan Juda Onan heciya , Nicinye tawicu qon ekta ye ca , he yuza wo . Hecen nicinye cinkši ye kte cin yakage kta ce .
01038009	Unkan cinca kin he iye tawa yawapi kte šni Onan sdonye , ca cincu cinca kicage kte šni e cincu tawicu qon en i eca , maka kin atpapson .
01038010	Unkan taku econ kin he šica e Jehowa wanyake ca , he nakun te ya .
01038011	ĥehan Juda iye takošku kin Tamar heciya , Wiwazica niyate ti kin en yanka wo , micinkši šela tanka icage cin hehanyan . Okini iš nakun cinye wicaye cin iyecen te kta kecin , heon hecen eya . Unkan Tamar kihde ca atkuku ti kin en yanka .
01038012	He iyohakam anpetu ota , qa šuha cunwintku Juda tawicu kin wanna ta ; unkan Juda wanna magaga yapi , qa Timnat ekta taĥin wanuyanpi tawa yušdapi kin ekta itawankanhde ya , iye takodaku ĥira Adulami kin kicica .
01038013	Unkan Tamar heciyapi , Iho nitunkan taĥin wanuyanpi tawa hdušda kta e Timnat ekta itawankanhde ya ce , eyapi .
01038014	Unkan Tamar iyoyakeca wokoyake hdušdoke ca , ite ahaĥpe on aihdaĥpe ca , Timnat canku iyahde kin he icahda taninyan iyotanka ; šela wanna tanka , tuka qupi šni he wanyaka , heon hecon .
01038015	Juda he wanyaka ite aihdaĥpe cin heon winoĥinca wihomni heca kecin ;
01038016	Qa canku kin etanhan ekta i , qa takošku kin hee kin sdonye šni heon , Tokin unwanken , eciya . Unkan unwanke ca , taku mayaqu kta he ? eya .
01038017	Unkan , Miš wanuyanpi kin etanhan tatokadan cincadan wan nicahipi waye kta , eya . Unkan , Au wicayakiye cin itokam taku mayaqu kinhan , eya .
01038018	Unkan , He cicu kta e sdonyaye kte cin on etanhan taku e nakaha cicu kta yacin he ? eya . Unkan , Maza huhu duhe cin ikan iyahna , qa nakun nitacanĥpi ninape ohna duhe cin , eya . Unkan hena qu qa , kici wanka ; unkan iye etanhan ihdušaka .
01038019	Qa najin qa hde ca ite akaĥpe hdušdoke ca ake wašihda .
01038020	Unkan Juda taku qu qon , winoĥinca nape kin etanhan ehdaku kta e , takodaku Adulami kin tatokadan cincadan aye ši , tuka iye winoĥinca qon iyeye šni .
01038021	Qa wicašta heciya yakonpi kin iwicawanga ; Witkowin canku ohna taninyan iyotanke ciqon tukte e he ? eya . Unkan , Tohini witkowin wan deciya yanke šni , eyapi .
01038022	Unkan ihdamna , qa Juda ekta i qa heciya ; Winoĥinca qon iyewaye šni qa , nakun wicašta heciya yakonpi kin , Witkowin wanjidan tohini deciya un šni ce , eyapi .
01038023	Unkan , Yuha un nunwe . Tatokadan cincadan kin de aye ciši tuka iyeyaye šni ; sanpa unkakite cinhan , okini wowiĥaĥa unke kta , Juda eya .
01038024	Unkan hetanhan wi yamni hehan , Nitakoš Tamar wawiciĥaĥa econ , qa wanna wawiciĥaĥa kin etanhan ihdušaka ce , Juda eciyapi . Unkan , Tankan aupo ; ĥuĥnage kta ce , eya .
01038025	He aupi kin icunhan tunkanku hecen wahoya , Tokin maza huhu kin de ikan iyahna , qa canĥpi kin de , dena tuwe tawa imiyecidukcan . Tuwe dena tawa ye cin , wicašta kin he etanhan ihdumašaka ce , eya .
01038026	Unkan Juda hena iyekiye ca , Winoĥinca kin he oĥan owotanna miš hemacece šni ; he micinkši šela waqu šni kin heon etanhan , eye ca hetanhan icimana winoĥinca qon sdonye šni .
01038027	Unkan wanna cinca ton kte cehan , inyun tezi mahen cekpa yukan .
01038028	Qa tonpi kin icunhan , wanji nape kin qu ; unkan cinca tonkiye cin he nape kin icu , qa taku duta iyakaške ca , De tokaheya hinanpe kta ce , eya .
01038029	Unkan nape kin ehdaku , hehan inyun cincu hiyu . Unkan winoĥinca kin heya , Token payaĥdeca ; Opaĥdeca kin de anicipe nunwe , eye ca , Parez eya caš ton .
01038030	Hehan sunkaku taku duta nape kin akan yuhe cin he hiyu ; unkan he Zara eya caš ton .
01039001	Unkan Išmayeli kin Josep Egupta ekta ayapi . Unkan Potipar Egupton wicašta kin heca , Paro taakicita tancan kin he aupi kin Josep opewicakicaton .
01039002	Unkan Jehowa Josep kici un . Unkan taku econ kin owasin tanyan ihuni ye ca iye yuhe cin Egupton ti kin en yanka .
01039003	Unkan Jehowa kici un , qa taku nape econ kin owasin Jehowa tanyan yuštan kiye cin he yuhe cin wanyaka .
01039004	Unkan Josep yuhe cin okiye ca iyokipi ya ; unkan tiyohnaka tawa owasin awanyag ši , qa taku tawa owasin nape kin en qu .
01039005	Unkan tipi tawa , qa taku tawa owasin awanyag ši kin ehantanhan , Jehowa Josep on etanhan Egupton tiyohnaka kin yawašte , qa taku ti ohnaka , qa tamaga ekta wanke cin ko owasin , Jehowa yawašte kin akan un .
01039006	Hehan taku tawa owasin Josep nape kin en eĥpeye ca , iš takudan awakicin šni , aguyapi hdute cin heceedan . Unkan Josep owanyag wašte , tancan ite ko wašte .
01039007	Hena owasin hecetu ; unkan hehan yuhe cin tawicu kin Josep atonwe ca , Mici wanka ye , eya .
01039008	Tuka wicada šni qa yuhe cin tawicu kin heciya ; Hiya , mayuhe cin taku tawa owasin minape kin en qu , qa taku tipi ohnaka kin mici un kin iye sdonye šni .
01039009	De tipi kin ohna tuwedan iyamakapa šni ; qa nihihna miye etanhan takudan tpatan šni , niš nana miyuze cin heon etanhan , qa token woaĥtani tanka kin de ecamon , qa Wakantanka en wawaĥtani kta he ? eya .
01039010	Unkan winoĥinca qon anpetu owasin heciya , qa kitan ĥinca , tuka Josep anagoptan šni , kici iwanke šni qa ecaca kici un šni .
01039011	Unkan kaketu , anpetu wan Josep taku tokon kta e ti mahen i ehan , wicašta hen tipi kin tuwedan timahen un šni .
01039012	Unkan winoĥinca qon Josep tašina kin iyaĥpaye ca , Mici iwanka ye , eya ; tuka šina kin winoĥinca nape kin etanhan eĥpeya našdog hdicu , qa tankan iyaya .
01039013	Unkan nape kin etanhan šina eĥpeya tankan našdog hdicu kin he winyan kin wanyake ca ,
01039014	Hehan wicašta tona ti kin ohna tipi kin hena wicakipan , qa hewicakiya , Wanyakape , Heberi wicašta wan den unkahdipi , unkan wištenunyanpi cin . Manke cin en mahi qa mici wanke kte ĥinca , tuka ho tankakiya nina wašicahowamda .
01039015	Nina ho tankakiya wašicahowamde cin he naĥon , qa wapan qehan , mitankiyedan šina eĥpeya našdog tankan iyaya ce , eya .
01039016	Qa yuhe cin hdi kte cin hehanyan šina qon , itankiyedan ehnaka .
01039017	Qa eye ciqon owasin ake ecen okiyaka , Heberi hokšidan unyakahdipi kin he imaĥa kta e mikiyadan u .
01039018	Qa ho tankakiya wašicahowamde cehan mitankiyedan šina eĥpeya našdog tankan iyaya ce , eya .
01039019	Unkan yuhe cin he tawicu oie kin , Hokšidan nitawa kin hecen ecamicon , eciye cin he naĥon hehan cantiyahdeya .
01039020	Qa yuhe cin Josep icu , qa wicašta yatapi tona . Kaška wicahnake cin tipi wan en kaška wicahnakapi kin he en Josep kaška ehnaka . Unkan wicakaška tipi kin en yanka .
01039021	Unkan Jehowa Josep kici un qa , towaonšida kin hiyohiya qa wicakaška tipi kin itancan kin he Josep wacin en yus kiya .
01039022	Unkan wicakaška tipi itancan kin , tona wicakaška tipi kin en kaška wicahnakapi kin owasin Josep nape kin en qu . Unkan taku hen econpi kin owasin Josep econ wicakiya .
01039023	Hecen Jehowa Josep kici un , qa taku econ kin owasin tanyan yuštan kiya ; heon wicakaška tipi itancan kin , taku Josep nape en yuhe cin hena takudan awanhdake šni .
01040001	Hena owasin hecetu , unkan hehan Egupta wicašta yatapi tawayatkekiye tawohekiye ko , wicayuhe cin Egupta wicašta yatapi kin en waĥtanipi .
01040002	Hecen Paro akicita nom wicayuhe cin canniye wicaya , wayatkekiyapi tancan , qa wohekiyapi tancan kin henioza .
01040003	Qa akicita tancan tipi tawa wicakaška tipi kin tukten Josep kaška hnakapi yanke cin he en awanyag wicakiyapi kta e ewicahnaka .
01040004	Unkan akicita tancan kin he Josep hena awanwicayag kiya , unkan owicakiya . Unkan anpetu ota kaška hnakapi ecen yukanpi .
01040005	Hehan Egupta wicašta yatapi tawayatkekiye , tawohekiye ko , wicakaška tipi kin ohna kaška wicahnakapi , hanyetu wanjidan en kinukan wowihanmde ihanmnapi , otoiyohi wihanmnapi kin iyukcanpi kin iyecen .
01040006	Hehan ihanĥanna Josep en wicahi qa iyokišicapi kin wanwicayaka .
01040007	Qa Paro taakicita wicakaška tipi kin , iye yuhe cin tipi tawa kin he en iye kici unpi wiwicawanga ; Tokeca nakaha ite iyoyag dukanpi he ? eya .
01040008	Unkan wowihanmde wiunhanmnapi , tuka tuwe iyukcan kte cin den wanica ce , eciyapi . Unkan wiyukcan kin Wakantanka hee šni he ? Wiyahanmnapi kin omakiyakapo , Josep ewicakiya .
01040009	Hehan wayatkekiyapi tancan kin wihanmde ciqon ohdaka qa , Wiwahanmde cin en hastanhanka iyuwi wan mitokam han .
01040010	Qa adetka yamni wiyuwi aicage ca ape waĥca ko icaĥ ye , qa iyage hastanhanka suton yapi .
01040011	Hehan Paro wiyatke tawa kin minape ohna mduha , qa hastanhanka kin iwacu , qa Paro wiyatke tawa kin ohna mduškice ca Paro nape kin en wiyatke kin ewehde , eya .
01040012	Unkan Josep heciya , Wiyahanmde cin he kaken ka . Adetka yamni qon anpetu yamni ee .
01040013	Ebake yamni can Paro nipa kin yuwankan inicu kte ca nanke ciqon ake en anihde kta ; unkan tokaheya wayatkeyakiye ciqon wicoĥan kin ake ecen ecanon kta , Paro nape kin en tawiyatke kin yaqu kta .
01040014	Hena hecetu kinhan miksuya wo . Tokin tanyan yaun kinhan wowašte ecamiyecon , Paro en caje mayadaten qa tipi kin de etanhan hinanpe mayayen .
01040015	Awicakehan Heberi tamakocepi kin etanhan mamanonpi , qa deciya takudan ecamon šni on makoĥdoka kin den emahnakapi kta , eya .
01040016	Hehan wohekiyapi tancan kin wiyukcan wašte e wanyake ca Josep heciya ; Miš nakun wiwahanmde ca inyun , aguyapi makanopiye yamni mapa kin akan .
01040017	Qa makanopiye akantu kin ohna Paro tawoyute ocaje owasin wohekiyapi kage cin . Unkan zitkadan hena temyapi , makanopiye mapa kin iwankam un kin hetanhan .
01040018	Unkan Josep ayupta ; He kaken ka . Makanopiye yamni kin anpetu yamni eepi .
01040019	Ehake yamni can Paro pa kin yuwankan inicu qa , can akan otke niye kta ; hehan zitkadan niceĥpi kin etanhan yutapi kta .
01040020	Unkan iyamni can , anpetu en Paro tonpi kin he kiksuyapi kta e wowidag wicaye cin owasin wowicakihe , ca wayatkekiyapi tancan wohekiyapi tancan henioza wowidake wicaye cin wicehna hdinanpe wicaya .
01040021	Qa wayatkekiyapi tancan kin wayatke wicakiye ciqon wicoĥan ake hecon ši ; unkan wiyatke kin Paro nape kin en qu .
01040022	Tuka wohekiyapi tancan kin otke ya , Josep iwicakiciyukcan qon iyecen .
01040023	Unkan wayatkekiyapi tancan kin Josep kiksuye šni , tuka akiktonja .
01041001	Hehan tanhan waniyetu nonpa hehan Paro wihanmna . Unkan iho wakpa kahda inajin .
01041002	Qa inyun wakpa kin etanhan , pte šakowin owanyag wašte qa cepa heca hinanpapi , qa tinta en wiĥanpi .
01041003	Qa hena ihektapa tanhan pte tokeca šakowin owanyag šica qa tamaheca hecapi , wakpa etanhan hinanpapi , qa pte umanpi qon ehna wakpicahda najinpi .
01041004	Qa pte owanyag šica tamaheca hena pte owanyag wašte cepapi šakowin qon temwicayapi . Unkan Paro kikta .
01041005	Ake ištima qa inonpa wihanmna . Unkan inyun wamnaheza hu wanjidan wahuwapa šakowin suton , qa waštešte aicaga .
01041006	Qa hena iyohakam wahuwapa tokeca šakowin hinanpa , tuka šikšica qa wiyohiyanpa tanhan tate on šnija .
01041007	Qa wahuwapa conica ton šni kin wahuwapa suton qa ojugjudan qon owasin temya . Paro hecen wihanmde ca hehan kikta .
01041008	Unkan ihanĥanna qehan Paro nagi kin iyokišice ca , Egupton en pejihuta wicašta qa wicašta ksapapi kin owasin wicakico , qa wihanmde ciqon Paro owasin owicakiyaka ; tuka tuwedan yukcan okihi šni .
01041009	Hehan Paro wayatkekiyapi tancan kin ie ca , Anpe dehan wawaĥtani kin weksuya ce .
01041010	Paro taokiye kin canniye wicaye ca , akicita tancan tipi kin en kaška mahnaka , miye qa wohekiyapi tancan kin he nakun .
01041011	Unkan hanyetu wanjidan en wiunhanmnapi , miye iye kici kinukan , wihanmnapi iyukcanpi kin iyecen wiunhanmnapi .
01041012	Unkan hen unkicipi koška wan Heberi kin heca , akicita tancan tahokšidan kin he wiunhanmnapi kin unkokiyakapi , unkan iye hena iyukcan otoiyohi wiunhanmnapi kin iyecen unkiciyukcanpi .
01041013	Unkan unkiciyukcanpi kin ecetu ; miye ake wiyatke yuhe makiye ca uman kin otke ya .
01041014	Hehen Paro Josep huwe ye wicaši , unkan wicakaška tipi kin etanhan kiyuškapi , hehan putin hin hdasan , qa wokoyake tokeca kicun qa Paro yanke cin en hi .
01041015	Unkan Paro Josep heciya , Wowihanmde wan iwahanmna , unkan he yukcan kta okihi tuwedan iyewaye šni , tuka wihanmnapi niš nayaĥon unkan idukcan oyakihi keyapi nawaĥon .
01041016	Unkan Josep ayupte ca , Miye ee šni , Wakantanka eqe toketu kin tanyan oniciyake kta ce , eciya .
01041017	Unkan Paro ie ca , Wiwahanmde ca watpa hutata kin nawajin ;
01041018	Qa inyun wakpa kin etanhan , pte šakowin cepa , owanyag wašte hinanpapi , qa tinta kin en wiĥanpi .
01041019	Unkan hena iyohakam pte tokeca šakowin tamaheca , owanyag šikšica hinanpapi ; tamahenheca šica hena iyececa , Egupta makoce kin en tohini wanmdake šni .
01041020	Qa pte tamahenheca šice cin pte šakowin cepa tokaheya qon temwicayapi .
01041021	Unkan tan mahen iyayapi kin hehan , tan mahen iyayapi kin sdonye pica šni ; otokahe ekta šikšica taninpi qon nahaĥin hececapi . Unkan hehan wekta .
01041022	Qa ake wiwahanmde ca inyun wamnaheza hu wanjidan wahuwapa šakowin hanskaska waštešte aicage cin wanmdaka .
01041023	Hehan ake wahuwapa šakowin cikcistina , wiyohiyanpata tateyanpa kin on šnijapi , qa co wanica hinanpapi .
01041024	Qa wahuwapa cikcistina wahuwapa šakowin waštešte qon owasin temyapi . Unkan wicašta wiyukcan heca owicawakimdaka , tuka miciyukcanpi šni .
01041025	Hehan Josep Paro heciya , Paro wihanmde cin hena okonwanjidan , Wakantanka token econ kte cin he Paro okiyaka .
01041026	Pte šakowin wašte qon , hena waniyetu šakowin ee ; qa wahuwapa šakowin waštešte qon , hena nakun waniyetu šakowin ee , wowihanmde kin hena wanjidan .
01041027	Qa pte šakowin tamaheca , qa šice cin umanpi kin iyohakam hinanpapi kin , hena waniyetu šakowin ee , qa wahuwapa šakowin cikcistina wiyohiyanpata tateyanpa kin on šnija kin hena nakun , waniyetu šakowin wicaakiĥan kte cin hee .
01041028	Paro taku ewakiye cin he dee . Wakantanka taku econ kte cin he Paro wanyag kiye .
01041029	Hecetu kta , tokata waniyetu šakowin hehanyan , Egupta makoce kin owancaya taku owasin iyakicuya icage kta .
01041030	Qa hena iyohakam waniyetu šakowin wicaakiĥan kta , qa Egupta makoce kin en taku iyakicuya icage kte ciqon akiktunjapi kte ca , wicaakiĥan kte cin makoce kin awihnuni kta .
01041031	Unkan hehan wicaakiĥan kte cin iyotan teĥike kte cin makoce kin en , heon wipipi qon sdonyapi kte šni .
01041032	Qa wicoie kin de Wakantanka yuecetu kte ca , wanna kohanna Wakantanka econ kta , heon Paro nonpa akihde wihanmna .
01041033	Qa wanna Paro wicašta wan ksape ca wayupika akite ca , Egupta makoce kin yuhe kiya nunwe .
01041034	Qa Paro akicita wicakage ca makoce kin en wicahdusuta kte ; unkan waniyetu šakowin wipipi kta hena icunhan , taku makoce aicage kte cin owasin izaptanptan icupi nunwe .
01041035	Hecen waniyetu šakowin waštešte kte cin hena icunhan , woyute ocaje owasin kamnapi kte , Paro nape kin ihukuya , tonwanyanpi kin en aguyapi pahipi kte cin he woyute awanyakapi nunwe .
01041036	Qa waniyetu šakowin wicaakiĥan kte cin Egupta makoce kin en hena on , taku yutapi kihnakapi kinhan , makoce kin wicaakiĥan kte cin on awihnuni kte šni , eya .
01041037	Unkan Paro ookiye wicaye cin ko wicoie kin he wašte dakapi .

01041039	Qa Paro Josep heciya , Wakantanka de owasin sdonye niciye cin , niš nana widukcan qa yaksapa , tuwedan iyenicece šni .
01041040	Niš wati kin awanmiyecidake kta , qa oyate mitawa owasin oie ananigoptanpi kta . Oiyotanke kin en hecedan iciwankam waun kta .
01041041	Qa wanyaka wo , Egupta makoce kin owasin yuhe ciciya ce , eya .
01041042	Hehan Paro maza napcupe hdušdoke ca Josep nape kin ohna iyeye ca , miniĥuha ska wašte koyag ye ca , mazaskazi wanapin wan napin kiya .
01041043	Qa canpahmihma inonpa kin he ohna iyotang ye ca , Itokam canpeška makehde inajinpo , ieyanpaha eyapi , qa Egupta makoce kin owasin yuhe kiyapi .
01041044	Qa Paro Josep heciya , Paro miye ce . Oyate kin tuwedan iye cinka takudan econ kte šni . Niš nana token econ wicayaši kin hecetu kta ce .
01041045	Qa Paro Josep , Wicoicage nikiye cin , eya caš ton , qa On otonwe kin en wošnapi kage cin , Potipera he cunwintku Asenat tawicu kta e qu . Unkan Josep Egupta makoce kin ehna iyaya .
01041046	Josep , Egupton wicašta yatapi Paro itokam najin qehan , wanna waniyetu wikcemna yamni qa , hehan Josep Paro itokapa tanhan inanpe ca Egupta makoce kin owancaya iyoptapta iyaya .
01041047	Unkan waniyetu wipipi kin hena icunhan , makoce kin napohnahnaka icaĥ ya .

01041049	Qa Josep , miniwanca kahdaya wiyaka wanke cin iyecen , aguyapi ota ĥinca pahi , yawapica šni nakaeš yawapi kte cin ayaštanpi .

01041055	Unkan Egupta makoce kin owancaya akiĥanpi kte cehan , oyate kin aguyapi on Paro hoyekiyapi . Unkan , Josep ekta yapi qa , token econ nišipi kin ecen econpo , Paro Egupton owasin ewicakiya .
01041056	Wanna maka ohnaka owancaya wicaakiĥan , hehan Josep aguyapi opiye kin owasin hduĥdoke ca , Egupton taku yutapi wicaqu ; Egupta makoce kin en wicaakiĥan teĥika aye nakaš .
01041057	Unkan maka owancaya etanhan , Egupta ekta Josep en taku yutapi opeton hipi , maka kin owancaya nina wicaakiĥan ece .
01042001	Hehan Egupta makoce kin en aguyapi yuke cin Jakob wanyake ca cinkši wicaye cin hewicakiya , Tokeca ecin opakiciĥta dukanpi he ?
01042002	Ihopo Egupta heciya aguyapi yukan keyapi nawaĥon . Ecin kutkiya ekta yapi qa heciya tanhan woyute ope unkicatonpo , kinhan unnipi qa untapi kte šni ce , eya .
01042003	Unkan Josep cinye wicaye cin wikcemna qon aguyapi opetonpi kta e Egupta makoce kin ekta kutkiya ipi .

01042013	Unkan , Hokšidan nitawa hunka wanjin unkiciyapi ake unnonpapi ; Kanan makoce kin en wicašta wanjidan ate unyanpi , qa hakakta kin he anpe dehan ate unyanpi kin kici yanka , qa wanjidan tanin šni , eyapi .
01042014	Unkan , Makoce iwanyakapi kin henicapi ; eya eciciyapi qon he hecetu ce .

01042017	Qa iyamni can hehanyan witaya onatag wicahnaka .

01042019	Wicayakapi kinhan , hunka wanjin yayapi kin wanjidan kaška yanke kta , tipi kin de onatag nihnakapi kin he en , qa niye umanpi kin ihopo , tiyohnaka nitawapi kin wicaakiĥan kin on woyute akiyahdapo .
01042020	Qa sunka yayapi cistina kin he miye en makaupo , hecen nioie yahduwicakapi kinhan nitapi kte šni . Unkan ecen econpi .
01042021	Qa iyakitedan hekiciyapi , Ehanqon waunĥtanipi . Sunka unyanpi wacin iyokišin wanunyakapi qa ceunkiyapi , tuka anaungoptanpi šni , heon wocante šice cin de unhiyahdepi ce , eyapi .
01042022	Unkan Ruben ayupte ca , Hokšidan kin en waĥtanipi šnipo eciciyapi šni he ? tuka anamayagoptanpi šni ; unkan ecin iye we kin wanna wiunwangapi kin he dee ce , eya .
01042023	Unkan Josep he naĥon sdonyapi šni . Taku ewicakiya eca wicašta wan ie ska kiya ece nakaeš .
01042024	Tuka Josep wicitokapa tanhan toki ye ca ceya . Hehan icicawin en wicahdi qa , taku ewicakiye ca , hehan umanpi kin etanhan šimeyon icu qa , ištapi kin wicitokam pakiĥta .
01042025	Hehan Josep wojuha tawapi kin aguyapi on ojuwicakicitonpi kta , qa mazaska tawapi otoiyohi wojutonpi kin en owicakicihnakapi kta ; waneya nakun wicaqupi kta , keya . Unkan hecen ecawicakicon .
01042026	Unkan šuktanka šonšonna kin taku yutapi qin wicakiyapi qa hdapi .

01042028	Unkan hunka wanjin wicaye cin hewicakiya , Mazaska mduhe ciqon ake micupi . Wanyakapo , wojutonpi mitawa kin en ohnakapi ce . Unkan owasin icanwankapi qa ikopapi qa , De taku Wakantanka ecaunkiconpi hwo , ekiciyapi .

01042033	Unkan , Oĥan oniwotanpidan kinhan , detanhan sdonwaye kta ce . Hunka wanjin yayapi kin wanjidan den mici yanke kta , qa yatipi kin en wicaakiĥan kin on , woyute icupi qa ekta hdapo .
01042034	Qa sunka yayapi hakakta kin he makaupo . Kinhan makoce iwanyakapi kin henicapi šni , qa oĥan oniwotanpidan kin sdonwaye kta ce , qa hehan , hunka wanjin yayapi kin de cicupi kta ; kinhan makoce kin den wopeyatonpi kta ce , makoce yuhe cin unkekiciyapi c

01042036	Hehan Jakob ate yapi kin hewicakiya ; Miye micinca mayakipi Josep tanin šni , qa šimeyon tanin šni , qa Benjamin iyacupi kta ; hena owasin iyokišin mayanpi .

01043001	Wanna makoce kin en wicaakiĥan teĥika aya .

01043019	Qa Josep ti kin awanyake cin he en ikiyedan hinajinpi , qa tipi tiyopa kin en okiyapi .
01043020	Qa , Itancan otokahe ekta taku yutapi opeuntonpi kta e kun unhipi .
01043021	Qa owanka qon , en unkiwankapi , qa wojutonpi unhduĥdokapi , unkan mazaska unkahipi qon otoiyohi wojutonpi unkitawapi i kin ohna yanka , mazaska aspeunkiye unkitonpi qon he iyececa , he owasin nape ohna unnicicahipi .

01049001	Qa Jakob cinkši wicaye cin wicakico qa heya , Mniciyapo , tokata anpetu yeye cin token nihiyahdepi kte cin ociciyakapi kta .
01049002	Jakob cinkši wicaye cin witaya upi qa anagoptanpo . Israel niyatepi kin he anakicigoptanpo .
01049003	Ruben micinkši tokapa kin he niye , mitowašake mitowookihi tokaheya kin iyotan wicimdeza iyotan suta .
01049004	Mini iyecen nihduhepicašni , heon initancan kte šni . Niyate ohehde kin ayadi qa hehan mitowinja kin dušapa ce .
01049005	šimeyon Lewi kici hunka wanjin kiciyapi . Tacanĥpipi kin wipe wicakisa kin heepi .
01049006	Canteptanyanpi qehan wicašta wan ktepi , qa iyokipi iciyapi kta e oinatake wan oqapi ; heon wohdakapi kin en minagi kin ye kte šni , qa omniciye tawapi kin en wowitan mitawa un šni numwe .
01049007	Wicocanniye tawapi kin yašicapi nunwe , waditaka ce , towaĥanicidapi kin he nakun , wohitika ce ; Jakob en yukinukan wicawakiye ca Israel ohna yuomden iyaye wicawakiye kta .
01049008	Juda niye hunka wanjin wicayaye cin niyatanpi kta . Ninape kin toka niyanpi tahu kin akan niyate cinkši wicaye cin nitokam patujapi kta .
01049009	Mnaja cincadan wan Juda heca . Wicayapotapi kin etanhan micinkši nayajin . Mnaja iyecen canpeška makehde wanka , qa mnaja wiye wan iyecen , tuwe he paĥice kta he ?
01049010	Juda etanhan maza sagye yutokanpi kte šni , tuka cadotahedan wicašta yatapi yuke kta , šilo hi kin hehanyan , qa iye en oyate kin mniciyapi kta .
01049011	Tašunke šonšonna hastanhanka iyuwi kin en iyakaškahan , qa tašunke šonšonna cinca kin hastanhanka wašte ĥinca iyuwi kin ekta , taonĥdoĥda kin miniša on hdujaja kta qa tašina hastanhanka we kin on .
01049012	Išta kin miniša on ša kte ca hi kin pte asanpi on ska kta .
01049013	Zebulon miniwanca huta kin en ti qa iye en wita wata oihuni kta , qa Zidon otonwe kin hehanyan yuhe kta .
01049014	Isakar šuktanka šonšonna wašake cin heca wan , conkaške otahedan makan wanka .
01049015	Okiĥpapi kin he wašte kin , qa makoce kin wiciyokipi kin he wanyake ca qin kta e taĥpa kin qu , hecen wayaka wicoĥtani kin econ .
01049016	Dan Israel wicoun wan iyecen taoyate kin wicayaco kta .
01049017	Wamduška wan canku tukte ohna yapi kte cin ohna naiciĥbe ca , šuktanka siyete kin yaĥtaka on tuwe akan yotanke cin itunkam hinĥpaye kta Dan hecece kta .
01049018	Jehowa woyuške nitawa kin awape .
01049019	Ozuye wan Gad azuye kta , tuka ihakam iye azuwicaye kta .
01049020	Ašer taaguyapi kin wašte qa wicašta yatapi woyute wiciyokipi kin wicaqu kta .
01049021	Neptali tamdoka kiyuškapi kin heca iapi wicimdeza ia .
01049022	Josep adetka waicaĥya ece , adetka waicaĥya mini ĥdoka icahda , taadetka kin conkaške iyadipi .
01049023	Wanhinkpe yuhapi kin hena iyaonpapi qa kigepi qa šicaya kuwapi .
01049024	Tuka tinazipe kin sutaya han , Jakob wašagye cin towašake kin eciya tanhan nape isto kin yuwašakapi ce . Heciya tanhan Israel taimnija qa wo wicaqu kin hee ;
01049025	Niyate Taku wakan da kin eciya tanhan . Iye oniciye ca Iyotan wašake cin iye niyawašte kta , maĥpiya wankan tanhan wowašte kin , ošbe kin ihukuya wanke cin wowašte kin , aze tezi ko wowašte kin nicu kte .
01049026	Niyate wicayawašte kin he wawokihika , ĥe ohinniyan he cin isanpa . Paha owihanke wanice cin taku wiciyokipi aicage cin he Josep pa kin en , qa tuwe hunka wanjin wicaye cin etanhan yukinukanpi qon , pesdete kin en unpi kte .
01049027	Benjamin šunktokeca yatesa heca anpao kte cin hehanyan yute kta ece ; ĥtayetu eca wawicaki kin pamni kta .
01049028	Israel wicoun ake nonpa kin hena owasin heepi , qa hecen ate yapi kin ewicakiye ca wicahdawašte , otoiyohi towašte kin iyecen wicayawašte .
01049029	Qa hecen wahokonwicakiya , Miš oyate mitawa kin en ope mayanpi kta , ate wicawaye cin om emahnakapo , imnija oĥdoka maga wan Epron ĥeti kin tawa qon en un kin , he en .
01049030	Kanan makoce kin etu , Mamore itokam , Makpela maga kin en imnija oĥdoka wanke cin he ohna . Abereyam wicašta ohna hnakapi kte cin he tawa kta e maga kin he Epron ĥeti kin he opekicaton .
01049031	Hen Abereyam tawicu Sara kici wicahnakapi , hen Izak tawicu Rebeka kici wicahnakapi , qa hen miš Leha wehnaka .
01049032	Maga kin he imnija oĥdoka ohna wanke cin ko , ĥet cinca wicaye cin opewicakicaton qon , ewicakiya .
01049033	hecen Jakob cinkši wicaye cin wahokonwicakiye cin ayaštan qehan , siha kin ohehdepi kin en ehdaku qa ta ; unkan taoyate kin ekta okipe yapi .
01050001	Hehan Josep atkuku ite kin akan eĥpeiciye ca iiputake ca ceya .
01050002	Qa Josep taokiye peji huta wicaštapi kin atkuku yuĥwin šni waštemna ye wicaši . Unkan peji huta wicašta kin Israel waštemna yanpi ; anpetu wikcemna tom hecakiconpi .
01050003	Tona yuĥwin šni waštemna yanpi eca hehanyan yuštanpi ece . Unkan Egupton anpetu wikcemna šakowin Jakob aceyapi .
01050004	Anpetu hena aceyapi kin wanna iyokiptapi , hehan Josep Paro tiyohnaka tawa kin hewicakiya , Wanna wašte mayadapike cinhan miye makapi qa Paro itokam hecen eyapo .
01050005	Ate hecen emakiya , Iho miš wanna mate kta ce . Kanan makoce kin heciya ohna hnakapi wan micice cin he ohna mahnaka wo , eye ca Wakantanka cajeyate maši . Unkan tokin wanna itawankanhde mde ca ate wehnaken , kinhan wahdi kta .
01050006	Unkan Paro ayupte ca , Itawankanhde ye ca niyate kihnaka wo , konza eye niši qon iyecen .
01050007	Unkan Josep atkuku kihnake kta e itawankanhde ye ca Paro taokiye kin owasin opapi , tiyohna hunka wicayapi , qa Egupta makoce kin hunka wicayapi ko owasin .
01050008	Qa Josep tiyohnaka tawa , qa hunka wanjin wicaye cin atkuku tiyohnaka tawa owasin ; tašiceca qa taĥinca , pte ko yuhapi kin henana Gošen makoce kin en kihnakapi .
01050009	Canpahmihma qa wicašta šuktanka akan yotankapi ko opapi , hecen ošpaye tanka ĥinca .
01050010	Unkan Atad tahocoka kin ekta ipi he Jordan akasanpa wanka , qa heciya woceye tanka anpetu šakowin atkuku kin nina aceyapi .
01050011	Unkan makoce wojutipi kin Kanani hena Atad tahocoka ohna ceyapi kin he wanyakapi qa , Egupton de nina ceyapi ce , eyapi ; heon oyanke kin he Egupton oceyapi kin eciyapi , he Jordan akasanpa wanka .
01050012	Hecen cinkši wicaye cin token econ wicaši qon , ecen ecakiconpi .
01050013	Qa cinkši wicaye cin , hena Kanan makoce kin ekta hduha yapi , qa Makpela maga kin en imnija oĥdoka wanke cin he ohna kihnakapi ; Mamore itokam ; maga kin he Abereyam Epron ĥeti kin etanhan opekicaton wicašta ohnahnakapi tawa kta e hecon .
01050014	Unkan Josep Egupta ekta hda , atkuku hnakapi kin iyohakam ; iye hunka wanjin wicaye cin , qa tona iye om atkuku hnakapi kta e itawankanhde yapi qon owasin .
01050015	Unkan Josep cinye wicaye cin ate yapi kin te cin , heon wikopapi qa heyapi , Okini Josep šicaya unkuwapi qa iye en taku šica ecaunkiconpi qon iš owasin tokicon kta .
01050016	Qa hecen Josep okiyag wicašipi ; Niyate te cin itokam hecen wahokonunkiyapi .
01050017	Josep kaken eyakiyapi kta , Tokin nicinye waĥtanipi kin wicayecicajujun . šicaya ecaniconpi tuka niyate ta Wakantanka kin wowindag wicaye cin waĥtanipi qon kajujun ; eya ce , eyapi . Unkan Josep wicoie okiyakapi kin on ceya .
01050018	Hehan Josep cinye wicaye cin iye en ipi , qa itokam eĥpeiciyapi qa , Iho unyaduhapi ce , eciyapi .
01050019	Unkan , Ihnuhan ininihanpi kin . Miš Wakantanka hemaceca he ?
01050020	Niyepi kin šicaya ecamicon wacanipi , tuka Wakantanka wašte kta e cin , oyate ota ni wicaye kta anpe dehan iyecen hecon ce .
01050021	Heon nakaha inihanpi šnipo . Miš wo cicupi kta niyepi nitašicecapi ko , ewicakiye ca , hecen wicakihna qa cantowicahnaka .
01050022	Josep Egupta en ounyan ; iye atkuku tawicoun koya , qa Josep waniyetu opawinge sanpa wikcemna ni .
01050023	Qa Josep Epraim cinca takojatpaku , qa sanpa cinca wanwicahdake ca nakun Manaše cinhintku Makir cinca kin hena Josep šiyoto akan wicahduha .
01050024	Hehan Josep hunka wanjin wicaye cin hewicakiya ; Miš mate kta tuka Wakantanka niyepi en nihipi kte ca , makoce kin de etanhan itawankanhde ye niyanpi kta ; makoce wan Abereyam Izak Jakob ko konza ewicakiye cin he ekta .
01050025	Qa Josep Israel cinca kin konza ewicakiya , Awicakehan Wakantanka niyepi kin en nihipi kta ; qa mihu kin detanhan ayahdapi kta ce , eya .
01050026	Hehan Josep ta iyaya . Wanna waniyetu opawinge sanpa wikcemna hehan . Unkan iye tancan yuĥwin šni waštemna yanpi , qa Egupta makoce kin en can ohna knakapi wan ohna hnakapi .
59001001	Jakob , Wakantanka taokiye , qa Jesus Messiya Itancan tawa kin he , wicowazi akenonpapi enanakiya eyaye cin hena wowapi wicakicaga ; wookiye .
59001002	Mihunkawanji , taku wawiyutanyan un kin ota ayakipapi kinhan , he wowiyuškin ocawasin hdawa po :
59001003	Wacinyayapi iyutanpi kin he wacintankapi kaga e sdonyayapi .
59001004	Tuka wacintankapi kin he toĥan kin tanyan hduštan kte ; hecen niyuštanpi qa ocowasin yaunpi kta , qa takudan iyonitpanipi kte šni .
59001005	Niyepi etanhan tuwe woksape nice cinhan , Wakantanka kida kta , iye owasin iyakicuya wicaqu ece , qa iyopewicaye šni ; unkan qupi kta .
59001006	Tuka takudan cetunhda šni wacinyan kida kta ; tuwe wacetunhda kin he miniwanca taja kin iyececa , tateyanpa kaškanškan qa kaĥoya eĥpeye cin .
59001007	Wicašta kin he Itancan kin etanhan taku icu kta kecin kta iyecece šni .
59001008	Wicašta tawacin nonpa kin he tacanku owasin ohna kaktihanhan un ece .
59001009	Hunkawanjinkiciyapi waĥpanica kin yuwankan iyeyapi kinhan , heon iyuškin kta .
59001010	Tuka wijica un kin yuwaĥpanicapi kinhan , on iyuškin kta ; peji ĥca kin he iyecen tokan aye kte cin heon .
59001011	Anpetu wi kin hinanpe ca kata aya eca , wato kin šnišya ece , qa waĥca iĥpaye ca owanyake wašte kin he atakuni šni ece : he iyecen wicašta wijica kin iye toĥan kin en awihnuni kta .
59001012	Wicašta iyutanyanpi kin he yawaštepi ece ; tohan tanyan yukcanpi kinhan , hehan wiconi watešdake , Itancan kin tona waštedakapi iwahowicaye ciqon , hee icu kta .
59001013	Tuwe iyutanyanpi kinhan , Wakantanka iyutanmayan ce , eye kte šni : Wakantanka taku šica on iyutanyanpi kta okihi šni , qa nakun tuwedan iyutanye šni .
59001014	Tuka wicašta otoiyohi iye cantiheye šice cin on iyutanpi qa iyakapeyapi ece .
59001015	Hehan wocantiheye šice cin icage cinhan woaĥtani kaga ; qa woaĥtani yuštanpi eca , wiconte icaĥya ece .
59001016	Mihunkawanji wašte , icihnayanpi šni po .
59001017	Taku wicaqupi wašte qa yuštanpi kin owasin wankantanhan un , qa iyoyanpa A teyapi kin eciyatanhan kun u ece ; iye qe tokeca šni , qa yuhomnipica šni ĥinca .
59001018	Iye tawacin kin eciyatanhan , wowicake oie kin on cinca unkagapi , hecen taku kage cin ehna unkiye waskuyeca tokaheya iyeuncecapi kta .
59001019	Heon etanhan , mihunkawanji wašte , wicašta otoiyohi wanaĥon oĥanko kta , ie kapin kta , qa wacintanka kte :
59001020	Wicašta šinhdapi kin he Wakantanka toowotanna kin icaĥye šni .
59001021	Heon etanhan , wicowaĥtešni kin owasin , qa taku šica iyatahdepi kin eĥpeya po ; qa wicoie ninagipi niye kta okihi kin he onšiiciya icu po .
59001022	Tuka wicoie kin ecen econ po , qa iye icihnayanpi , naĥonpi ecedan , unpi šni po .
59001023	Tuwe wicoie naĥon ešta ecen econ šni kinhan , he wicašta wan ihdiyomdasin on ite iwanihdake cin iyececa ;
59001024	Iwanihdake ca tankan iyaya , unkan hehan hinnakaha ite tokeca kin he akiktonja ece .
59001025	Tuka tuew wicoope on tawaiciyapi yuštanpi kin he opaĥta yanke ca , en un kinhan , tuwe naĥon qa akiktonje cin heca šni , tuka wicoĥan econ kin heca , hee e taku econ kin en yawaĥtepi kta .
59001026	Tuwe niyepi kin etanhan woohodapi kin en opa se ececa hecinhan , qa ceji hdaške šni tuka iye cante icihnaye cinhan , he woohodapi ope cin he taku šni .
59001027	Wakantanka qa Ateyapi kin itokam woohodapi opapi ecedan qa ašape šni kin he dee ; Wamdenica qa wiwazica kakijapi eca en wicahipi , qa wicoicage kin en taku iyaonpepica šni ihduhapi kin hee .
59002001	Mihunkawanji , Jesus Messiya , wowitan Itancan wacinyanpi kin , on wicašta iwandakapi kte cin he yuhapi šni po .
59002002	Nitomniciyepi kin en , wicašta wan mazaskazi napcupe yuhe ca wokoyake wašte kicun kin en hi kinhan ; qa nakun wicašta waĥpanica wan heyake šica un kin en hi kinhan ;
59002003	Qa tuwe wokoyake wašte kicun kin he tanyan ayatonwanpi , qa heyakiyapi , Oiyotanke wašte kin de en hiyotanka wo ; qa wicašta waĥpanica qon , Hen najin wo , qa iš , siha wahde kin ihukuya hiyotanka wo , eyakiyapi kinhan ;
59002004	Otoiyohi tanyan canteyeciyuzapi šni , qa wicotawacin šica eciyatanhan widukcanpi šni he .
59002005	Naĥon po , mihunkawanji wašte ; Wakantanka maka akan waĥpanicapi kin hena wicakaĥniga he , wacinyanpi on wijicapi , qa tona iye waštedakapi wokiconze iwahowicaye ciqon he tawayapi kte cin .
59002006	Tuka niye waĥpanicapi kin waĥtewicayadapi šni . Wijicapi kin hen iyotanhan iyeniciyapi šni , qa woyaco oiyotanke kin en aniyanpi šni he .
59002007	Wicaceje wašte on cajeniyatapi ece kin he yašicapi šni he .
59002008	Wowapi kin eciyatanhan , woope iyotan wašte , Nikiyedan un kin niye inihdacin wašteyadake kta ce , eyapi kin he ecen ecanonpi kinhan , tanyan ecanonpi kta .
59002009	Tuka wicašta token ihduze cin ekta eyatonwanpi kinhan , woaĥtani ecanonpi , qa woope kin on šicaya econ oniyakapi ece .
59002010	Tuwe woahope owasin yuha ešta , wanjidan kicakse cinhan , he ocowasin on yacopi .
59002011	Tuwe , Wawiciĥaĥapi ecanon kte šni ce , eye ciqon he iš nakun , Wamayanon kte šni ce , eya . Unkan wawiciĥaĥapi takudan ecanon šni ešta , wamayanon kinhan , wanna woope kin kiyecaksa .
59002012	Tona woope on tawaiciyapi kin on wicayacopi kte cin hena iyecen iapi , qa econ po .
59002013	Tuwe waonšida šni kin he wowaonšida wanin woyaco ecedan qupi kta ; qa wowaonšida woyaco kin kapeya iyuškin ece .
59002014	Mihunkawanji , tuwe wacinyan keya ešta , iyecen wicoĥan yuhe šni kinhan , he taku iyokihi kta he . Wacinyan un kin he niyan okihi he .
59002015	Nihunkawanji qa nitawinoĥtin tancokapidan , qa anpetu iyohi woyute nicapi kinhan ;
59002016	Qa wanji hewicayakiyapi , Wookiye on hdapo , cosiciyapi qa wipiiciya po ; tuka taku wicatancan icakije cin hena wicayaqupi šni ehantanhan , taku iwaštepi kta he .
59002017	He iyecen wacinyanpi kin , wicoĥan codan kinhan , he wanna ta , išnana un kin heon .
59002018	Han , tuwe heye kta ; Niye wacinyan yaun , qa miye wicoĥan mduha ; hecen wacinyaye cin he nioĥan codan makipazo wo , kinhan mioĥan kin on wacinwaye cin he cicipazo kta ce .
59002019	Taku Wakan kin wanjidan he wicayada ; he tanyan ecanon ; taku wakan šicapi kin iš eya wicadapi qa cancanpi ece .
59002020	Tuka , wicašta wacinton šni kin , wacinyanpi wicoĥan codan kin he ta e sdonyaye kta he .
