59002021	Abraham ateunyanpi kin he , cinhintku Isaak wahna wošnapi akan wahdušna qon he ehan , wicoĥan on yaowotanpi šni he .
59002022	Qa iye oĥan kin kici wacinye cin token oĥanye ca , wicoĥan on wacinye ciqon he yuštanpi e wandaka he .
59002023	Unkan hecen wowapi kin , Abraham Wakantanka wicada , unkan he woowotanna kiciyawapi , qa he Wakantanka takicuwa eciyapi ce , eyapi qon he yuecetupi .
59002024	Heon , Wacinyanpi ecedan on etanhan šni , tuka wicoĥan kin on wicašta owatanna yawapi ece he wandakapi .
59002025	Nakun Rahab witkowinna kin ohnihde unpi qon hena iyowinwicakiye ca canku tokeca ohna hde wicaši qehan , iš eya wicoĥan on owatanna yawapi šni he .
59002026	Wicatancan kin woniya codan un kin he ta ece , he iyecen wacinyanpi kin wicoĥan codan kinhan , he nakun ta ece .
59003001	Mihunkawanji , wicota waonspekiya unpi šni po ; woyaco iyotan tanka unkicupi kta e sdonyayapi .
59003002	Owasin taku ota on waunĥtanipi ece . Tuwe oie on waĥtani šni kinhan , he wicašta yuštanpi qa tancan ocowasin hdaške kta okihi .
59003003	Wanyaka po , šuktanka anaungoptanpi kta e heon iikiyuwi i kin en iyewicunkiciyapi ; qa tancanpi ocowasin wicunyuhomnipi ece .
59003004	Wita wata kin hena nakun wanyaka po , tankinkinyan qa tate otikita on kaha iyeyapi ešta , iyupse yuza cistinna on token itancan kin cin eca , yuhomnipi ece .
59003005	He iyecen wicaceji kin taku cistinna , tuka tanka icida ece . Iho , peta cistinna keš can tanka ideya ece .
59003006	Wicaceji kin he peta , qa woaĥtani iyatahdepi ; hecen wicaceji unhuhapi kin ehna un , wicatancan kin ocowasin ašamya , qa wicoicage ohomniyan aideye ca , iš eya wakanšica ti kin etanhan ideiciya .
59003007	Woteca ocaje owasin , qa taku kinyan unpi , taku sdohan unpi qa miniwanca mahen unpi kin , henakiya etanhan wicašta wanunyanpi wicakage ca wicayuha :
59003008	Tuka wicaceji kin he tuwedan yuwaĥbaka okihi šni ; he wošice wicašta šni , pejihuta šica on wicata ece kin he ojudan .
59003009	He on Wakantanka Ateyapi kin unyawaštepi ; qa he on wicašta akantu , Wakantanka ouncage iyecen kagapi kin hena wicunyašicapi ece .
59003010	Wicai wanjidan etanhan wayawaštepi qa wayašicapi kin hinanpa ece . Mihunkawanji , hena hecetu šni .
59003011	Miniyowe wan oenape wanjidan etanhan , mini wašte qa nakun mini pa ĥinca hiyuya he .
59003012	Mihunkawanji , suken can wan Oliwe waskuyeca aicaga , qa iš hastanyanka iyuwi wan suken waskuyeca okihi he ; he iyecen miniyowe wan mini wašte qa nakun mini pa ĥinca hiyuye šni ece .
59003013	Enitanhanpi tuwe wicašta ksape ca wiyukcan un he ; woksape wowaĥbadan on tanyan aihduhe cin eciyatanhan iye oĥan wašte hdutanin kte .
59003014	tuka winawizipi pa ĥinca , qa wakinicapi nicantepi kin en duhapi kinhan , ihnuhan widuškinpi qa wowicake kin on iyatonpi šni kin .
59003015	Wicoksape kin he wankantanhan u šni ; tuka maka kin etanhan , wicaceĥpi etanhan , qa wakanšica iyececa .
59003016	Tukten winawizipi qa wakinicapi yuke cinhan , wicotoketu tanin šni qa wicoĥan šica owasin hen un ece .
59003017	Tuka woksape wankantanhan un kin he tokaheya ecedan , hehan wokiyapi kaga , waĥbadan , waanagoptan , wowaonšida qa waskuyeca wašte on ojudan , owotanna wiyukcan qa owotanna wohdaka ece .
59003018	Unkan tona wookiye kagapi kin hena woowotanna waskuyeca kin wookiye en owicakicijupi ece .
59004001	Niyepi ekta wicokicize qa wakinicapi kin tokiyatanhan u he ; cantiheyayapi šica nihuhapi en wakis un kin hena eciyatanhan šni he .
59004002	Cantiheyayapi tuka duhapi šni ; wicayaktepi qa yuhe wacannipi , tuka icu oyakihipi šni ; wicayakizapi qa zuya dapi , tuka taku duhapi šni , yadapi šni kin heon etanhan .
59004003	Yadapi tuka iyacupi šni ece , ecinšniyan yadapi kin on , cantiheyayapi šica on dusotapi kte cin heon .
59004004	Wiinayaĥmanpi qa wawiciĥaĥapi ecanonpi kin , wicoicage kin de waštedapi kin he Wakantanka šicedaka e sdonyayapi šni he . Heon tuwe wicoicage kin de wotakuye wacin kinhan , he Wakantanka tokaya .
59004005	Wowapi wakan kin , Woniya en unyakonpi kin he winawizipi cantiheya ce , ituya eya idukcanpi he .
59004006	Tuka sanpa wowaonšida wicaqu ece ; heon heya , Wakantanka waĥanicidapi kin wicakipajin , tuka tona onšikiĥanpi kin hena wowaonšida wicaqu ece .
59004007	Heon etanhan , Wakantanka ihukuya iyeiciya po . Wakanšica kipajin po , kinhan nanicipapi kta .
59004008	Wakantanka ikiyedan u po , hecen is nikiyepidan u kta . Waĥtanipi sa , nape hdujaja po ; qa wacin ninonpapi kin , cante hduecepidan po .
59004009	Iyokišicapi , wašihdapi qa ceya po ; iyaĥapi kin he wicaceya ee kta , qa widuškinpi kin he woiyokišice kta .
59004010	Itancan kin itokam makata eĥpeiciya po , kinhan yuwankan inicupi kta .
59004011	Mihunkawanji , otoiyohi akiciiapi šni po . Tuwe hunkawanjitku aie ca hunkawanjitku hdaco kinhan , he woope kin aie ca woope kin yaco ; tuka woope kin daco kinhan , woope kin ecen econpi kin henica šni , tuka wayaco kin henica .
59004012	Woope kage cin he Wanjidan , he wanikiye ca nakun waihangya okihi . Wicašta tokeca daco kin niš nituwe he .
59004013	Iho po , nakaha tona hehapi ; Dehan , qa iš heyakecinhan , otonwe kin kae ekta unyanpi qa waniyetu wanji en unyakonpi kta , wopeuntonpi qa wiyopeunyanpi qa taku unkamnanpi kta ce .
59004014	Tuka heyakecinhan taku u kte cin sdonyayapi šni ; yanipi kin he taku he , opo wan cistiyedan tanin qa hehan atanin šni kin he heca .
59004015	Kaken ehapi kta iyececa ; Itancan kin iyowinunkiyapi qa unnipi kinhan , decen qa iš kaken econkupi kta ce .
59004016	Tuka nakaha waĥannicidapi kin on iduškinpi ; hecen wiyuškinpi kin owasin šica .
59004017	Heon etanhan , tuwe taku wašte econ kta sdonkiya tuka econ šni eca , he woaĥtani icicaga ece .
59005001	Iho po , tona wijica yaunpi kin , wokakije nihiyahdepi kte cin hena on ceyapi qa šicahowaya po .
59005002	Woyuha nitawapi kin kuka , qa nitawokoyake kin wamduškadan yapotapi .
59005003	Mazaskazi qa mazaska nitawapi kin gigi aya ; qa gigi kin he niyutaninpi kta , qa niceĥpipi kin ihangye kta , peta iyececa . Woyuha anpetu ehake kin amnaniciyapi .
59005004	Wanyaka po , tona maga nitawapi abaksapi wokajuju hnaye ayanicapi kin he howaya ; qa tona aguyapi baniciksapi qon hoyeyapi kin he Sabaoth Itancan noge kin en hiyoĥpaya .
59005005	Maka akan woiyokipi imnahan yaunpi qa tanyan wayatapi ece ; wapatapi anpetu kin en iyecen cante cemyakiyapi .
59005006	Wicašta owotanna kin he dacopi qa yaktepi ; tuka nicipajinpi šni .
59005007	Heon etanhan , mihunkawanji , Itancan kin hi kte cin hehanyan wacintanka po . Wanyaka po , wicašta woju ece kin he maka waskuyeca wašte aigage cin hena ape yanke ca , on tehan wacintanka , magaju tokaheya qa nakun ehake kin ahinhe kte cin hehanyan .
59005008	Niš eya wacintanka po ; cante hdusuta po ; Itancan kin u kte cin he wanna kiyedan ihan .
59005009	Mihunkawanji , otoiyohi okiciĥinyanpi šni po , okinni niyacopi kta . Wanyaka po , Wayaco kin he tiyopa kin itokam inajin .
59005010	Mihunkawanji , wicašta wokcan Itancan caje kin on iapi qon hena kakijapi qa wacintankapi on waonspekiya wicayuha po .
59005011	Wanyaka po , tona wacintankaya unpi kin hena wašte kecanwicunkinpi ece . Job token wacintanka qon he nayaĥonpi , qa Itancan owihankeye cin he wandakapi ; Itancan kin waonšida qa wawacinkta yuza tanka .
59005012	Tuka mihunkawanji , taku owasin isanpa , Taku namaĥon ce , eyapi šni po , maĥpiya kin he , qa maka kin de , qa taku tokeca cajeyatapi ece kin nakun ; tuka , han , ehapi kin he han ecedan kta , qa hiya , ehapi kin he hiya ecedan kta ; okinni woyaco kin en iyoyaĥpadapi nun ce .
59005013	Niyepi kin etanhan wanji kakija he ; wocekiye eye kta . Wanji wiyuškin he ; odowan ahiyaye kta .
59005014	Niyepi kin ekta wanji wayazanka he ; okodakiciye kin en hunkawicayapi kin wicakico kta ; on cekiyapi qa Itancan caje kin on wihdi on sdayapi kta .
59005015	Unkan wacinyan cekiyapi kin he wayazanke cin asniye kta ; qa Itancan kin he najinkiye kta ; qa woaĥtani econ hecinhan , hena kicicajujupi kta .
59005016	Wayaĥtanipi kin otoiyohi okiciciyakapi qa otoiyohi wocekiye ekiciciya po , hecen anisnipi kta . Wicašta owatanna nina wašagya cekiye cin he taku tanka okihi ece .
59005017	Elijah wicašta wacinyuza iyeuncecapi , qa wocekiye on magaju kte šni e icekiya ; unkan waniyetu yamni sanpa wi šakpe hehanyan maka kin ahinhe šni .
59005018	Hehan ake wocekiye eya , unkan maĥpiya kin magaju hiyuye ca , maka kin waskuyeca icaĥya .
59005019	Mihunkawanji , wanji enitanhanpi wowicake kin etanhan nuni , qa tuwe he ake ekta yuhomni kinhan ,
59005020	Tuwe wicašta waĥtani sa wan canku onuni kin etanhan yuhomni kinhan , he wicanagi wan wiconte etanhan eyaku kta , qa woaĥtani ota akaĥpe kta e he sdonkiye kta .
60001001	Inyan , Jesus Messiya yeši qon , wicašta toktokeca enanakiya unpi , Pontus , Galatia , Kappadokia , Asia qa Bithunia ekta ,
60001002	Wakantanka Ateyapi kin otokaheya tanhan sdonwicaye cin eciyatanhan , qa Woniya wicayuecedan kta on wicakaĥniga , anagoptanpi kta , qa Jesus we kin awicamnimni kta e on , hena wowapi wicakicaga : Wowaonšida en niunpi , qa wookiye niciyuotapi nunwe .
60001003	Wakantanka , Jesus Messiya Itancan unyanpi Atkuku kin he yawaštepi nunwe ; iye towaonšida ota eciyatanhan Jesus Messiya wicate cin etanhan kinikiye ciqon he on wowacinyan ni un kin en piya icaĥunyanpi ;
60001004	Woaiĥpeye wan ĥwinpica šni , ašapapi šni , qa ohinniyan un kta , maĥpiya ekta enicihnakapi kin on ;
60001005	Wacinyanpi eciyatanhan Wakantanka towašake kin on wiconi anikpatanpi , eqe anpetu ehake kin en yuotaninpi kta .
60001006	Heon nina iduškinpi ece , tuka nakaha ptenyedan , he hecetu naceca , taku wawiyutanyan un kin ota on iyonicišicapi :
60001007	Hecen wacinyayapi iyutanpi kin , he mazaskazi peta ece on šdoyapi keš atakuni šni ece , sam iyeya nina teĥike cin he woyaonihan , wicakinihanpi qa wowitan on tanin kta , tohan Jesus Messiya ihdutanin kinhan .
60001008	He wandakapi šni ešta wašteyadakapi ; qa nakaha wanyake šni yaunpi keš wacinyayapi kin on iduškinpi , wowiyuškin oyagpica šni qa wowitan ojudan kin on :
60001009	Wacinyayapi ihanke kin iyacupi , ninagipi ni kte cin hee .
60001010	Wiconi kin he on , wicašta wokcan wowaonšida en niunpi kin he oyakapi qehan , aiciciya akitapi qa wiwangapi ;
60001011	Messiya Taniya iyepi en un kin , tohantu qa anpetu kin tukte e ka e iwangapi , Messiya kakije kte ca wowitan ihakam un kte cin hena itokamoyake ciqon he ehan .
60001012	Unkan , iš iyepi kte šni , tuka tona wotanin wašte , Woniya Wakan maĥpiya eciyatanhan kun u šipi kin iyahna sdonyeniyanpi kin eqe nakaha taku oniciyakapi kin hena unkiyepi on yuhapi e owicakiyakapi ; taku kin hena maĥpiya ohnihde kin en eyokasin wacinpi .
60001013	Heon etanhan , nitawacin nisehu kin opta ipiyagkiton po , waktaya un po , qa Jesus Messiya ihdutanin kinhan wowašte nicaupi kte cin he ape yukan po , owihanke kin hehanyan .
60001014	Wicacinca waanagoptanpi kin iyenicecapi kta , qa ehanna wasdonye šni yaunpi qehan cantiheyayapi šica ake iyecen nicicagapi kte šni .
60001015	Tuka tuwe nicopi kin he wakan , he iyecen niš eya oyaĥandapi kin ocowasin en niwakanpi nunwe .
60001016	Heon hecen owapi qon , Wakanyan un po , miye mawakan kin heon etanhan .
60001017	Qa Ateyapi kin wicašta itohnake iwanyake šni wicašta otoiyohi iye oĥan kin eciyatanhan wicayukcan ece kin he hoyeyakiyapi kinhan , tohanyan den unhdaka yaunpi kin kokipeyahan un po .
60001018	Witkotkoya oyaĥandapi kin , nihunkakepi wohdakapi eciyatanhan duhapi qon he etanhan , taku atakunišni ece , mazaskazi qa mazaska on openicitonpi šni e sdonyakiyapi ;
60001019	Tuka Messiya we teĥike cin he on , taĥin wanunyanpi cincadan , taku iyaonpepica šni qa ecedan un kin iyececa .
60001020	Iye qe maka kin de kagapi šni itokam wakiconzapi , tuka anpetu ihankeya kin dena en yutaninpi , niyepi kin on ;
60001021	Wakantanka wicate cin etanhan najinkiye ca wowitan qu qon he wicayadapi , iye eciyatanhan ; hecen wicayadapi qa wacinyayapi kin he Wakantanka en un kta .
60001022	Woniya kin eciyatanhan wowicake anayagoptanpi kin heon nagi nihduskapi , hunkawanjinkiciyapi kin awicakehan waštewicayadakapi kta , heon cante ecedan on otoiyohi nina waštekicidaka po .
60001023	Piya icaĥniyanpi , oicage kuke kte cin etanhan šni , tuka kukepica šni kin on , Wakantanka oie kin ni un qa owihanke wanice kte cin hee on .
60001024	Wicaceĥpi owasin peji iyececa , qa wicašta towitan kin owasin peji ĥca kin iyececa . Peji kin he šniš aye ca waĥca kin hinĥpaya ece ;
60001025	Tuka Itancan oie kin he owihanke wanin un kta . Unkan wotanin wašte oniciyakapi kin wicoie kin he hee .
60002001	Heon etanhan , wocanniye owasin , qa wohnaye ocowasin , qa woanakiĥbe , qa wowinawizi , qa iapi šica iyuĥpa eĥpeya po ;
60002002	Qa hokšiyoqopa nakaha tonpi kin iyecen , wicoie asanpi wohnaye wanin un kin he cin po , hecen on inicagapi kta :
60002003	Itancan kin wacantkiya e uyatapi hecinhan .
60002004	He en yahipi , inyan wan ni un kin iyececa , wicašta akantu eĥpeyapi , tuka Wakantanka e kaĥnige ca teĥike daka ;
60002005	Unkan niš eya , inyan ni un kin iyececa , tipi wakan wan en icaĥniyanpi , wawayušnapi wakan kin , hecen wošnapi wakan qa Jesus Messiya eciyatanhan Wakantanka iyokipi kin wadušnapi kta .
60002006	Heon etanhan nakun wowapi en kagapi qon , Wanyaka po , Zion en inyan wan oise pa ĥinca ewahde , kaĥnigapi , teĥika ; unkan tuwe he wacinye cinhan wištece kte šni ce .
60002007	Niye wacinyayapi kin he teĥike yadapi ; tuka tona waanagoptanpi šni kin hena , inyan tipi kagapi eĥpeyapi qon he oise pa ĥinca icaga , inyan on siha ibotopi qa imnija on šinhdapi ece kin hee ;
60002008	Tona wicoie kin on šinhdapi qa waanagoptan šni unpi kin hena on ; heon hecen ewicahdepi .
60002009	Tuka wicoicage kaĥnigapi , wawayušnapi wicaštayatapi , wicoun wakan , qa oyate opewicakitonpi kin he niyepi ; hecen tuwe otapaza etanhan , iye iyoyanpa wakan tawa kin en nicopi kin he oĥan wašte kin odakapi kta .
60002010	Ehanna oyate henicapi šni , tuka nakaha Wakantanka taoyate yaunpi ; he ehan onšinidapi šni , tuka wanna wowaonšida iyoyahipi .
60002011	Waštecicidapi , ceciciyapice , oyate tokeca qa unhdaka unpi kin iyecen wicaceĥpi cantiheyapi kin , wicanagi kin kici kicize cin , hena ayuštan po :
60002012	Qa Ikcewicašta ehna owotanna oĥanyan po ; hecen šicaya econ keniciyapi keš , wiwicawangapi anpetu kin en , nioĥanpi wašte wanyakapi kte cin hena on Wakantanka yaonihanpi kta .
60002013	Itancan kin on etanhan , wicašta akantu wakonzapi kin owasin anagoptan po ; wicaštayatapi kin he iyotan tanka ;
60002014	Qa wicašta itancanpi kin iš tona šicaya oĥanyanpi šitkihdawicayapi kta , qa tona tanyan econpi wicayaonihanpi kta e on u wicaši kin hena .
60002015	Hecen Wakantanka tawcin , tanyan oyaĥandapi kin on wicašta witkotkoka wiyukcan šni kin hena inina yankewicayakiyapi kta .
60002016	Nihduhapi , tuka tawaniciyapi kin he wocanniye onĥoĥda iyecen yecunpi kte šni , tuka Wakantanka tawowidake kin iyececa .
60002017	Owasin wicayuonihan po . Hunkawanjinkiciyapi kin waštekida po . Wakantanka kokipa po . Wicaštayatapi kin yuonihan po .
60002018	Wowidake yaunpi kin , tona niyuhapi kin ocowasin kokipeyahan anawicagoptan po , tona wašte qa waĥbadan kin hecedan šni , tuka tona ksizece cin hena nakun .
60002019	Tuwe Wkantanka awacin un kin on , hecetu šni ešta kakišyapi qa woiyokišice yuha un kinhan , he wowašte .
60002020	Wayaĥtanipi kin on anipapi , qa wacinnitankapi kinhan taku iyokihi kta he ; tuka tanyan ecanonpi kin on kakišniyanpi kinhan , wacinnitankapi hecinhan , he Wakantanka iyokipi .
60002021	Unkan he on nicopi ; Messiya unkiyepi on kakije ca woonspe aiĥpeunkiyapi kin he iyecen niš eya iye owe kin en opa dapi kta .
60002022	Iye qe woaĥtani takudan econ šni , qa i kin ohna wohnaye takudan iyeyapi šni ;
60002023	Kigepi qehan itkom wicakige šni ; kakišyapi he ehan owawicakiye šni ; tuka tuwe owotanna wiyukcan ece kin he en ihdoya .
60002024	Iye ĥinca can akan un qehan , iye tancan kin en waunĥtanipi kin yuha ; hecen unkiye woaĥtani eĥpeunyanpi woowotanna en unnipi kta : Iye apapi qon on asniniyanpi ce .
60002025	Taĥin wanunyanpi nunipi kin iyenicecapi ; tuka wanna tuwe wonniyanpi qa nagi awanniyakapi kin he ekta yahdipi .
60003001	He iyecen , winoĥincapi kin , nihihnapi wicihukun un po ; hecen tona wicoie kin anagoptanpi šni kin hena , wicoie codan ešta , iye tawicupi oĥanpi kin on iyakapewicayapi kta ;
60003002	Nioĥanpi wašte wokokipe iyahna wanyakapi kin icunhan .
60003003	Ihduzapi kin he akantanhan , paha kisonpi , qa mazaskazi oinpi , qa wokoyake unpi kin hee kte šni :
60003004	Tuka wicašta mahentanhan cante kin ekta , taku ĥwinpica šni kin , tawacin waĥbadan qa inina un , he Wakantanka itoham taku teĥike cin ee .
60003005	Iš eya , wanakaja , winoĥinca waštešte Wakantanka wacinyanpi qon hena e hecen kicunpi , qa hihnakupi kin wicihukun unpi .
60003006	Hecen Sara Abraham anakigoptan , qa , Itancan , eciya ece ; he cunkšiwicaye cin hena niyepi , tanyan ecanonpi qa wokokipe takudan on niyušinyayapi šni kinhan .
60003007	Nakun wicašta yaunpi kin , wosdonye eciyatanhan om yukan po , nitawinpi wakšica wankadan iyececa , qa om wiconi wowašte kin tawaniciyapi kta iyecen wicahduonihan po ; hecen wocekiye nitawapi kin kagipi kte šni .
60003008	Ehake , owasin cante wanjidan hduwitaya onšikicida po ; hunkawanjinkiciyapi kin iyecen waštekicida po , waonšidapi qa wacantkiya po .
60003009	Taku šica on itkom taku šica econpi šni po ; qa nicigepi ešta wicakigepi šni po ; tuka itkopatanhan wayawašte po ; heon nicopi , hecen woyawašte tawayayapi kta e sdonya po .
60003010	Tuwe wiconi waštedake ca anpetu wašte wanyaka cin kinhan , iye ceji kin taku šica en yeye kte šni , qa iha kin wohnaye takudan ie kte šni .
60003011	Taku šice cin okamna kta , qa taku wašte e econ kta ; wookiye akite ca kuwa aye kta ce .
60003012	Jehowa išta kin wicašta owotanna awicatonwan , qa wocekiye eyapi kin he anoĥwicakiciya ; tuka tona šicaya econpi kin Jehowa itohnake kin itkowicakipa ece .
60003013	Unkan taku wašte kin pasi yaunpi kinhan , tuwe e kiunniniyanpi kta he .
60003014	Tuka owotanna oĥanyanpi kin on šicaya nicuwapi kinhan , he wowašte ; hecen wokokipe tawapi kin kokipapi šni , qa cante hahayedan yankapi šni po ;
60003015	Tuka nicantepi kin en Wankantanka Itancan kin wakanda po ; qa tuwe wowacinye en niunpi kin on iniwangapi kinhan , waĥbayedan kokipeyahan aduptapi kta e ohinniyan wiyeya yanka po ;
60003016	Wawiyukcan wašte hduha po ; hecen šicaya oĥanyanpi iyecen tona anniiapi kin hena ištecapi kta , Messiya on nionĥanpi wašte kin itonšniyan oniyakapi kin .
60003017	Wakantanka hecen tawacin hecinhan , taku šica econpi kin hee šni , tuka taku wašte econpi kin on kakišniyanpi kinhan hee wašte kta .
60003018	Messiya iš eya wancadan woaĥtani on kakija , owotanna un kin owotanpidan šni kin hena on , Wakantanka ekta unkaunpi kta e heon , wicaceĥpi kicun ktepi , tuka Woniya kin on kiniyanpi .
60003019	Nakun he on ekta ye ca wicanagi wicakaĥka tipi ohna unpi kin hena wowicakiyaka ;
60003020	Hena e ehanna waanagoptanpi šni , Wakantanka wawacinkta yuza tanka tehan awicape , Nowa taanpetu kin en , wita wata kagapi kin icunhan , he ohna tonana , wicanagi šahdoganna mini on nipi .
60003021	Qa wiyacinpi kin he iyececa , baptem nakaha niunyanpi ece ; wicaceĥpi ašape cin yutokan iyeyapi kin hee šni , tuka Wakantanka ekta waiyukcan wašte waayupte cin hee , Jesus Messiya ihduekicetu kin heon etanhan ;
60003022	Iye qe maĥpiya kin ekta kihde ca Wakantanka etapa kin eciyatanhan yanka ; maĥpiya ohnihde , qa wicookihi , qa wowašake kin owasin iye ihukun iyewicayapi .
60004001	Heon etanhan , Messiya wicaceĥpi en unkiyepi on kakije cin heon , niš eya iyecen tawacin kicun po : tuwe wicaceĥpi kin en kakije cin he wanna woaĥtani ayuštan :
60004002	Hecen , hetanhan icimana wicaceĥpi eciyatanhan ni kte šni , wicašta taku šica cantiheyapi kin en , tuka Wakantanka tawacin kin eciyatanhan .
60004003	Hekta unnipi kin , Ikcewicašta tawacinpi kin ecen econkupi kin he ota , wicoĥan šica , wocantiheye šica , miniša ota , wakan wacipi , witkopi , qa wakagapi wakandapi šice cin hena omaunnipi qehan .
60004004	He en iš iye witkoya škanpi kin on iyecen iyatahdeniciyapi šni kin heon tognihdapi qa niyašicapi ece ;
60004005	Hena e tuwe ni unpi tapi koya wicayaco kta wiyeya yanke cin hee itokam wohdakapi kta .
60004006	Heon etanhan , nakun tona tapi kin hena wotanin wašte owicakiyakapi qon , hecen wicašta wicaceĥpi en un kin iyecen wicayacopi ešta woniya en Wakantanka eciyatanhan nipi kta .
60004007	Tuka taku owasin ecadan owihanke kta . Heon etanhan wacinksapa po , qa wocekiye on waktaya un po .
60004008	Qa taku owasin isanpa niye iyakitedan nina cantekiciya po ; wacantkiyapi kin he woaĥtani ota akaĥpe kta .
60004009	Iapi šica wanin otoiyohi wonkiciya po .
60004010	Taku wicaqupi kin wicašta otoiyohi icu kin he iyecen iyakitedan okinikiciciya po , tona Wakantanka towaonšida ocaje ota tanyan yuhapi kin iyececa .
60004011	Tuwe ie cinhan Wakantanka oie kin iyecece kta ; qa tuwe waokiya hecinhan wookihi Wakantanka qu kin he eciyatanhan kte ; hecen taku owasin on Wakantanka yatanpi kta , Jesus Messiya eciyatanhan ; iye qe woyatan qa wookihi owihanke wanin kiciun nunwe . Amen .
60004012	Waštecicidapi kin , ptea on iyutanpi kin on iniyutanpi kte cin he on yušinyayapi šni po , taku tokeca ayakipapi iyececa .
60004013	Tuka Messiya kakije ciqon en oyapapi kin heon iyuškin po ; hecen tohan towitan tanin kinhan nina iduškinpi kta .
60004014	Messiya caje kin on niyašicapi kinhan , niyuwaštepi ece ; wowitan qa Wakantanka Taniya kin en niunpi kin heon . Hena e eciyatanhan oštehdapi , tuka niye eciyatanhan yatanpi ece .
60004015	Tuka ihnuhan wanji tin wicakte sa , qa wamanon sa , qa taku šica econ sa , qa tokan tawa i en iyewicakiciciye cin iyecen kakišniyanpi kinhan .
60004016	Hececa ešta tuwe Messiya tawa kin on kakišyapi kinhan ištece kte šni ; tuka heon Wakantanka yatan kta .
60004017	Wakantanka tiyohnaka tawa kin wicayukcanpi kte cin wanna iyehantu . Unkan he unkiyepi etanhan aye cinhan , tona Wakantanka tawootanin wašte wicadapi šni kin hena token owihankepi kta he .
60004018	Qa wicašta owotanna kin kitan se ni kinhan , tuwe šicaya econ qa waĥtani sa kin hena tukten yakonpi kta he .
60004019	Heon etanhan , tona Wakantanka eciyatanhan kakijapi kin hena , wašte ece econpi kin en , Wawicaĥye wacinyepica kin iyecen iye nagipi kin yuhekiyapi kte .
60005001	Miye hunkayapi kin hemaca , qa Messiya kakije ciqon wanmdake ca , wowitan yutaninpi kte cin he en owapa , tona hunkayapi yaunpi kin ceciciyapi ce ;
60005002	Wakantanka optaye tawa ehna yaunpi kin he wonwicaya po ; econ niciyapi kin iyecece šni , tuka iyokipiya awanwicadakapi kta ; woyuha šica kin on etanhan šni , tuka tawacin wašte on ecanonpi kta :
60005003	Wakantanka taku tawa ĥince cin en itancanpi kin eyenicecapi kte šni , tuka optaye kin en waonspekiya yaunpi kta .
60005004	Hecen Waawanhdake Itancan kin tohan ihdutanin kinhan , hehan wowitan watešdake wan šnije kte šni kin he iyacupi kta .
60005005	Nakun , tona aškatudan yaunpi kin , hunkawicayapi kin anawicagoptan po : Han , owasin otoiyohi anakicigoptan po , qa wowaĥbadan koyaka po . Tona waĥanicidapi kin hena Wakantanka wicakipajin , tuka tona onšikiĥanpi kin hena wowaonšida wicaqu ece .
60005006	Heon etanhan , Wakantanka nape wašake cin ihukuya onšikiĥan po ; hecen tohan iyehantu kinhan yuwankan inicupi kta :
60005007	Wacin akipam duzapi kin owasin iye en aiĥpeya po ; iye qe awanicinpi ece .
60005008	Witkopi šni po , waktaya un po ; Wakanšica tokaniyanpi kin he mnaja hoton ece kin iyecen omani un , tuwe yapote kte cin he akita ece .
60005009	Sutaya wacinyayapi kin on he kipajin po ; nihunkawanjipi maka akan unpi kin hena en wokakije kin dena iyececa yuštanpi ece e sdonyayapi .
60005010	Tuka Wakantanka wowaonšida ocowasin hduhe cin , Jesus Messiya eciyatanhan , wowitan owihanke wanica iye tawa kin en unkicopi kin he , tohan cistiyedan nicakijapi kinhan , niyuštanpi kte , pahohošni enihnakapi , niyuwašakapi , qa sutaya nihdepi nunwe .
60005011	Iye qe wowitan qa wokiconze kin owihanke wanin tawa nunwe . Amen .
60005012	Siluanos nihunkawanjipi wan wacinyepica wadake cin on wowapi ptecedan cicagapi ; wahokonciciyapi qa wociciyakapi , Wakantanka towašte wicakapi en nayajinpi kin he dee ce .
60005013	Babulon ekta tona om nicaĥnigapi kin hena nape niyuzapi , qa nakun Markos micinkši kin .
60005014	Wacantkiyapi iiputakapi kin on otoiyohi nape kiciyuza po . Tona Jesus Messiya en yaunpi kin owasin wookiye nicipi un nunwe . Amen .
61001001	Simon Inyan , Jesus Messiya tawowidake qa yeši qon he , tona Wakantanka unkitawapi toowotanna kin on , qa Jesus Messiya Wanikiye cin eciyatanhan , unkiye unhapi kin eyecen wowacinye teĥika yuhapi kin hena wowapi wicakicaga .
61001002	Wowaonšida , wookiye ko , Wakantanka sdonyapi kin en , qa Jesus Itancan unkiyapi kin on niciyuotapi nunwe .
61001003	Iye towašake wakan kin he taku on wiconi qa woohodapi kte cin owasin unqupi kin he iyececa , tuwe wowitan qa wookihi on unkicopi kin he sdonyapi kin eciyatanhan .
61001004	Hena on taku tanka ĥinca , qa taku teĥike ĥinca iwahounyanpi ; hecen hena on Taku Wakan ouncage kin en oyapapi kta , wiconi kin de en wocantiheye šica on wicošice nayecipapi kin .
61001005	Qa nakun he on nina mniheiciya po , wacinyayapi kin en waditakapi kin ikoyagya po ; qa waditakapi kin en wosdonye ;
61001006	Qa wosdonye kin en iyatahdeiciyapi šni ; qa iyatahdeiciyapi šni kin en wacintankapi ; qa wacintankapi kin en taku wakan iyececapi ;
61001007	Qa taku wakan iyecepi kin en waštekicidapi ; qa waštekicidapi kin en wacantkiyapi ikoyagya po .
61001008	Hena taku kin en niunpi qa niciyuotapi kinhan , Jesus Messiya Itancan unkiyapi sdonyapi kin en taku icaĥye ca waskuyeca aicage cin henicapi kta e nicagapi .
61001009	Tuka tuwe dena yuhe šni kinhan , he ištagonge ca tehan wawanyaka okihi šni , qa waĥtani qon hena kipakintapi kin he akiktonja .
61001010	Heon etanhan , mihunkawanji , nicopi qa nicaĥnigapi kin aiciciya hdusuta po ; hena hecen ecanonpi kinhan icimana nihinĥpayapi kte šni .
61001011	Qa nakun heon Jesus Messiya Itancan qa Wanikiya unkitawapi tokiconze owihanke wanice cin en yaipi kte cin wijinya nicupi kta .
61001012	Heon etanhan taku hececa ohinniyan kiksuyeciciyapi kta awektonje kte šni , hena niye ĥinca sdonyayapi , qa nakaha wowicake kin de en sutaya nihdepi ešta .
61001013	Tohanyan wakeya kin de ohna waun kin hehanyan kiksuyeciciyapi kin on iyocipaštakapi kte cin he hecetu wadake :
61001014	Wakeya mitawa kin de aškadan wehnake kta sdonwakiya , Jesus Messiya Itancan unkiyapi omakiyake ciqon iyececa .
61001015	Tuka nakun detanhan imdamde cin iyohakam , taku kin dena ohinniyan yeksuya oyakihipi kta e awakite kta .
61001016	Jesus Messiya Itancan unkiyapi towašake qa hi kte cin hena unkoniciyakapi qehan , hitunkakanpi ksamya kagapi kin unkunpi šni , tuka iye tanka ĥince cin he išta on wanunyakapi .
61001017	Wakantanka Ateya cin eciyatanhan woyuonihan wowitan ko icu , wowitan wašte kin etanhan wicaho kin de hiyu qehan , Micinkši waštewakidake cin he dee , on iyomakipi ĥinca ce .
61001018	Unkan wicaho kin he maĥpiya eciyatanhan u kin he naunĥonpi , paha wakan kin akan kici unyakonpi qehan .
61001019	Tuka wokcanpi oie iyotan suta wan unhapi ; he qe anayagoptanpi kinhan tanyan ecanonpi kta , petijanjan tukten otpaze cin en ijanjan kin iyececa , nicantepi kin ekta anpao kamdeze ca , en anpao wicanĥpi kin hinanpe kte cin hehanyan .
61001020	Qa de tokaheya sdonya po , wowapi wakan kin en wokcanpi kin owasin tuwedan iye cinka oyake šni .
61001021	Wokcanpi kin wanakajatanhan wicašta tawacin kin eciyatanhan u šni ; tuka wicašta wakan Wakantanka tawa Woniya Wakan kin token iewicakiye ciqon hena hecen eyapi ece .
61002001	Tuka he ehan oyate kin ehan wicašta wokcan itonpi šni yukan qon , he iyecen niyepi kin ehan waonspekiya itonpi šni kin heca yuke kta , naĥmana wohnuni woihangye kin en aupi kta , Itancan opewicakiton qon he eĥpeyapi , qa wicotakunišni oĥanko amnaiciyapi kta .
61002002	Qa wicoĥan šica econpi kin en wicota opapi kta ; hena on wowicake canku kin yašicapi ece e kta .
61002003	Qa waicu wacinpi kin eciya tanhan wicoie skuya on wiyopeniyanpi kta ; hena e wicayacopi kin wanakajatanhan en awicau , qa ihangwicayapi kte cin he ĥba šni .
61002004	Wakantanka maĥpiya ohnihde waĥtanipi qon hena wicakpatan šni , tuka wakanšica ti kin ekta iyayewicaya , qa woyaco kte cin hehanyan wicayuhapi kta e otpaza maza icicaĥiĥa on wicakaška hecinhan ;
61002005	Qa maka tannike cin kpatan šni , tuka Nowa wicašta wicišahdogan wicoowotanna oyake cin he kpatan , qa wicoicage waĥtanipi sa amnitanwicaya ;
61002006	Qa Sodom qa Gomorra otonwe kin caĥota kaĥya eĥpewicaye , woihangye on wicayaco , qa tona tokata waĥtani sa unpi kte cin hena woonspe wicakicaga ;
61002007	Qa Lot owotanna un , wicašta waĥtepi šni oĥan šicapi kin wacin iyowicakišica ece kin he ehdaku :
61002008	Wicašta owotanna kin he hena wicehna ti , qa taku wanyake ca naĥon kin on , anpetu eca iye nagi owotanna ekta wacin iyowicakišica ece , šicaya oĥanyanpi kin on :
61002009	Itancan kin wicašta wašte wowiyutanye kin etanhan token ewicaĥdaku kta sdonya , qa nakun wicaĥta owotanna šni kin woyaco anpetu kin hehanyan wicayuhe kta , šitkihdawicayapi kta e heon :
61002010	Tuka tona woašamye cantiheyapi kin en wicaceĥpi eciyatanhan manipi , qa wokiconze waĥtedapi šni kin hena iyotan : hena waĥanicidapi qa wamnaicidapi ece ; qa tona tankapi kin wicayašicapi kokipapi šni .
61002011	Maĥpiya ohnihde kin , wookihi qa wowašake on iyotanpi qeyaš , Itancan kin itokam wayašicapi woyaco kin en awicayapi šni ece .
61002012	Tuka dena iš , woteca iyececa , wicayuzapi qa ihangwicayapi kta e on wicakagapi kin , taku okaĥnigapi šni keš he yašicapi ece ; qa wicotakunišni tawapi kin en ihangiciyapi kta ;
61002013	Qa anpetu icunhan tanyan wotapi kin he woiyokipi dakapi kin heon woaĥtani iyunwin kin icupi kta . Hena om wayatapi icunhan wohnayeiciyapi kin on iyuškinpi , woašape qa taku samya wanke cin hecapi ;
61002014	Išta yukanpi wiinaĥmanpi kin on ojudan qa woaĥtani ayuštanpica šni ; wicanagi kacegya unpi kin hena wicahnayanpi ece ; cante wawicakipi e ecewakta kin heca yuhapi , wicotakunišni cincapi kin :
61002015	Canku owotanna kin ayuštanpi , qa onuniyata unpi , Balaam Bosor cinhintku woaĥtani iyunwin waštedake ciqon he tacanku kin en opapi :
61002016	Iye takue šica econ qon on iyopeyapi ; šonšonna kin ia okitpani ece wicaho on ie ca , wicašta wokcan witkotkoya oĥanye cin he kišica .
61002017	Miniyowe mini wanica , maĥpiya šapa tate iyumni on toke cincin eyaye cin hena hecapi ; hena on otpaza sape ĥinca owihanke wanica wickicihnakapi .
61002018	Waĥanĥanicidaya takušnišni eyapi eca , wicaceĥpi cantiheyapi kin eciyatanhan , witkoya oĥanyanpi kin on , tona wohnaye en ounyanpi kin kitan ecinyan nawicakicipapi qon hena iyakapewicayapi ece .
61002019	Tawaiciyapi kin wicaqupi kta keyapi , tuka iyepi kaeš wicotakunišni iwicadaka . Taku on tuwe iyakapeyapi kinhan , he on wowidagyapi ece .
61002020	Itancan qa Wanikiya Jesus Messiya sdonyapi kin eciyatanhan , wicoicage kin de en woanšape kin nakipapi ešta , ake hena on iyakapeyapi qa en ihdaškapi kinhan , hena otokahe ekta wašte qa owihankepi kin he šica ece .
61002021	Woowotanna canku kin he sdonyapi šni unkanš he wašte kta tuka , qa he sdonyapi qa woahope wakan wicaqupi kin ayuštanpi kin he šice ĥinca .
61002022	Tuka wiyacinpi eyapi wicakapi kin he iyecen waakipapi ; Sunka taku hiyuye cin he ake hduta ce ; qa , Kukuše yujajapi qon he ake upšija en iwanka ce .
61003001	Waštecicidapi kin , de nakaha wowapi inonpa cicagapi ; hena en nitawacinpi mdesahan kiksuyapi on iyocipaštakapi .
61003002	Hecen wicašta wokcan wakan token oieyapi qon , qa nakun unkiye Itancan qa Wanikiya yeunšipi qon token econ unnišipi kin hena yeksuyapi kta .
61003003	Qa de tokaheya sdonya po , anpetu ehake kin en waiĥaĥapi , iye cantiheyapi šica eciyatanhan manipi kin heca hipi kta ;
61003004	Qa heyapi kta ; Hi kta keyapi qon he tukte e he ; wicahunkake ištinma iĥpayapi ehantanhan otokaheya tanhan taku owasin tokeca šni wanka ce .
61003005	Tuka he de sdonyapi šni , Wakantanka oie kin eciyatanhan maĥpiya kin ehanna un , qa maka kin mini mahen qa nakun mini akan han ;
61003006	Qa nakun he eciyatanhan , maka ehanna un qon he mini apašbog hiyaye ca ihangya .
61003007	Tuka maĥpiya qa maka nakaha un kin hena iye oie kin on kihnakapi , peta on ayuhapi , woyaco anpetu qa wicašta šica šitkihdawicayapi kte cin hehantu .
61003008	Tuka , waštecicidapi kin , he de sdonye šni yukanpi šni po , Itancan kin ekta anpetu wanjidan waniyetu kektopawinge iyececa , qa waniyetu kektopawinge anpetu wanjidan iyececa ece .
61003009	Itancan kin taku wahowicaye cin yutehan šni , wicašta wanjikši yutehanpi eyapi kin iyececa ; tuka unkiyepi on wawacinkta yuza tanka , tuwedan awihnuniiciye kte šni , tuka owasin woiyopeiciye en ihdoupi kta cin .
61003010	Tuka Itancan taanpetu kin wamanon sa wan hanyen hi ece kin he iyecen u kta , hehan maĥpiya kin ĥmunĥmunyan hinhda on tokan iyaye kta , qa taku kin peta ĥinca on skan kta ; qa maka kin wicoĥan ohna un kin hena ĥuĥnage kta .
61003011	Hena taku kin owasin hecen skan kta hecinhan , wicoĥan wašte qa Taku Wakan iyececapi kin en taku wicašta yaunpi kta iyececa he :
61003012	Wakantanka taanpetu u kte cin he ayapepi qa on inayaĥnipi kta ; he en maĥpiya kin aide ecen atakuni kte šni , qa taku kin peta tanka ĥinca on skan kta .
61003013	Hececa ešta , unkiye , iye wahounyanpi kin eciyatanhan , maĥpiya teca qa maka teca en woowotanna ounye cin he wanunyakapi kta e unkapepi .
61003014	Heon etanhan , waštecicidapi kin , taku hececa ayapepi kin heon aiciciya po , hecen iye wookiye en ešape šni qa iyaonpepicašni iyeniyanpi kta .
61003015	Qa Itancan wawacinkta yuza tanka kin he wiconi kecankin po ; Palos , hunkawanjinun yanpi wašte kin , iš eya woksape qupi kin eciyatanhan , wowapi nicagapi kin iyececa ;
61003016	He wowapi kage cin owasin en taku hececa cajeyata ece ; hena wanjikši okaĥniĥ teĥika , tona onspepi šni qa kaktihanhan unpi kin yatokecapi , wowapi unma kin iyececa , iye ihdutakunipi kte šni heon .
61003017	Heon etanhan , waštecicidapi kin , niš niyepi hena itoham sdonyayapi , heon ihnuhan wicašta šica wohnaye kagapi kin nihnayanpi , qa sutaya nihdepi kin etanhan nihinĥpayapi kinhan .
61003018	Tuka wowašte kin en , qa nakun Itancan unyanpi Wanikiya Jesus Messiya sdonyapi kin en icaga po . Iye kin wowitan nakaha qa owihanke wanica kiciun nunwe . Amen .
62001001	Taku otokaheya tanhan un , taku naunĥonpi , qa išta on wanunyakapi , oaunĥtapi qa nape on unzapi , Wiconi Oie kin hee .
62001002	Wiconi kin he ihdutanin ; unkan Wiconi Owihanke Wanica Ateyapi kin kici un , qa unkiyepi kin en ihdutanin qon he wanunyakapi , qa unyaotaninpi qa unkoniciyakapi .
62001003	Taku wanunyakapi qa naunĥonpi kin he unkoniciyakapi , hecen niye unyecicapi kta ; unkan awicakehan Ateyapi kin kici okiciciya unyakonpi , qa nakun iye Cinhintku Jesus Messiya kici .
62001004	Unkan nitowiyuškinpi kin yucopi kta e heon dena decen wowapi unnicagapi .
62001005	Hehan wotanin wašte iye eciyatanhan naunĥonpi qa unkoniciyakapi kin , Wakantanka he iyoyanpa , qa otpaza takudan en un šni kin he hee .
62001006	Iye kici okiciciya unyakonpi ce , unkeyapi qa otpaza kin omaunnipi kinhan , unkitonpišni qa wowicake kin econkupi šni ece .
62001007	Tuka iye iyoyanpa en un kin he iyecen iyoyanpa kin en maunnipi kinhan , otoiyohi okiciciya unyakonpi , qa iye Cinhintku Jesus Messiya we kin he woaĥtani owasin unkipakintapi kta .
62001008	Woaĥtani unnicapi ce , unkeyapi kinhan , unkicihnayanpi qa wowicake kin unkiyepi en un šni .
62001009	Tuka waunĥtanipi kin unkohdakapi kinhan , iye kin wacinyepica qa owotanna un , hecen woaĥtani yutokan iyeunkiciciyapi kta , qa taku šica owasin unkipakintapi kta .
62001010	Eca waunĥtanipi šni ce , unkeyapi kinhan , iye itonšni undakapi , qa iye oie kin unkiyepi en un šni ece .
62002001	Micinca cikcistinpidan wayaĥtanipi kte šni e heon dena decen wowapi cicagapi . Unkan tuwe waĥtani kinhan Ateyapi kin ekta Wawiciya wan unhapi , Jesus Messiya owotanna kin hee .
62002002	Unkan waunĥtanipi wokajuju kin he iye ; qa unkiye unkitawapi kin hecedan šni , tuka maka kin owancaya woaĥtani econpi kin hena .
62002003	Unkan deciyatanhan iye kin wanna sdonunyanpi e sdonunkiyapi , tawoahope unkokicipapi kinhan .
62002004	Tuwe , He sdonwaya ce , eye ca tawoahope okicipe šni kin he itonšni , qa wowicake kin en un šni .
62002005	Tuka tuwe iye oie kin okicipe cinhan , awicakehan he en Wakantanka waštedake cin yuecetupi . Heciyatanhan iye kin en unyakonpi kin sdonunkiyapi ece .
62002006	Tuwe he kici un keye cinhan , iye token omani qon iš iyecen omani kta iyececa .
62002007	Mihunkawanji , woahope teca wan cicagapi šni , tuka woahope tanina , otokaheya tanhan duhapi qon hee . Woahope tanina kin wicoie otokahe ekta nayaĥonpi qon he hee .
62002008	Hehan akeš woahope teca wan cicagapi ; he iye kin en wowicake , qa nakun niyepi kin en ; otpaze cin he wanna henakeca , qa iyoyanpa wicake cin he wanna tanin kin heon etanhan .
62002009	Tuwe iyoyanpa kin en un keiciye ca , hunkawanjitku kin šicekidake cin he dehantu otpaza kin en un .
62002010	Tuwe hunkawanjitku waštekidake cin he iyoyanpa kin en un ece , qa wokašeye takudan en un šni .
62002011	Tuka tuwe hunkawanjitku šicekidake cin he otpaza en un , qa otpaza omani , qa tokiya ye cin sdonkiye šni , išta kin otpaza kašeya , heon etanhan .
62002012	Hokšiyopa cikcistinpidan , iye caje kin on wayaĥtanipi kin nicigajujupi kin heon wowapi cicagapi .
62002013	Hunkakeniyanpi kin , tuwe otokaheya tanhan un kin he sdonyayapi kin heon wowapi cicagapi . Koškapi kin , tuwe šice cin he ohiyayapi kin heon wowapi cicagapi .
62002014	Hokšiyopa cikcistinpidan , Ateyapi kin sdonyayapi kin he etanhan wowapi cicagapi . Hunkakeyapi kin tuwe otokaheya tanhan kin he iye sdonyayapi kin heon wowapi cicagapi . Koškapi kin , wanišakapi , qa Wakantanka oie kin en niunpi , qa tuwe we šice cin he yaktepidan kin he etanhan wowapi cicagapi .
62002015	Wicoicage kin de waštedapi šni po , qa taku wicoicage kin ekta un kin hena nakun . Tuwe wicoicage kin de waštedake cinhan , Ateyapi kin waštedake cin en un šni .
62002016	Taku wicoicage en un kin owasin , wicaceĥpi cantiheye cin , wicaišta cantiheye cin , qa wiconi kin den waĥanicidapi kin , hena Ateyapi kin etanhan šni , tuka wicoicage kin de etanhan .
62002017	Unkan wicoicage kin de atakuni kte šni , qa wocantiheye kin nakun ; tuka tuwe Wakantanka tawacin kin yuhe cinhan , he owihanke wanin ounye kta .
62002018	Hokšiyopa cikcistinpidan , anpetu ihankeya kin wanna hiyohi ; unkan , Messiya kipajin kin he u kta ce , nayaĥonpi qon he iyecen Messiya kipajinpi kin ota wanna hipi ; heon de anpetu ehake kin sdonunyanpi .
62002019	Unkiyepi kin etanhan inanpapi , tuka hena unkicicapi šni . Hena unkicicapi unkanš , unkici pi un wacinpi kta : tuka owasin unketanhanpi šni tanin kta e heon etanhan hececa .
62002020	Tuka Wanji Wakan kin he niye sdaniyanpi , qa heon taku owasin sdonyayapi .
62002021	Wowicake kin sdonyayapi šni kin heon wowapi cicagapi šni ; tuka he sdonyayapi , qa woitonšni takudan wowicake kin eciyatanhan u šni , heon etanhan .
62002022	Tuwe itonši he ; tuwe Jesus he Messiya kin ee šni , keye cin hee ; Messiya kipajin kin hee , Ateyapi qa nakun Cinhintku kin anawicakiĥbe cin hee .
62002023	Tuwe Cinhhintkuyapi kin wicada šni kin he Ateyapi kin yuhe šni : tuka tuwe Cinhintkuyapi kin oyake cinhan , he Ateyapi kin nakun yuha ece .
62002024	Taku otokaheya tanhan nayaĥonpi qon he yuha po . Taku otokahe ekta nayaĥonpi qon en niunpi kinhan , Cinhintkuyapi kin en yaunpi kta , qa nakun Ateyapi kin en .
62002025	Unkan wahoyapi qon taku iwahounyanpi kin , owihanke wanin wiconi kin hee .
62002026	Tona nihnayanpi kta cinpi kin hena on decen wowapi cicagapi .
62002027	Tuka sdaniyanpi , iye eciyatanhan duhapi kin he nicipi un ; qa tuwe waonspeniciyapi kta iyenicecapi šni ; tuka sdaniyanpi kin he taku owasin onspeniciyapi , he wowicake qa woitonšni wanica ; he taku onspeniciyapi kin iyecen , iye kin en unn po .
62002028	Unkan dehan , hokšiyopa cikcistinpidan , iye kici un po ; hecen tohan iye ihdutanin kinhan wacinunyanpi kta , qa taninyan hinajin kinhan , itokam unkištecapi kte šni .
62002029	Iye owotanna un sdonyayapi kinhan , tuwe woowotanna econ kin he iye kin eciyatanhan wanna teca nien tonpi e nakun sdonya po .
62003001	Wanyaka po , Ateyapi kin wocantekiye hinsko tanka unqupi kin , Wakantanka cinca unkekiciyapi kta : heon etanhan wicoicage kin sdonunyanpi šni , iye kin sdonyapi šni qon iyececa .
62003002	Waštecicidapi kin , wanna Wakantanka cinca kin heuncpi ; qa tounkecapi kte cin hinaĥin tanin šni : tuka iye kin ihdutanin kinhan , iyeuncecapi kta e sdonunkiyapi ; he token un kin wanunyakapi kta nakaeš .
62003003	Unkan tuwe hecen wacinyan canteyuze cinhan ihduecedan ece , iye kin ecedan un kin iyecen .
62003004	Tuwe woaĥtani econ kin he woope kin kicaksa ece ; woaĥtani he woope kicaksapi kin hee .
62003005	Unkan iye ihdutanin qon , waunĥtanipi kin yutokan iyeye kta e heon , he sdonyayapi ; qa iye kin woaĥtani takudan en un šni .
62003006	Tuwe iye en un kin he waĥtani šni ; tuwe waĥtani ece kin he iye kin tohinni wanyake šni , qa nakun sdonye šni .
62003007	Hokšiyopa cikcistinpidan , ihnuhan tuwe nihnayanpi kinhan ; tuwe taku owotanna econ ece kin he owotanna , iye kin owotanna un kin iyececa .
62003008	Tuwe woaĥtani econ ece kin he wakanšica eciyatanhan un ; otokaheya tanhan wakanšica kin waĥtani ece . Heon etanhan Wakantanka Cinhintku kin ihdutanin , wakanšica oĥan kin ihangye kte cin heon .
62003009	Tuwe Wakantanka eciyatanhan teca nien tonpi kin he woaĥtani econ šni , taku on icaĥye cin he en un kin heon ; unkan waĥtani okihi šni , Wakantanka eciyatanhan teca nien tonpi kin he etanhan .
62003010	Detanhan Wakantanka cinca kin sdonwicayapi , qa nakun wakanšica cinca kin ; tuwe taku owotanna ece econ šni kin he Wakantanka eciyatanhan šni , qa nakun tuwe hunkawanjitku tanyan cante kiyuze šni kin .
62003011	Otokaheya tanhan taku iwahokonunkiciyapi nayaĥonpi qon he dee , otoiyohi wašteunkicidakapi kte cin .
62003012	Qain taku šice cin eciyatanhan un , qa iye sunkaku kikte qon iyecece šni . Unkan taku on kikte he . Iye kin oĥan šica , qa sunkaku kin wašte kin heon etanhan .
62003013	Mihunkawanji , wicoicage kin šicenidapi ešta inihanpi šni po .
62003014	Hunkawanjinkiciyapi waštewicunkidapi kin heon wiconte etanhan wiconi e ekta unkiyohipi sdonunkiyapi ; tuwe hunkawanjitku waštekida šni kin he wiconte ehna un .
62003015	Tuwe hunkawanjitku šicekidake cin he tinwicakte kin heca ; unkan tuwe tinwicakte kin he wiconi owihanke wanica aihduhe šni e sdonyayapi .
62003016	Deciyatanhan wacantkiyapi kin sdonunyanpi ; iye kin unkiyepi on wiconi eĥpekiye cin heon ; hecen unkiš eya hunkawanjinkiciyapi kin on wiconi eĥpeunkiyapi kta iyececa .
62003017	Tuka tuwe maka akan woyuha ton , qa hunkawanjitku waĥpanica wanhdake ca , cantekiye cin anakipte cinhan , tooken Wakantanka waštedake cin en un kta he .
62003018	Micinca cikcistinpidan , wicoie qa wicaceji ecedan on wacanunkiyapi kte šni , tuka wicoĥan qa wowicake kin on .
62003019	Unkan deciyatanhan wowicake eciyatanhan unyakonpi , qa iye itohnake kin en cante unhdutinzapi kta e sdonunkiyapi .
62003020	Uncantepi kin unhdacopi kinhan , Wakantanka uncantepi kin sam iyeya tanka , qa taku owasin sdonya un .
62003021	Waštecicidapi kin , uncantepi kin unhdacopi šni kinhan , Wakantanka ekta wowaditake kin unhapi :
62003022	Qa taku unkidapi kin owasin unkicupi ece , tawoahope kin unkiciyuhapi , qa taku iye išta kin en iyokipi kin he econkupi , heon etanhan .
62003023	Unkan tawoahope kin he dee , Iye Cinhintku Jesus Messiya caje kin wacinunyanpi , qa otoiyohi wašteunkicidapi kta , econ unšipi qon iyececa .
62003024	Tuwe tawoahope kin ope cinhan , he Wakantanka kici un , qa iš iye kin en un ; unkan Woniya unqupi kin he eciyatanhan iye unkicipi un kin he sdonunyanpi ece .
62004001	Waštecicidapi kin , ihnuhan woniya owasin wicayadapi kinhan ; tuka woniya kin wicayukcan po , Wakantanka etanhan unpi kinhan ; wicašta wokcan itonpišni ota wanna wicoicage kin ehna iyayapi .
62004002	Deciyatanhan Wakantanka Taniya kin sdonyayapi kta ; woniya kin tona Jesus Messiya wicaceĥpi un hi oyake cin hena Wakantanka eciyatanhanpi ece .
62004003	Qa woniya kin tona Jesus Messiya wicaceĥpi un hi oyake šni kin hena Wakantanka eciyatanhanpi šni ; tuka Messiya kipajin u kta nayaĥonpi qon he dee , wanna wicoicage kin en un .
62004004	Hokšiyopa cikcistinpidan , Wakantanka eciyatanhan yaunpi , qa hena ohiwicayayapi ; tuwe en niunpi kin he tuwe wicoicage en un kin isanpa tanka .
62004005	Hena e wicoicage kin etanhanpi ; heon wicoicage kin iyecen iapi , unkan wicoicage kin anawicagoptan ece .
62004006	Unkiye Wakantanka unketanhanpi ; tuwe Wakantanka sdonye cin he unkiye anaungoptanpi ece ; qa tuwe Wakantanka eciyatanhan šni kin he anaungoptanpi šni . Deciyatanhan wowicake woniya qa wohnaye woniya kin napin sdonunyanpi .
62004007	Waštecicidapi kin , otoiyohi canteunkiciciyapi kte ; wacantkiyapi kin he Wakantanka eciyatanhan un ; qa tuwe wacantkiye cin he Wakantanka eciyatanhan tonpi , qa Wakantanka sdonya .
62004008	Tuwe wacantkiye šni kin he Wakantanka sdonye šni ; Wakantanka he wacantkiyapi kin hee .
62004009	Wakantanka canteunkiyapi kin he deciyatanhan tanin , Wakantanka iye Cinhintku išnana icage cin he makata u ši , heciyatanhan unnipi kta e heon .
62004010	Wacantkiyapi kin he deciyatanhan , unkiye Wakantanka wašteundakapi kin hee šni , tuka iye canteunkiyapi , qa Cinhintku waunĥtanipi yutokan iyeye kta e on u ši qon hee .
62004011	Waštecicidapi kin , Wakantanka hecen canteunkiyapi kinhan , unkiš eya otoiyohi canteunkiciciyapi kta iyececa .
62004012	Tuwedan tohinni Wakantanka wanyake šni . Otoiyohi canteunkiciciyapi kinhan Wakantanka unkicipi un , qa iye canteunkiyapi kin unkiyepi en tanyan yuštanpi ece .
62004013	Heciyatanhan unkiye kici unyakonpi , qa iye unkicipi un kin sdonunyanpi ece , iye Taniya unqupi kin heon .
62004014	Unkan wanunyakapi , qa Ateyapi kin Cinhintku ukiya , wicoicage kin ekta , Wanikiya hee kta e he unyaontaninpi .
62004015	Tuwe Jesus he Wakantanka Cinhintku kin hee e oyake cin he kici Wakantanka un , qa iš eya Wakantanka en un ece .
62004016	Wakantanka canteunkiyapi kin he sdonunyanpi qa wicaundapi . Wakantanka wacantkiyapi kin hee ; qa tuwe wacantkiyapi en un kin he Wakantanka kic un , qa Wakantanka iš nakun iye en un ece .
62004017	Deciyatanhan wocantekiye unkiyepi en unkiciyuštanpi ece , hecen woyaco anpetu kin en wowaditake unhapi kta : iye un kin unkiš iyecen wicoicage kin den unyakonpi ece .
62004018	Wacantkiyapi kin en wokokipe wanica , tuka wacantkiyapi yuštanpi kin he wokokipe tankan eĥpeya ece ; wokokipe kin he wicocante šica yuha ece ; tuwe wakokipe cin he nahanĥin wacantkiyapi kin en yuštanpi šni .
62004019	Iye tokaheya canteunkiyapi kin heon unkiye Wakantanka wašteundakapi .
62004020	Tuwe , Wakantanka waštewadaka ce , eye ca hunkawanjitku šicekidake cinhan , he itonšni . Tuwe hunkawanjitku wanhdake cin he waštekidake šni kinhan , token ecin Wakantanka wanyake šni kin waštedaka okihi kta he .
62004021	Unkan iye etanhan woahope kin de unhapi ; tuwe Wakantanka waštedake cin he hunkawanjitku kin iš nakun waštekidake kta ce .
62005001	Tuwe Jesus he Messiya kin ee e wicada kin he Wakantanka eciyatanhan tonpi ; qa tuwe waicaĥye cin waštedake cinhan , he tuwe iye eciyatanhan teca ni en tonpi kin he nakun waštedaka ece .
62005002	Deciyatanhan Wakantanka cinca kin waštewicundakapi kin sdonunkiyapi , Wakantanka wašteundakapi qa tawoahope kin tanyan unkiciyuhapi kinhan .
62005003	Wakantanka waštedakapi kin he dee , tawoahope kin tanyan ounpapi kin he ; unkan tawoahope kin wošitkihda šni .
62005004	Tuwe Wakantanka eciyatanhan tonpi kin he wicoicage kin ohiya ece ; unkan woohiye wicoicage ohiye cin he dee , wacinunyanpi kin hee .
62005005	Wicoicage ohiya ece kin he tuwe he ; tuwe Jesus he Wakantanka Cinhintku kin ee e wicada kin hee .
62005006	Tuwe mini qa we eciyatanhan hi qon he Jesus Messiya ee ; mini ecedan on hi šni , tuka mini we ahna . Unkan wayaotanin kin he Woniya kin hee ; Woniya kin he wowicake , heon etanhan .
62005007	Maĥpiya kin ekta yamni wayaotaninpi ece , Ateyapi kin , Wicoie kin , qa Woniya Wakan kin ; unkan hena yamni wanjipidan .
62005008	Nakun maka akan taku yamni wayaotanin ece , Woniya kin , qa mini kin , qa we kin ; unkan hena yamni wanjidan en un .
62005009	Wicašta akantu taku yaotaninpi kin he unkicupi kinhan , Wakantanka taku yaotaninpi kin he iyotan tanka ; Wakantanka taku yaotanin kin he dee , iye Cinhintku hdaotanin qon hee .
62005010	Tuwe Wakantanka Cinhintku kin wicada kin he wayaotanin iye atayedan yuha un . Tuwe Wakantanka wicada šni kin he itonšni daka ece ; wayaotanin kin on Wakantanka iye Cinhintku hdaotanin qon he wicada šni kin heon .
62005011	Unkan wayaotanin qon he dee , Wakantanka wiconi owihanke wanica unqupi kin he ; unkan wiconi kin he iye Cinhintku kin en un .
62005012	Tuwe Cinhintkuyapi kin yuhe cin he wiconi yuha ; qa tuwe Wakantanka Cinhintku kin yuhe šni kin he wiconi yuhe šni .
62005013	Wakantanka Cinhintku caje kin wacinyayapi kin dena wowapi cicagapi kin ; wiconi owihanke wanica duhapi e sdonyakiyapi kta , qa Wakantanka Cinhintku caje kin wacinyayapi kta e heon .
62005014	Unkan iye ekta wowaditake unhapi kin he dee , Iye tawacin kin eciyatanhan taku unkidapi eca naunkiĥonpi ece :
62005015	Qa taku unkidapi ece naunkiĥonpi ece e sdonunkiyapi kinhan , taku tona unkidapi kin hena unhapi e nakun sdonunkiyapi ece .
62005016	Tuwe hunkawanjitku waĥtani wanhdake cinhan , woaĥtani kin he wiconte ekta šni kinhan , wocekiye ekiciye kta , unkan Wakantanka wiconi qu kta , tona waĥtanipi wiconte ekta iyahde šni hena on . Woaĥtani wanji wiconte ekta ; he on wocekiye eye kta epe šni .
62005017	Taku šica econpi kin owasin woaĥtani ; unkan woaĥtani wiconte iyohi šni kin heca yukan .
62005018	Tuwe Wakantanka eciyatanhan tonpi kin he waĥtani šni ece e sdonunyanpi ; tuka tuwe Wakantanka eciyatanhan icage cin he tanyeĥ ihduhe ca hecen taku šice cin he oyutan šni ece .
62005019	Wakantanka eciyatanhan unyakonpi kin he sdonunkiyapi ; qa wicoicage kin ocowasin woaĥtani en wanka .
62005020	Unkan Wakantanka Cinhintku kin he hi , qa wicoksape unqupi , on tuwe wicake cin iyeunkiyapi kta e sdonunyanpi ; unkan tuwe wicake cin he en unyakonpi , iye Cinhintku Jesus Messiya hee . Wowicake Wakantanka qa owihanke wanin wiconi kin hee .
62005021	Hokšiyopa cikcistinpidan , taku wakagapi kin itehan ihduha po . Amen .
63001001	Hunkayapi un kin , Kuria kaĥnigapi qon wowapi kicaga ; iye cinca kin , wowicake eciyatanhan waštewicawadake cin hena om , qa mišnana šni , tuka nakun tona wowicake sdonyapi kin hena owasin ;
63001002	Wowicake kin en unyakonpi , qa owihanke wanin unkicipi un kte cin heon etanhan .
63001003	Wowašte , wowaonšida , wookiye ko , Wakantanka Ateyapi kin eciyatanhan , qa nakun Jesus Messiya Itancan , Ateyapi kin he Cinhintku kin eciyatanhan , wowicake wacantkiyapi ko en , nicipi un nunwe .
63001004	Ateyapi kin woahope unqupi qon iyecen , nicinca wowicake eciyatanhan manipi iyewicawakiye cehan nina imduškin .
63001005	Unkan nakaha , Kuria , ceciya ce , woahope teca wan cicage cin iyecece šni , tuka wanji otokahe ekta unhapi qon , otoiyohi canteunkiciciyapi kte cin hee .
63001006	Qa wacantkiyapi kin he dee , tawoahope kin eciyatanhan maunnipi kte cin hee . Woahope kin he dee , Otokahe ekta taka nayaĥonpi qon he ohna mayanipi kte cin .
63001007	Wanna Wicahnaye sa ota wicoicage kin ehna iyayapi , hena Jesus Messiya wicaceĥpi un hi qon oyakapi šni . He wicahnaye sa qa Messiya kipajin kin heca .
63001008	Iwanihdaka po , hecen taku unkamnanpi kin toki eĥpeunyanpi kte šni , tuka wokajuju iyakicuya unkicupi kta .
63001009	Tuwe waĥtani qa Messiya tawoonspe kin en un šni kin he Wakantanka yuhe šni . Tuwe Messiya tawoonspe kin en un kin he Ateyapi kin yuhe ca nakun Cinhintku kin .
63001010	Tuwe en niipi qa woonspe kin de yuhe šni kinhan , tin u šipi šni po , qa wookiye eciyapi šni po .
63001011	Tuwe wookiye eciye cin he iye oĥan šice cin en opa .
63001012	Taku ota wowapi cicagapi kta mduha ešta , miniĥuha minisapa ko on ecamon kte šni : tuka en ciupi qa i eciyatanhan ociciyakapi kta e ecin cante mduza ; hecen wowiyuškin unkitawapi kin ojudan kta .
63001013	Nitanka kaĥnigapi qon cincawicaye cin hena nape niyuzapi . Amen .
64001001	Hunkayapi waun kin , Gayos waštedakapi kin , wowicake en waštewadake cin he , wowapi cicaga .
64001002	Waštecicida , taku owasin isanpa , tanyan iyoopte de kta qa zaniyan yaun kta e cewakiya ece , ninagi iyoopta ye cin iyececa .
64001003	Hunkawanjinkiciyapi kin den hipi , qa wowicake en niun kin he oyakapi qehan , wowicake eciyatanhan mayani kin heon nina imduškin .
64001004	Micinca wowicake kin eciyatanhan manipi nawaĥon kin heon wowiyuškin iyotan tanka mduha , takudan kape šni .
64001005	Waštecicida , taku hunkawanjinkiciyapi kin , qa nakun wicašta toktokeca ecawicayecon kin he tanyeĥ ecanon :
64001006	Hena e okodakiciye kin en wacanyakiye cin tanyan oyakapi : hena icimanipi en , Taku Wakan iyecen , owicayakiye cinhan tanyan ecanon kta .
64001007	Iye caje kin on iyayapi , qa Ikcewicašta kin etanhan takudan icupi šni , heon etanhan .
64001008	Heon tona hececapi kin hena iyowinwicunkiyapi kta iyececa ; hecen wowicake kin ounkiyapi kta .
64001009	Okodakiciye kin wowapi wicawecaga ; tuka hena ehna Diotrephes itancan icida kin he iyowinunkiyapi šni .
64001010	Heon etanhan wau kinhan , iye oĥan kin , oie šica on unkaiapi ece kin hena weksuye kta . Unkan he on imnan šni , tuka iye ĥinca hunkawanjinkiciyapi kin iyowinwicakiye šni , qa tona hecon wacinpi kin iyowicaki šni , qa okodakiciye kin etanhan tankan iyayewicaya ece .
64001011	Waštecicida , taku šice cin he en ope šni wo , tuka taku wašte kin . Tuwe taku wašte econ kin he Wakantanka eciyatanhan un , tuka tuwe taku šica econ kin he Wakantanka wanyake šni .
64001012	Demetrios owasin on tanyan oyakapi , qa wowicake kin nakun eciyatanhan ; unkan unkiš eya he unyaotaninpi , qa waunyaotaninpi kin he wowicake e sdonyayapi .
64001013	Taku ota ociciwa kta mduha tuka , tuka minisapa wiyaka ko on hena wowapi cicage kte šni :
64001014	Tuka ecadan wanciyake kta , qa i eciyatanhan unkokiciciye kta wacin .
64001015	Wookiye niye en niciun nunwe . Takukiciyapi kin hena nape niyuzapi . Takukiciyapi kin cajeyan nape wicayuza wo .
65001001	Judas , Jesus Messiya tawowidake kin , qa Jakob sunkaku kin , tona Wakantanka Ateyapi kin en wicayuecepidan , qa Jesus Messiya en wicakpatanpi , qa wicakicopi kin hena wowapi wicakicaga .
65001002	Wowaonšida , qa wookiye , wacantkiyapi ko niyepi en niciyuotapi nunwe .
65001003	Waštecicidapi kin , wiconi ptaya unhapi kin on aiciciya wowapi cicagapi eca , wowacinye ehanna wicašta wakan wicaqupi qon he nina yakitanpi kta e on wowapi cicagapi , qa wahokonciciyapi kta iyececa .
65001004	Wicašta wanjikši naĥmana en opapi , wanakajatanhan woyaco kin de on owicawapi ; hena Taku Wakan iyececapi šni , qa Wakantanka unkitawapi towaonšida kin he wicowicaštašni kagapi , qa Wakantanka ecedan Itancan kin he anaĥmanpi , qa nakun Jesus Messiya Itancan unyanpi kin .
65001005	Heon etanhan , taku , ehanna sdonyayapi ešta , he ake kiksuyeciciyapi kta wacin , Itancan kin oyate kin Egupta etanhan ehdaku , qa iyohakam tona wicadapi šni kin hena ihangwicaye cin .
65001006	Qa nakun maĥpiya ohnihde otokahe unpi kin kpatanpi šni , tuka iye tipi eĥpekiyapi qon , hena otpaza ihukuya , owihanke wanin mazaicicaĥa kin on , anpetu tanka woyaco kin he en awicayuha .
65001007	Sodam qa Gomorra iyececa , qa otonwe hena ihdukšan wanke cin , hena iš eya iyecen wiinaĥmanpi kin en icicupi , qa wicaceĥpi toktokeca akitapi ece qon hena e woonspe on ehdepi , qa peta owihanke wanica on wošitkihda en unpi .
65001008	He iyececa , wihamnanpi sa kin dena wicaceĥpi kin ašamyapi , qa wokiconze waĥtedapi šni , qa taku tanka yašicapi ece .
65001009	Hececa , tuka Mikael maĥpiya ohnihde itancan kin he wakanšica kin kici econ , qa Moses tancan kin on akinicapi qehan , wooštehda woiyaonpe wan en aya tawatenye šni , tuka , Itancan kin iyopeniyan nunwe , eciya .
65001010	Tuka dena e qe taku sdonyapi šni kin hena yašicapi ece : tuka iye icagapi kin eciyatanhan taku sdonyapi kin hena on ihdušicapi , woteca ia okitpanipi kin iyececa .
65001011	Woteĥi wicakiciun nunwe ; Qain tancanku kin ohna yapi , qa wokajuju on , Balaam tawohnaye kin nina ainyankapi , qa Kore wicakipajin qon en ihangiciyapi .
65001012	Hena woašape kin heca , wacantkiya wayatapi kin en opeya wotapi , qa wikopešniyan cemiciyapi : maĥpiya šapa mini wanica tate on ayapi ece kin ; can kin ptanyetu eca šeca aya , waskuyeca codan , inonpa šeca , qa hute eciyatanhan yujunpi kin hena hececapi .
65001013	Miniwanca taja ohitika , iye wowištece tawapi kin minitaga iyecen hiyuyapi ece ; wicanĥpi ononiyata unpi , on otpaza sape ĥinca owihanke wanin wicakicihnakapi .
65001014	Henok Adam etanhan wicašta išakowin qon he itokam hena owicayake ca heya ; Wanyaka po , Itancan kin wicašta wašte wicayuhe cin woyawa tanka om u ce ;
65001015	Owasin wicayaco kta , qa tona Taku Wakan ohdašni kin hena wicoĥan šikšica owasin ohodašniyan econpi qon hena sdonkiyewicaye kta , qa wicoie canksiksi owasin waĥtanipi sa Taku Wakan ohodapi šni oie kicatonpi ece qon hena nakun .
65001016	Hena e wihnupi sa , wawiyaonpapi sa , iye cantiheyapi kin eciyatanhan manipi ece ; qa i eciyatanhan waĥanĥanicidaya iapi , qa taku on etanhan wicašta itohnake kin waštedakapi ece .
65001017	Tuka waštecicidapi kin , niyepi , Jesus Messiya Itancan un yanpi yewicaši qon hena oiepi ehanna oyakapi qon hena kiksuya po ;
65001018	Anpetu ihankeya kin en wicašta wawiĥaĥapi kin yuke kta , iye cantiheyapi šice cin eciyatanhan manipi kin , he oniciyakapi qon .
65001019	Ihdutokanpi kin dena eepi , witantanpi , qa Woniya kin yuhapi šni .
65001020	Tuka waštecicidapi kin , niš niyepi wowacinye iyotan wakan nitawapi kin he ohna icaĥiciyapi , qa Woniya Wakan kin eciyatanhan wocekiye eya po ;
65001021	Wakantanka waštedakapi kin en ihduha po ; qa Jesus Messiya Itancan unyanpi towaonšida wiconi owihanke wanica iyahde kte cin he ape yukan po .
65001022	Unkan hunĥ wicayukcan yan onšiwicada po ;
65001023	Qa hunĥ iš wokokipe on niwicaya po , peta etanhan iwicacupi kin iyececa ; qa wokoyake wicaceĥpi on ašapapi kin hena ee kaeš šicedaka po .
65001024	Unkan tuwe woaĥtani econ šni niyuhapi kta okihi , qa wowiyuškin yuha iye towitan kin en iyaonpepica šni enihdepi kte cin ,
65001025	Wakantanka ecedan ksapa , Wanikiya unkitawapi kin hee , Jesus Messiya Itancan unyanpi kin eciyatanhan , wowitan , woyaonihan , wookihi qa wokiconze , dehantu qa wicoicage owasin hehanyan , tawa nunwe . Amen .
66001001	Jesus Messiya wayuotanin tawa , taku ecadan u kta e he tawowidake kin sdonyewicakiye kta Wakantanka qu qon he dee ; unkan taohnihde wan u ši , qa tawowidake Johannes he okiyaka :
66001002	He Wakantanka oie kin , qa Jesus Messiya wohdake cin , taku tona wanyake cin hena yaotanin .
66001003	Tuwe wokcan oie kin de yawa , qa tona naĥonpi , qa taku en kagapi kin anagoptanpi kin , hena wowašte yuhapi . Wanna kiyadan ihan .
66001004	Johannes , Asia ekta okodakiciye šakowinpi kin wowapi wicakicaga . Wowaonšida , wookiye ko , tuwe un , qa un qon , u kte cin hetanhan niyepi en nicipi un nunwe ; qa Woniya šakowinpi oiyotanke tawa kin itokam unpi kin hena eciyatanhan ;
66001005	Qa Jesus Messiya etanhan , he waayatanin wicaka , wiconte etanhan tokaheya tonpi , qa maka wicaštayatapi kin Itancan kin hee . Tuwe wašte unkidapi , qa waunĥtanipi kin etanhan iye we kin en unyujajapi ,
66001006	Qa Atkuku Wakantanka ekta wicaštayatapi , wošna kagapi ko unkagapi kin hee , wowitan , wowašake ko owihanke wanin tawa nunwe . Amen .
66001007	Wanyaka po , maĥpiya šapa kin akan u ; unkan wicišta owasin wanyakapi kta , qa tona he capapi qon hena nakun , qa iye on oyate maka ohnaka kin owasin aicipapi kta . Hecetu nunwe . Amen .
66001008	Alpha qa Omega , otokahe qa owihanke kin he miye ce ; Itancan un , qa un qon , u kta , iyotan wašake cin he hena hecen eya .
66001009	Johannes hunkawajinyayapi , wokakije , qa wokiconze , wowaĥbadan ko , Jesus Messiya tawa kin en , tawaši yayapi kin he miye ; Wakantanka oie qa Jesus Messiya wohdake cin on etanhan , wita wan , Patmos eciyapi , hen waun .
66001010	Itancan taanpetu kin en Woniya kin kici waun ; unkan mihektapa tanhan wicaho wan tanka , maza yahotonpi tanka wan iyececa , nawaĥon ;
66001011	He kaken eya , Alpha qa Omega , tokaheya qa ehake kin he miye ce . Taku wandake cin wowapi ecen kage ca , Asia ekta okodakiciye kin iwahowicaya wo ; Ephesos , qa Smurna , qa Pergamos , qa Thuatira , qa Sardis , qa Philadelphia , qa Laodikia .
66001012	Unkan wicaho omakiye cin he wanmdake kta e ekta mihdamna . Unkan mihdamna qehan mazaskazi petijanjan ihupa šakowin wanmdaka .
66001013	Qa petijanjan ihupa šakowin kin cokaya Wanji Wicašta Cinhintku kin iyececa , tawokoyake kin siha kin ekta iyahdeya , qa maku kin opta mazaskazi ihduskita .
66001014	Qa pa kin paha ko ska , taĥinca wanuyanpi hin kin iyecen ska , qa wa iyececa , qa išta kin peta ide kin iyececa ;
66001015	Qa siha kin iš mazazi ecedan iyececa , peta tanka en itkonyahe seca ; qa ho kin he mini ota iĥaĥa kin iyececa .
66001016	Qa nape etapa kin ohna wicanĥpi šakowin hduhe ca , i kin eciyatanhan maza sagye anog ope kin heca wan hiyu , qa itohnake kin he anpetu wi nina iyege cin iyececa .
66001017	He wanmdaka , unkan ta wanke cin iyecen siha hde kin en mahinĥpaya . Hehan iye nape etapa kin on omayutan qa , Ihnuhan koyakipe cin , emakiya ; Tokaheya qa ehake kin he miye ;
66001018	Tuwe te ca ake kini , qa ito owihanke wanin ni waun ; Amen ; qa Wakanšica ti kin wiconte ko tiyopa iyuĥdoke kin yuha manka ce .
66001019	Taku wandake cin he wowapi ecen kaga wo , taku nakaha un qa dena iyohakam taku u kte cin hena .
66001020	Wicanĥpi šakowin minape etapa kin ohna wandake ciqon wowiyukcan kin hee , qa mazaskazi petijanjan ihupa kin hena nakun . Wicanĥpi šakowin qon okodakiciye šakowinpi ohnihde yuhapi kin hena eepi ; qa petijanjan ihupa šakowin wandake cin okodakiciye šakowinpi kin hena eepi .
66002001	Ephesos ekta okodakiciye ohnihde yuhapi kin he ecen wowapi kicaga wo ; Tuwe wicanĥpi šakowin nape etapa kin ohna hduhe ca , mazaskazi petijanjan ihupa šakowin cokaya omani kin he hecen eya ;
66002002	Nioĥan , qa nitoĥtani , qa wacinnitanka kin he sdonwaya ; qa tona šicapi kin hena iyowinwicakiya ooyakihi šni ; qa tona yewicašipi kin hecadpi keiciyapi kin hena wicadukcan qa itonpišni kin heca iyewicayaya .
66002003	Wacinnitanka , qa ayape , qa micaje kin on ĥtayani , qa oyakite šni .
66002004	Tuka taku cistinna iyacionpa , tokaheya wašteyadake cin he aduštan .
66002005	Heon tokiya tanhan nihinĥpaye cin he kiksuye , ca ihduecetu , qa nioĥan tokaheya kin hduštan wo . Hecanon šni kinhan kohanna ekta ciu , qa petijanjan nitawa kin yutokan iyeciciye kta , nihduecetu šni kinhan .
66002006	Tuka he duha , Nikoleton wicoĥan kin šiceyadake cin , hena miš eya šicewadaka .
66002007	Tuwe noge yukan hecinhan , taku Woniya kin okodakiciye kin ewicakiye cin he naĥon kta . Tuwe ohiye cinhan he can wiconi , Wakantanka tamaga cokaya he cin , hetanhan yun wakiye kta .
66002008	Unkan Smurna ekta okodakiciye ohnihde yuhapi kin he ecen wowapi kicaga wo ; Tuwe tokaheya qa ehake un kin , te ca ake kini kin hee hecen eya ;
66002009	Nioĥan kin sdonwaya , wokakije wowaĥpanica ko nitawa kin , ( tuka winijica ; ) qa tona Juda wicašta keiciyapi qa hecapi šni , tuka Satan omniciye tawa kin etanhanpi , hena waaiapi kin nakun sdonwaya .
66002010	Token nicakije kte cin ihnuhan taku koyakipe cin . Iho , Wakanšica niyepi wanjikji wicakaška tipi kin en iyeniyanpi kta , iniyukcanpi kta e heon ; unkan anpetu wikcemna hehanyan wokakije duhapi kta ; tuka wicate cin hehanyan wicaka wo , kinhan wiconi watešdake wan cicu kta .
66002011	Tuwe noge yukan hecinhan , taku Woniya kin okodakiciye kin ewicakiye cin he naĥon kta . Tuwe ohiye cinhan he wiconte icinonpa kin on kiuniyanpi kte šni .
66002012	Unkan Pergamos ekta okodakiciye ohnihde yuhapi kin he ecen wowapi kicaga wo ; Tuwe maza sagye anog ope kin hduhe cin hee hecen eye ;
66002013	Nioĥan kin sdonwaya , qa tukten Satan oiyotanke tawa yanke cin hen yati ; qa micaje kin yuha yaun , qa wacinmaanpi kin aduštan šni , anpetu kin Antipas waayatanin wicaka mitawa kin niyepi kin en , tukten Satan ti kin , hen ktepi qon he ehan .
66002014	Tuka taku wanjikjidan iyacionpa ; Balaam hee Balak Israel cinca kin taku on waĥtani iciyapi kte cin wicitokam ehde kin he onspekiye ca , taku wakagapi wakiyušnapi kin yutapi , qa wiinaĥmanpi econpi kta , he tawoonspe tona yuhapi kin hena wicaduha ;
66002015	Qa nakun Nikoleton tawoonspe yuhapi kin hena wicaduha , he šicewadaka tuka .
66002016	Ihduecetu wo ; hecanon šni kinhan kohanna ekta ciu , qa mii maza sagye kin on hena kici wecize kta .
66002017	Tuwe noge yukan hecinhan , taku Woniya kin okodakiciye kin ewicakiye cin he naĥon kta . Tuwe ohiye cinhan he manna kihnakapi qon he etanhan yunwakiye ca inyan ska wan waqu kta , inyan kin he en wicacaje teca wan kagapi kin he tuwedan sdonye šni , tuka tuwe icu kte cin hecedan .
66002018	Unkan Thuatira ekta okodakiciye ohnihde yuhapi kin he ecen wowapi kicaga wo ; Wakantanka Cinhintku , išta peta ide kin iyecen hduhe ca , siha kin mazazi ecedan iyececa hee hecen eya ;
66002019	Nioĥan kin sdonwaya , wacanyakiye , ca ĥtayani , qa wicayada , qa ayape , qa nioĥan kin , qa ehake kin hena tokaheya kin sam iyeya ota .
66002020	Tuka taku tonana iyacionpa , winoĥinca wan Jezebel eciyapi , winoĥinca wokcanka keiciye cin he mitaokiye kin wicahnaye ca , wiinaĥmanpi econpi , qa taku wakagapi wakiyušnapi kin yutapi kta e onspe wicakiye cin hee iyowinyakiya .
66002021	Unkan he wawiciĥaĥapi econ kin on iyopeiciye kta e anpetu waqu , tuka iyopeiciye šni .
66002022	Ito , owinja wan akan ewaonpe kta , qa tona kici wawiciĥaĥapi econpi kin hena nakun , wokakije tanka en ; wicoĥan kin on iyopeiciyapi šni kinhan .
66002023	Qa iye cinca kin wiconte on wicawakte kta ; qa okodakiciye kin owasin , tuwe wicapakšin wicacante ko iyukcan kin he miye e sdonyapi kta . Qa niyepi kin otoiyohi nioĥanpi kin eciyatanhan cicupi kta .
66002024	Tuka niyepi , qa tona Thuatira ekta woonspe kin he yuhapi šni , qa Satan ošbe tawa eyapi kin sdonye šni yaunpi kin kaken eciciyapi ; Waqinpi tokeca acihnakapi kte šni ;
66002025	Tuka taku duhapi kin he tinsa hduha po , hibu kte cin hehanyan .
66002026	Qa tuwe ohiye ca owihanke kin iyahdeya mioĥan kin yuha un kinhan , oyate kin en wowašake waqu kta .
66002027	Qa maza icapsinte wan on wicayuhe ca maka wakšica iyecen wicakamdece kta ce ; hecen Ate etanhan hduha waun .
66002028	Qa anpao wicanĥpi kin he waqu kta .
66002029	Tuwe noge yukan hecinhan taku Woniya kin okodakiciye kin ewicakiye cin he naĥon kta .
66003001	Unkan Sardis ekta okodakiciye ohnihde yuuhapi kin he ecen wowapi kicaga wo ; Tuwe Wakantanka Taniya šakowin kin hena , qa wicanĥpi šakowin hduhe cin he hecen yea ; Nioĥan kin sdonwaya , caje wan duha , yani kin hee , tuka nita .
66003002	Kiktahan un , qa taku tona nahaĥin en un qa te kte cin hena hduwašaka wo ; Wakantanka itokam nioĥan kin owotanna e iyewaye šni .
66003003	Heon token iyacu , qa nayaĥon kin kiksuye ca , tinsa yuze ca , ihduecetu wo . Kiktahan yaun šni kinhan wamanon sa iyecen ekta ciu kta , qa tohan ekta cihi kte cin he sdonyakiye kte šni .
66003004	Tuka Sardis ekta wicacaje tonana duha , hena e tawokoyake kin hdušapapi šni ; qa ska ihduzapi ecen mici manipi kta ; he iyehantupi nakaeš .
66003005	Tuwe ohiye cinhan he wokoyake ska koyake kta , qa iye caje kin wiconi wowapi kin etanhan wapajuju kte šni , tuka he caje kin Ate itokam , qa ohnihde wicaye cin hena wicitokam omdake kta .
66003006	Tuwe noge yukan hecinhan taku Woniya kin okodakiciye kin ewicakiye cin he naĥon kta .
66003007	Unkan Philadelphia ekta okodakiciye ohnihde yuhapi kin he ecen wowapi kicaga wo ; Tuwe wakan qa wicaka un , qa Dawid tiyopa iyuĥdoke kin yuhe ca , yuĥdoka eca tuwedan ecen iyeye šni , qa ecen icu eca tuwedan yuĥdoke šni ece kin hee hecen eya ;
66003008	Nioĥan kin sdonwaya , tiyopa wan yuĥdokapi ecen he cin he nitokam ewahde , qa tuwedan ecen iyeya okihi šni ; wowašake cistinna duhe ca mioie kin yuha yaun , qa micaje kin eĥpemayaye šni .
66003009	Ito , Satan omniciye tawa kin etanhanpi Juda wicašta keiciyapi , tuka hecapi šni , qa itonpi šni kin , hena iho , upi , qa nisiha kin itokam canpeška makehde inajin wicawakiye kta , qa waštecicida e sdonyapi kta .
66003010	Woape oie mitawa kin he awandake cin , heon tohan taku wawiyutanyan un kin tona maka owancaya unpi kin iyutanwicaye kta u kinhan , hehan awanciyake kta .
66003011	Iho ecadan wau kta ; taku duhe cin he tinsa yuza wo , hecen watešdake nitawa kin tuwedan nici kte šni .
66003012	Tuwe ohiye cinhan , he tipi wakan mita Wakantanka tawa kin ohna can ihupa wan wakage kta , qa icimana tankan ye kte šni ; qa he akan mita Wakantanka caje kin owawa kta , qa mita Wakantanka otonwe tawa caje kin , Jerusalem teca kin hee , maĥpiya kin etanhan Wakantanka mitawa kin eciyatanhan u kin hee , qa nakun micaje teca kin .
66003013	Tuwe noge yukan hecinhan , taku Woniya kin okodakiciye kin ewicakiye cin he naĥon kta .
66003014	Unkan Laodikia ekta okodakiciye ohnihde yuhapi kin he ecen wowapi kicaga wo ; Tuwe Amen eciyapi , waayatanin owotanna , qa wicaka , Wakantanka woicage tawa otokahe kin hee hecen eya ;
66003015	Nioĥan kin sdonwaya , sni qa ipiga unmana ecen yaun šni , sni qa ipiga unma tukte e ecen yaun kta wacin ;
66003016	Tuka initeca , qa sni ipiga kici unmana ecen yaun šni , heon mii kin etanhan icihdepe kta .
66003017	Wimajica , qa woyuha ota waton , qa takudan imakakije šni , keha ce ; qa inicakije ca , onnišike ca , niwaĥpanica , qa išta nigonge ca , tanconikadan e sdonyakiye šni .
66003018	Kaken wahokonciciya ce , mazaskazi peta on yuecedan kagapi kin he opemicaton wo , winijica kta ce , qa wokoyake ska , kodake kta e heon , hecen tanconikadan on winištece cin he tanin kte šni ; qa wicišta wihdi kin , niišta iyakiun kta , hecen wawandake kta .
66003019	Tona cantewicawakiye cin hena wahokonwicawakiye ca , iyopewicawakiya ece . Heon mniheiciye ca ihduecetu wo .
66003020	Ito , tiyopa kin en nawajin qa wakabubu ece ; tuwe miho kin naĥon , qa tiyopa hduĥdoke cinhan , he ekta tin hibu , qa kici wawate kta , qa iš eya mici wote kta .
66003021	Tuwe ohiye cinhan he oiyotanke mitawa kin akan mici iyotanke wakiye kta , miye ohiwaye ca Ate oiyotanke tawa kin akan weci imdotanke cin he iyecen .
66003022	Tuwe noge yukan hecinhan , taku Woniya kin okodakiciye kin ewicakiye cin he naĥon kta .
66004001	Hena iyohakam wanmdake ca ito maĥpiya kin ekta tiyopa wan yuĥdokapi ; qa wicaho tokaheya nawaĥon kin he maza yahotonpi tanka kin iyececa , he omakiye ca heya , Deciya u wo , dena iyohakam taku u kte cin hena wanyagciciye kta ce .
66004002	Unkan kohanna Woniya kin en waun ; qa ito , maĥpiya kin ekta oiyotanke wan ecen hdepi , qa tuwe akan iyotankehan yanka .
66004003	Tuwe akan iyotanke cin he iwanyakapi kin inyan teĥika , iyaspis qa saĥdinos iyececa ; qa oiyotanke kin ihdukšan wihmunke wan hmihbeya yanka , smaĥagdos inyan kin iyececa .
66004004	Qa oiyotanke kin ihdukšan oyanke wikcemna nonpa sam topa wanka ; qa oyanke kin hena en hunkawicayapi wikcemna nonpa sam topa iyotankapi , qa wokoyake ska koyakapi e wanmdaka ; qa pa kin en mazaskazi tešdakapi .
66004005	Unkan oiyotanke kin etanhan wakanhdi qa wakinyan hotonpi qa wicaho hiyu ; qa oiyotanke kin itokam petijanjan šakowin peta ece ideyapi , hena Wakantanka taniya šakowin kin heepi .
66004006	Unkan oiyotanke kin itokam mde wan wanka janjan seca , caĥtowata iyecen kohdi ; qa oiyotanke kin cokaya , qa oiyotanke kin ihdukšan , taku ni un topa kin yukanpi , hena e tokapatanhan qa hektapatanhan ko išta ojupidan .
66004007	Unkan taku ni un tokaheya kin he mnaja ouncage kin iyececa ; qa taku ni un iyokihe kin he tatanka ouncage kin iyececa ; qa taku ni un iciyamni kin he wicašta itohnake kin iyecen yuha ; qa taku ni un icitopa kin he wanmdi kinyan un ouncage kin iyececa .
66004008	Qa taku ni un topa kin otoiyohi ĥupahu šakpekpe yuhapi , qa ihdukšan , qa mahen tanhan išta ojupidan ; qa anpetu hanyetu ko ayaštan šni hecen eyapi , Wakan , Wakan , Wakan , Itancan Wakantanka Iyotan wašaka , tuwe un , qa un qon , u kte cin hee ce .
66004009	Qa tohan taku ni un topa kin , tuwe oiyotanke kin akan kiyotanke ca owihanke wanin ni un kin he wowitan , qa wootanin , qa wopida qupi kinhan ;
66004010	Hehan hunkawicayapi wikcemna nonpa sam topa kin hena , tuwe oiyotanke kin akan kiyotanke cin he itokam makata eĥpeiciyapi , qa tuwe ohinniyan ni un kin ohodapi , qa watešdake tawapi kin oiyotanke kin itokam eĥpekiyapi , qa hecen eyapi ;
66004011	Itancan , wowitan , qa wootanin , qa wowašake iyacu kta e iyenihantu , taku owasin yakage ca nitoiyokipi kin on owasin kagapi qa ecen han .
66005001	Unkan tuwe oiyotanke kin akan kiyotanke cin he etapa kin eciyatanhan wowapi wan mahen tanhan qa akapatanhan owapi , qa ipuspe šakowin on apuspapi kin he wanmdaka .
66005002	Qa maĥpiya ohnihde wašaka wan wanmdaka , he hotankakiya hotanin qa , Wowapi kin he tuwe yumdaye ca ipuspe šakowin kin yuĥdoke kta okihi he , eya .
66005003	Unkan maĥpiya kin ekta , qa maka kin akan , qa maka kin ihukuya tanhan tuwedan wowapi kin he yumdaye ca , en wanyaka okihi šni .
66005004	Hehan nina waceya , tuwe wowapi kin yumdaye ca yawa , qa en wanyake kta iyekicihantu kin tuwedan iyeyapi šni kin heon etanhan .
66005005	Unkan hunkawicayapi kin wanji hemakiya ; Ceye šni wo , ito Juda wicoun kin etanhan , mnaja kin , Dawid hutkan kin hee wowapi kin yumdaye ca , ipuspe šakowin kin yuĥdoke kta okihi .
66005006	Hehan wanmdake ca , iho , oiyotanke kin cokaya , qa taku ni un topa , hunkawicayapi ko wicacokaya Amnos wan najin , wošnapi iyececa , he šakowin išta šakowin ko yukan , Wakantanka taniya šakowin maka kin owancaya ye wicayapi kin hena eepi .
66005007	He en hi , qa tuwe oiyotanke kin akan kiyotanke cin nape etapa kin etanhan wowapi qon icu .
66005008	Unkan wowapi kin he icu qehan , taku ni un topa kin , qa hunkawicayapi wikcemna nonpa sam topa kin hena Amnos kin itokam makata eĥpeiciyapi , otoiyohi candowankiyapi hduhapi , qa nakun mazaskazi wiyatke taku waštemna on ojudan , wicašta wašte wocekiye tawapi kin hee :
66005009	Qa odowan teca wan ahiyayapi , qa heyapi ; Wowapi kin iyacu , qa ipuspe kin duĥdoke kta e iyenihantu ce , waniyušnapi qa Wakantanka ekta niwe kin on opeunyakitonpi , wicoun otoiyohi etanhan , qa iapi kin , qa wicowazi kin , qa oyate kin otoiyohi etanhan ;
66005010	Qa Wakantanka ekta wicaštayatapi wawayušnapi ko unyakagapi ; unkan maka kin oununyanpi kta ce .
66005011	Unkan wanmdake ca , oiyotanke kin ihdukšan , qa taku ni unpi kin hunkawicayapi ko wicihdukšan , maĥpiya ohnihde woyawa tanka ota , qa kektopawinge ece kektopawinge , hena hopi kin nawaĥon ;
66005012	Hotankakiya heyapi , Amnos wošnapi qon he wowašake , qa woyuha , qa woksape , qa wicookihi , qa wootanin , qa wowitan , qa wowašte henakiya icu kta okihi ce .
66005013	Unkan taku maĥpiya ekta un , qa taku maka akan un , qa taku maka ihukuya tanhan un , qa taku miniwanca mahen un , hena taku ohnaka ko owasin kaken eyapi nawaĥon ; Tuwe oiyotanke kin akan kiyotanke cin Amnos kin kici wowašte kin , wootanin kin , wowitan kin , qa wowašake kin hanakiya owihanke wanin tawapi nunwe .
66005014	Unkan taku ni un topa kin hena , Hecetu nunwe , eyapi ; qa hunkawicayapi wikcemna nonpa sam topa kin hena makata eĥpeiciyapi , qa tuwe ohinniyan ni un mkin he ohodapi .
66006001	Unkan Amnos kin ipuspe tokaheya yuĥdoke cehan wanmdaka ; unkan taku ni un topa kin wanji , wakinyan hotonpi kin iyecen hotanin qa , U qa wanyaka wo , eya nawaĥon .
66006002	Unkan wanmdake ca , ito , šuktanka ska wan tuwe akan iyotanke cin he itazipa wan yuha ; qa watešdake wan qupi ; unkan ohiye ca , ohiye kta e iyaya .
66006003	Unkan ipuspe inonpa yuĥdoke cehan , taku ni un icinonpa kin he , U qa wanyaka wo , eya nawaĥon .
66006004	Unkan šuktanka wan tokeca hin ša kin he hinanpa ; unkan tuwe akan iyotanke cin he maka kin etanhan wookiye icu kta e qupi , hecen otoiyohi kiciktepi kta ; qa nakun maza sagye wan tanka qupi .
66006005	Unkan ipuspe iyamni kin yuĥdoke cehan , taku ni un wiciyamni kin he , U qa wanyaka wo , eya nawaĥon . Unkan wanmdake ca ito šuktanka sapa wan ; qa tuwe akan iyotanke cin he nape ohna taku on tke utapi wanji yuha .
66006006	Unkan taku ni un topa kin cokaya tanhan wicaho wan nawaĥon , Aguyapi iyutapi wanji he kašpapidan wanjidan , qa šuktanka tawote iyutapi nonpa he kašpapidan wanjidan kta ; qa wihdi miniša ko ihnuhan kiuniyaye cin , eya .
66006007	Unkan ipuspe itopa kin yuĥdoke cehan , taku ni un icitopa kin he ho kin nawaĥon ; U qa wanyaka wo , eya .
66006008	Unkan wanmdake ca ito šuktanka wan hin san ; tuwe akan iyotanke cin he Wiconte eciyapi , qa Wicaĥapi kin he ihakam iyaya . Unkan maka hanke itopa kin hehanyan maza sagye , qa wicaakiĥan , qa wiconte , qa wamanica maka akan un kin hena on wicašta wicakte kta e wowašake qupi .
66006009	Unkan ipuspe izaptan kin yuĥdoke cehan , wahna wošnapi kin ihukuya tona Wakantanka oie , qa iye waayataninpi kin he on wicaktepi qon hena nagipi kin wanwicamdaka .
66006010	Hena hotankakiya hotaninpi qa heyapi , Itancan wakan , qa wicaka , tohanyan tona maka kin akan yukanpi kin wicadaco šni qa we unkitawapi kin on toyecon šni he .
66006011	Unkan hena otoiyohi wokoyake ska wicaqupi , qa ptecedan ape yukanpi kta , tona om taokiye unpi qon , qa iye hunkawanjitkupi kin , iš iyepi iyecen wicaktepi kte cin he yuštanpi kta hehanyan , kewicakiyapi .
66006012	Unkan ipuspe išakpe kin yuĥdoke cehan , wanmdake ca ito maka škanškan tanka , qa anpetu wi kin sapa aya , wahinske ojuha kin iyececa , qa hanyetu wi kin iš we iyecen icaga .
66006013	Qa maĥpiya wicanĥpi kin makata hinĥpayapi , witanšna hu wan tateyanpa tanka kahuhuza eca waskuyeca štunkadan keš paĥpa ece kin he iyececa .
66006014	Qa wowapi pehan ehnakapi kin he iyecen maĥpiya kin tanin šni iyaye ca , ĥe otoiyohi , wita otoiyohi ko yutokan iyeyapi .
66006015	Qa maka wicaštayatapi , qa wicašta tankinkinyanpi , qa wicašta watonpika , qa wicašta itancanpi , qa wicašta wašakšakapi , qa wicašta wowidake unpi kin otoiyohi , qa ihduhapi kin otoiyohi , qa ihduhapi kin otoiyohi , makoĥdoka qa ĥe imnija kin ehna naiciĥmanpi ;
66006016	Qa inyan ĥe imnija ko hena heciyapi , Unkahinĥpayapi , qa tuwe oiyotanke kin akan kiyotanke cin itohnake kin etanhan , qa Amnos kin wocanniye tawa kin etanhan anaunĥman po :
66006017	He wošihda tawa anpetu tanka kin wanna hi ; unkan tuwe najin okihi kta he .
66007001	Unkan hena iyohakam maĥpiya ohnihde topa maka oise topa kin en inajinpi kin wanwicamdaka , maka tate ouye topa kin yuhapi , hecen maka qa miniwanca qa can hiyeye cin wanjidan atateyanpa kte šni .
66007002	Hehan maĥpiya ohnihde tokeca wan wiyohiyanpa tanhan wankantkiya u kin wanmdaka , he Wakantanka ni un ipuspe tawa kin yuhe ca maĥpiya ohnihde topa maka miniwanca ko kiuniyanpi kta e wicaqupi qon hena hotankakiya hoyewicakiye ;
66007003	Qa heya , Maka , qa miniwanca , qa can hiyeye cin kiuniyanpi šni po , Wakantanka unkitawapi taokiye wicaye cin itepi kin en wapetog wicuntonpi šni kin hehanyan .
66007004	Unkan tona wapetog wicatonpi wicayawapi kin nawaĥon , Israel cincapi wicoun owasin etanhan kektopawinge opawinge sam kektopawinge wikcemna topa sanpa kektopawinge topa wapetog wicatonpi .
66007005	Juda wicoun kin etanhan kektopawinge ake nom wapetog wicatonpi ; qa Ruben wicoun kin etanhan kektopawinge ake nom wapetog wicatonpi ; qa Gad wicoun kin etanhan kektopawinge ake nom wapetog wicatonpi ;
66007006	Aser wicoun kin etanhan kektopawinge ake nom wapetog wicatonpi ; qa Nepthalim wicoun kin etanhan kektopawinge akenonpa wapetog wicatonpi ; qa Manasse wicoun kin etanhan kektopawinge ake nom wapetog wicatonpi ;
66007007	Sumeon wicoun kin etanhan kektopawinge ake nom wapetog wicatonpi ; qa Lewi wicoun kin etanhan kektopawinge ake nom wapetog wicatonpi ; qa Isakar wicoun kin etanhan kektopawinge ake nom wapetog wicatonpi ;
66007008	Zabulon wicoun kin etanhan kektopawinge ake nom wapetog wicatonpi ; qa Joseph wicoun kin etanhan kektopawinge ake nom wapetog wicatonpi ; qa Benjamin wicoun kin etanhan kektopawinge ake nom wapetog wicatonpi .
